# 10 — Kiến trúc & luồng hoạt động (as-built)

> Tài liệu **bám sát code thực tế** (khác với `00`–`09` là design-intent). Mọi mô tả ở đây đối chiếu
> với mã nguồn hiện hành, link tới `file:line` thật. Nếu code đổi, cập nhật lại file này.
>
> **Lưu ý lệch so với design docs:** một số điểm trong `00`/`04` đã không còn khớp hiện thực — xem mục
> [Khác biệt so với design docs](#khác-biệt-so-với-design-docs) ở cuối.

## 1. Bản chất

VPN client **thuần userspace**: tự cài đặt toàn bộ ngăn xếp (IKE, ESP, L2TP, PPP, SSTP, TCP/IP) ở tầng
ứng dụng, **không cần TUN/TAP adapter của OS, không ghi bảng route hệ thống**. Ứng dụng nhận một IP ảo
trong đường hầm rồi mở TCP/UDP socket chạy *bên trong* đường hầm.

Hai triết lý:
- **Plugin theo driver** — mỗi giao thức là một `IVpnProtocolDriver`, đăng ký theo tên (`"sstp"`, `"l2tp-ipsec"`, `"ikev2"`).
- **Đảo ngược phụ thuộc** — mọi tầng chỉ phụ thuộc project `Abstractions`, không phụ thuộc ngang.

## 2. Phân lớp (40 project trong `src/`)

```
APP       TqkLibrary.VpnClient            VpnClient / VpnClientBuilder   (entry point)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Sockets   VpnTcpClient / VpnUdpClient / VpnNetworkStream
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
DRIVER    TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.L2tpIpsec   (IKEv1 + ESP + L2TP + PPP — lắp ráp toàn bộ stack; ESP-in-UDP/4500 NAT-T mặc định, hoặc native ESP proto-50 qua Transport.RawIp khi HonestFirst + no-NAT — P0.8c)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Sstp        (TLS + PPP + crypto binding — refs Abstractions+Ppp)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Ikev2       (IKEv2 + ESP tunnel mode — không PPP; V.1)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.CiscoIpsec  (IKEv1 Aggressive Mode group PSK + XAUTH + Mode-Config + ESP tunnel mode — không PPP; V.12; validate live vs strongSwan)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenVpn     (OpenVPN tun/tap: UDP/TCP + TLS-in-control + AEAD — không PPP; tap-mode bridge L2 (1-host/pure-DHCP/multi-host) + IPv6 trong tunnel opt-in enableIpv6 (NDISC L2.4 + SLAAC/DHCPv6 L2.6 qua DualStack* L2.9, best-effort) — V2.h, V.2-ipv6)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.WireGuard   (WireGuard: UDP + Noise_IKpsk2 (initiator + responder role opt-in acceptInbound cho peer-to-peer) + data type-4 + config tĩnh — không PPP; V3.f)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.SoftEther   (SoftEther SSL-VPN: TLS + Ethernet-over-TLS + DHCP/ARP/VirtualHost bridge 1-host hoac multi-host broadcast domain opt-in (uplink-as-port) — driver L2 that; V4.c; multi-connection 1-32 socket/1 session qua SoftEtherMultiConnectionMux — V.4; IPv6 trong tunnel opt-in enableIpv6: NDISC v6 (L2.4) + SLAAC/DHCPv6 (L2.6) qua DualStack* (L2.9) best-effort tren bridge SecureNAT — V.4-ipv6)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect (OpenConnect/ocserv: TLS byte-stream + HTTPS config-auth + HTTP CONNECT + CSTP data plane + DPD/keepalive + rekey X-CSTP-Rekey-* (re-establish make-before-break) — không PPP; data plane qua DTLS 1.2 khi server đẩy X-DTLS-* (Transport.Dtls/F.3), fallback CSTP-over-TLS; V5.b/V5.c/V5.d. DTLS-PSK (PSK-NEGOTIATE) hiện đại = đường ưu tiên: khi DTLS bật + không override factory, control channel chạy qua OpenConnectBouncyCastleTransportFactory (BouncyCastleTlsByteStream) để export RFC 5705 PSK; BuildDtlsPsk derive PSK 32B (label EXPORTER-openconnect-psk) → OpenConnectDtls12PskClient; codec gửi X-DTLS-CipherSuite: PSK-NEGOTIATE + parse X-DTLS-App-ID/X-DTLS-MTU + HasDtlsPsk; legacy resumption = fallback. VALIDATE LIVE ✅ vs ocserv 1.2.4)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Core        (scaffolding dùng chung: ReconnectingVpnConnection<TState> supervisor + VpnReconnectOptions — gom EstablishAsync/ReconnectLoopAsync/backoff-jitter/StateChanged/link-loss; consumer WireGuard + OpenConnect + OpenVPN + SoftEther + SSTP + IKEv2 + L2TP/IPsec — F.6 xong cho mọi driver)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Pptp        (PPTP RFC 2637: control TCP/1723 + GRE proto-47 qua IRawIpTransportFactory + MPPE + PPP/MS-CHAPv2 — Echo keepalive, auto-reconnect F.6; legacy/insecure; OFFLINE code+test, live chờ Q.1; V6.b)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.IpEncap     (IP-in-IP/GRE thuần: mở raw-IP F.9 theo proto-number (GRE-47/IPIP-4/SIT-41) qua IRawIpTransportFactory → GreTunnelChannel/RawIpPassthroughChannel sau facade L3 ổn định; connectionless — KHÔNG control plane/handshake/auth/keepalive, địa chỉ out-of-band; TRẦN không mã hóa, elevate; auto-reconnect F.6 kế thừa nhưng chỉ kích khi caller báo link-loss; OFFLINE code+test + VALIDATE LIVE GRE/IPIP/SIT 2 chiều (lab/ipencap, 0 bug); EtherIP/L2TPv3 chờ V.8c; V.8b)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Nebula      (Nebula mesh: UDP + handshake Noise IX initiator + verify cert responder (CA Ed25519) + data type-1 Message AES-256-GCM (header=AAD, nonce 0^4‖counter BE) + config tĩnh (overlay từ cert) — không PPP; tunnel lifecycle re-handshake make-before-break + supervisor F.6; endpoint tĩnh static_host_map (lighthouse discovery động chưa làm); OFFLINE code+test (9) + VALIDATE LIVE FULL-TUNNEL ICMP 2 chiều (lab/nebula nebula v1.9.5 thật, 0 bug data-plane); V.7.1 phase b)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Tinc        (tinc 1.1 SPTPS: TCP meta-connection (ID→SPTPS handshake reuse phase a→ACK→ADD_SUBNET→ADD_EDGE qua TincMetaConnection) + data-plane SPTPS RIÊNG (REQ_KEY/ANS_KEY over meta, label "tinc UDP key expansion") + bare-IP router-mode over UDP datagram (TincDataTransport relay header DSTID(nullid)‖SRCID(node_id=SHA512(name)[:6])‖SptpsDatagramRecordLayer) sau facade L3 ổn định; TincChannel PKT_PROBE type-2 reply (confirm UDP 2 chiều) + TCP data fallback SPTPS_PACKET(21); config tĩnh TincConfig (Ed25519 seed ta + peer host file)→TunnelConfig; supervisor F.6; point-to-point 1 peer (auto-mesh đa-node = STRETCH chưa làm). OFFLINE code+test (10) + VALIDATE LIVE (lab/tinc tincd 1.1pre18 thật router mode): meta activated + data SPTPS keyed + UDP probe 2 chiều RTT~2ms + client ICMP request mã hóa tới server tun + wire byte-verified; full ICMP echo-reply 2 chiều RESIDUAL server-side (kernel container net-unreachable trên reply tự-sinh, không phải client — xem "Khác biệt"). 5 bug interop sửa qua live. V.7.2 phase b)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.N2n         (n2n v3 ntop L2 mesh: UDP transport tới supernode → REGISTER_SUPER → REGISTER_SUPER_ACK (cookie-correlated, lifetime → keepalive) → data plane L2 PACKET (N2nEthernetChannel IEthernetChannel: egress đóng Ethernet frame thành PACKET dst-MAC-từ-header + transform NULL/AES, ingress decode → InboundFrame) cắm vào Ethernet fabric ArpResolver static-IP + VirtualHost → facade L3 ổn định; keepalive re-REGISTER_SUPER (token auth + dev_addr static giữ nguyên); config tĩnh N2nConfig (community + static -a overlay + MAC + transform)→TunnelConfig (KHÔNG DHCP); supervisor F.6; supernode-relay point-to-point (P2P hole-punching = STRETCH chưa làm). OFFLINE code+test (9: register + L2 round-trip 2 chiều NULL/AES qua ARP+VirtualHost + timeout + channel/config) + VALIDATE LIVE L2 FULL-TUNNEL (lab/n2n n2n v3.1.1 thật: supernode + edge gateway tun 10.7.0.1/24 + client .NET 10.7.0.2/24): REGISTER_SUPER+ACK+keepalive ACK (0 NAK sau fix) + ARP resolve gateway qua fabric + ICMP echo 2 chiều qua L2 overlay (tcpdump edge0: request+reply). 2 bug interop sửa qua live (keepalive token-reuse + dev_addr static). V.7.4 phase b)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.ZeroTier    (ZeroTier VL1/VL2 L2 mesh: UDP transport tới node/controller → VL1 HELLO(cipher0) ⇄ OK(HELLO)(cipher1, timestamp echo verified) → trả OK(HELLO) cho HELLO của peer (xác lập path 2 chiều) → VL2 join NETWORK_CONFIG_REQUEST (retry) → controller config dict (assigned IP `v4s`/`I` + COM `C`/`com`) → data plane L2 ZeroTierEthernetChannel (IEthernetChannel: egress đóng Ethernet frame thành EXT_FRAME + COM lần đầu + seal Salsa20/12+Poly1305 VL1, ingress decode EXT_FRAME/FRAME → InboundFrame) cắm vào fabric ZeroTierNeighborResolver (derive peer MAC, KHÔNG ARP) + VirtualHost → facade L3; ECHO keepalive; config tĩnh ZeroTierConfig (identity ta secret + peer/controller public + network id + optional static overlay) → TunnelConfig; supervisor F.6; planet/moon root discovery = out of scope (peer trực tiếp). OFFLINE code+test (6: HELLO/OK + network join + EXT_FRAME L2 round-trip 2 chiều + pinned-addr + timeout + caps/guard) + VALIDATE LIVE vs zerotier-one 1.4.6 thật: VL1 OK peering (timestamp echo) + network join (assigned 10.144.0.2/24 + COM) → Connected. 4 bug interop sửa qua live (Salsa20 block-boundary + OK(HELLO) reply + v4s/NUL dict + DeriveMac byte-exact MAC::fromAddress KAT vs 2 member thật). Data plane: derive MAC đúng ⇒ EXT_FRAME tới đúng tap MAC node (node nhận) + push COM qua NETWORK_CREDENTIALS. Data-plane VL2 ICMP live = còn lại: controller ERROR NEED_MEMBERSHIP_CERTIFICATE — COM trích từ dict C controller 1.4.6 chưa được chấp nhận (serialize COM 1.4.6 khác docs dev); 2 member zerotier-one thật ping nhau OK (lab+MAC đúng, residual ở COM exchange phía client). V.7.3 phase b)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Vtun        (vtun legacy daemon: MỘT kết nối TCP control+data → VtunControlChannel.AuthenticateAsync challenge-response (khối ASCII 50-byte NUL-pad: greeting→HOST:→OK CHAL:→CHAL:→OK FLAGS:/ERR; response = Blowfish-ECB(MD5(password)) trên challenge a..p) → kiểm cờ server (type tun/proto tcp/encrypt no/compress no) → data plane VtunPacketChannel (IPacketChannel L3 bare IP) frame length-prefix (word 2-byte BE flags|length) sau facade; receive loop data→channel + ECHO_REQ→ECHO_REP + CONN_CLOSE/EOF→link-loss; keepalive timer ECHO_REQ idle; config tĩnh VtunConfig (host name + password + IP tunnel tĩnh/peer)→TunnelConfig (OutOfBand, vtund up/down script đặt server tun); supervisor F.6; point-to-point 1 host. OFFLINE code+test (5: handshake + data-frame round-trip 2 chiều + reject wrong-pass + reject unsupported-flags + caps) + VALIDATE LIVE FULL-TUNNEL ICMP 2 chiều vs vtund 3.0.4 thật (lab/vtun: server log "Use SSL-aware challenge/response"+"Session test opened"+tun0 bound; 4/4 ICMP echo reply 10.11.0.2↔10.11.0.1 RTT~0.4ms; reject path live). 0 bug — golden vector OpenSSL Blowfish khoá offline. Encryption/compression/tap/UDP = CHƯA làm. V.11)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Ssh         (VPN-over-SSH: MỘT kết nối TCP/22 chạy SSH-2 → SshConnection.EstablishAsync resolve host → mở TCP qua seam ISshTransportFactory (tái dùng TcpByteStream F.1) → SshClient.ConnectAsync (version exchange → KEXINIT negotiate → curve25519-sha256 KEX → ed25519 hostkey verify + TOFU pin → NEWKEYS cipher chacha20-poly1305@openssh.com/aes256-gcm@openssh.com → userauth publickey-ed25519/password → channel tun@openssh.com point-to-point L3) → bind SshPacketChannel (IPacketChannel L3 bare IP, gói IP trần qua tun framing AF-only) sau facade + wire InboundIpPacket→Deliver / send→SendIpPacketAsync → RunReceiveLoopAsync (link-loss khi channel close/EOF); DisconnectAsync gửi CHANNEL_CLOSE best-effort; config tĩnh SshConfig (user + ed25519 seed/password + IP tunnel tĩnh/peer + RemoteTunUnit)→TunnelConfig (OutOfBand — SSH không thương lượng địa chỉ in-tunnel, admin đặt server tun qua PermitTunnel); supervisor F.6; point-to-point 1 server. OFFLINE code+test (6: full handshake + IP round-trip cả chacha20-poly1305@openssh.com lẫn aes256-gcm@openssh.com qua SimulatedSshServer + password auth + reject wrong-password + caps + state) + VALIDATE LIVE FULL-TUNNEL ICMP 2 chiều vs OpenSSH 9.6p1 (lab/ssh: PermitTunnel point-to-point + ed25519 authorized_key; publickey ed25519 ACCEPTED + tun@openssh.com open (phải đăng nhập root — OpenSSH gắn tun vào uid phiên) + ICMP 2 chiều 10.10.0.1↔10.10.0.2). 1 bug interop sửa qua live (tun framing AF-only, KHÔNG packet_length dẫn đầu). KEX/cipher/auth bổ sung (rsa/ecdsa hostkey, dh-group, aes-ctr EtM, keyboard-interactive) + rekey mid-session + tap mode = CHƯA làm. V.10)
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
PROTOCOL  TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec     Ike/V1 , Ike/V2 , Esp , Nat (NAT-T UDP 500↔4500, ghép kênh IKE/ESP)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp      L2TPv2 control + data
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp       LCP (+ đáp LCP Echo-Request→Echo-Reply, RFC 1661 §5.8) / IPCP / IPV6CP / MS-CHAPv2 / HDLC + Ipv6/ (global IPv6 over PPP: RS/RA/SLAAC/DHCPv6 qua PppEthernetChannelAdapter tái dùng engine Ethernet NDISC/SLAAC — P1.1; refs Ethernet)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack   IPv4+IPv6 / TCP / UDP / ICMP userspace (dual-stack)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet  L2 Ethernet: codec frame/MAC + EthernetSwitch hoc MAC (host-port + uplink-port ConnectUplink) + VirtualHost bridge + ARP IPv4 + NDISC IPv6 + DHCPv4 + SLAAC/DHCPv6 client + EthernetAdapter rap multi-host + MultiHostSession (N station = N IVpnSession) + composite dual-stack (DualStackNeighborResolver/Configurator) (L2.0-L2.9)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn   OpenVPN: codec + reliability + TLS-in-control + tls-auth/crypt + data channel (AEAD GCM/ChaCha + non-AEAD AES-CBC+HMAC qua IOpenVpnDataChannel) + P_DATA_V1/V2 + push/keepalive + NCP + TCP/UDP/tap (V.2, VALIDATE LIVE RỘNG: VPN Gate + server tự host lab/openvpn — tun UDP+NCP AES-256-GCM, tun TCP framing, gói lớn 64KB, tap L2/ARP)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard WireGuard: handshake Noise_IKpsk2 + codec type-1/2/3 + TAI64N + mac1/mac2 + cookie-reply + data channel type-4 (counter u64 + anti-replay 64-gói + keepalive) + timers/state machine rekey/keepalive + WireGuardConfig/WireGuardPeer/WireGuardChannel + crypto-routing đa-peer longest-prefix (IpPrefix/WireGuardCryptoRouter/WireGuardMultiPeerChannel) (V3.f + V.3)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther SoftEther SSL-VPN: PACK codec (binary typed key-value — list element {name≤63, type int/data/str/unistr/int64, mảng value} big-endian) + helper Set/Get theo tên (V4.a) + control handshake: watermark POST + hello/login codec + auth SHA-0 (secure_password) qua IByteStreamTransport (V4.b) + data plane Ethernet-over-TLS: block frame codec (uint32(n)+{uint32(size)·bytes}) + SoftEtherEthernetChannel (IEthernetChannel) + keep-alive (V4.c) + multi-connection (welcome max_connection/half_connection + additional_connect codec + SoftEtherMultiConnectionMux gộp 1-32 socket = 1 session: round-robin egress + N decode loop, SoftEtherConnectionDirectionPlanner full/half-duplex — V.4) + payload codec (use_compress: SoftEtherPayloadCompressor DEFLATE per-frame magic 0xDEADBEEFCAFEFACE; use_encrypt: SoftEtherEncryptedTransport RC4 per-direction tái dùng Crypto.Rc4 — V.4)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect OpenConnect/AnyConnect (ocserv): CSTP framing 8-byte (STF|len|type — DATA/DPD/KEEPALIVE/DISCONNECT/COMPRESSED/TERMINATE, seam F.2) + HTTP auth config-auth XML (init/form/reply/success + cookie) + HTTP CONNECT /CSCOSSLC/tunnel parse X-CSTP-* + X-DTLS-* → TunnelConfig (V5.a) + CstpChannel (IPacketChannel CSTP-over-TLS) + CstpDatagramChannel/CstpDatagramFraming (IPacketChannel CSTP-over-DTLS, header 1-byte type, 1 datagram=1 gói — V5.c) + OpenConnectHttpTransactor (auth POST/CONNECT byte-exact qua IByteStreamTransport) + CstpDpdState (clock-inject DPD/keepalive) (V5.b) + CstpRekeyState/OpenConnectRekeyMethod (clock-inject rekey X-CSTP-Rekey-Method/-Time, ParsedRekeyMethod None/Ssl/NewTunnel — V5.d)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp     PPTP (RFC 2637): control TCP/1723 codec (SCCRQ/SCCRP, OCRQ/OCRP, Echo, Set-Link-Info, Call-Clear/CDN, Stop-CC — magic 0x1A2B3C4D, big-endian) + reassembler + PptpControlConnection state machine (PNS/client) + CCP/MPPE negotiator (CcpNegotiator trên PppNegotiator, option MPPE RFC 2118/3078) + MppeSessionFactory (ráp MppeSession F.5b từ MS-CHAPv2) + GRE data plane (PptpGreCodec/PptpGreChannel Enhanced GRE §4.1 trên IDatagramTransport proto-47 + MppePppFrameChannel decorator MPPE). OFFLINE code+test (V6.a + V6.b); Drivers.Pptp runtime chạy trên F.9 raw-IP. VALIDATE LIVE 2026-06-24 (lab/pptp accel-ppp): client ĐÚNG tới tầng MPPE (control/GRE-47/LCP/MS-CHAPv2/CCP-MPPE OK, MPPE encrypt byte-perfect khớp kernel ppp_mppe.c + reference pppd); IPCP blocked server-side (accel-ppp không mở IPCP, reference pppd fail y hệt) — xem bảng "Khác biệt"
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap  IP-in-IP/GRE thuần (TRẦN, không mã hóa) trên IDatagramTransport raw-IP (F.9): GRE chuẩn v0 (RFC 2784/2890 — GreCodec/GreTunnelChannel proto-47, KHÁC Enhanced GRE PPTP) + RawIpPassthroughChannel header-less cho IPIP (proto-4, RFC 2003) & SIT/6in4 (proto-41, RFC 4213) — mỗi loại 1 IPacketChannel (L3). OFFLINE codec+kênh (V.8a); driver runtime ở Drivers.IpEncap (V.8b); GRE/IPIP/SIT VALIDATE LIVE 2 chiều (lab/ipencap, pcap khớp Linux ip-tunnel byte-for-byte, 0 bug); EtherIP/L2TPv3 chờ V.8c
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Nebula   Nebula (Slack mesh, V.7.1 phase a): handshake Noise IX (NebulaNoiseIxHandshake Noise_IX_25519_AESGCM_SHA256 — tái dùng NoiseSymmetricState, KHÔNG refactor) + Nebula cert codec protobuf v1 (NebulaCertificateCodec MarshalDetails proto3-đúng khớp byte CA ký + NebulaCertificateValidator verify Ed25519 + NebulaPem) + packet header codec 16B BE (NebulaHeaderCodec) + handshake payload codec (NebulaHandshakePayloadCodec). OFFLINE code+test (22). VALIDATE LIVE handshake 2026-06-24 (lab/nebula, nebula v1.9.5 thật): nebula chấp nhận stage-1 + gửi stage-2, ta giải mã + verify cert responder + cert THẬT offline khớp byte (re-marshal==signed 100==100, sig valid against CA) — first-run, 0 bug interop. Driver runtime (UDP/data-plane/re-handshake) = Drivers.Nebula (phase b XONG, full-tunnel live)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc     tinc 1.1 SPTPS (mesh full-mesh, V.7.2 phase a — VALIDATE LIVE vs tincd 1.1pre18): handshake SPTPS (SptpsHandshake KEX→SIG→derive — ECDH có khóa Ed25519 SptpsEcdh + Ed25519Signer; transcript fill_msg(flag‖kex0‖kex1‖label), KDF seed "key expansion"‖init_nonce‖resp_nonce‖label) + TLS-1.0 P_hash XOR HMAC-SHA-512 (SptpsPrf prf_xor: 2 HMAC/khối inner+outer, XOR-fold) + ECDH có khóa Ed25519 (SptpsEcdh: KEX public = Ed25519 Edwards, shared = X25519 ladder trên Edwards→Montgomery-x, scalar clamp(SHA512(seed)) — KHÔNG X25519 thuần) + record cipher biến thể tinc (TincChaChaPoly1305: nonce seqno 8B BE djb, poly key=keystream block0, tag-on-ciphertext — KHÁC RFC 8439, BC ChaChaEngine+Poly1305) + record layer TCP stream (SptpsRecordLayer, seqno đếm CẢ handshake record → record mã hóa đầu = seqno 2) + UDP datagram (SptpsDatagramRecordLayer + AntiReplayWindow) + KEX codec 65B (SptpsKex) + meta request codec (TincMetaRequest ID/ADD_EDGE/…) + base64 little-endian phi chuẩn tinc (TincBase64, KHÁC RFC 4648) + host-config parser (TincHostConfig Ed25519PublicKey base64-tinc). 35 test offline (+5 KAT interop golden từ live). VALIDATE LIVE: tincd báo "server SIG VERIFIED" + client giải mã đúng record meta đầu server (ACK) — lab/tinc build tinc 1.1pre18 từ source + harness publish linux-x64. 4 bug interop self-pair-offline-không-bắt sửa qua live (TincBase64 LE, SptpsEcdh Ed25519-keyed, SptpsPrf TLS-1.0 XOR, seqno-đếm-cả-handshake). Driver runtime (meta lifecycle/data-plane SPTPS/UDP data/route/IPacketChannel/F.6/UseTinc) = Drivers.Tinc (phase b XONG, full-tunnel live data-plane proven 2 chiều; full ICMP echo-reply residual server-side). Mở rộng phase a cho phase b: SptpsHandshake.BuildUdpLabel + SptpsDatagramRecordLayer EncodeHandshake/DecodeHandshake (plaintext seqno‖type‖data, đếm seqno chung với data records) + EnableEncryption/ctor unkeyed
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier ZeroTier V1 (overlay L2 Ethernet-over-UDP, V.7.3 phase a + codec phase b): identity C25519 (ZeroTierAddress 40-bit + ZeroTierIdentity 64B pubkey=Curve25519‖Ed25519 + ZeroTierIdentityCodec idtool-string/binary + ZeroTierAddressDerivation memory-hard hash: Salsa20/20 KEY=digest[0:32] IV=digest[32:40] trên 1 stream LIÊN TỤC, genmem 2MB CBC-like, shuffle 131072 vòng đọc index big-endian re-encrypt digest mỗi vòng, hashcash digest[0]<17, addr=digest[59:64]) + VL1 transport (Vl1Header 27B clear + verb byte 28; Vl1PacketCodec seal/open: _salsa20MangleKey (shared key XOR header: IV+dest+src 18B, flags hops-mask 0xf8, size LE 2B) → Salsa20/12 + Poly1305, cipher 0 C25519_POLY1305_NONE no-encrypt (HELLO) / cipher 1 Salsa2012Poly1305, poly key=keystream block0, **payload cipher bắt đầu ở block KẾ — DiscardToNextBlock bỏ 32B đuôi block0** (Salsa20 ZeroTier block-granular), tag 8B trunc; Vl1KeyDerivation C25519→SHA-512 shared key tái dùng Curve25519DhGroup; HelloMessageCodec verb HELLO + Identity::serialize + nil InetAddress; **OkMessageCodec** OK common header + OK(HELLO) (timestamp echo + versions + physical InetAddress); **InetAddressCodec** (0x00 nil/0x04 v4/0x06 v6 + port 2 BE)) + VL2 (NetworkId 64-bit; **Vl2FrameCodec FRAME body = networkId(8)‖etherType(2)‖data KHÔNG flags** + DeriveMac; **Vl2ExtFrameCodec EXT_FRAME** networkId‖flags‖[COM]‖dstMac‖srcMac‖etherType‖data; **ZeroTierDictionary** key=value text escape + **NetworkConfigCodec** NETWORK_CONFIG_REQUEST + decode config dict: assigned IP key `I`(binary)/`v4s`(legacy text) + routes `RT` + COM `C`/`com` + mtu).           TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tailscale  Tailscale control plane ts2021 (V.7.5 — VALIDATE LIVE FULL vs Headscale v0.29.1): kênh điều khiển Noise IK (Ts2021NoiseHandshake `Noise_IK_25519_ChaChaPoly_BLAKE2s`, tái dùng NoiseSymmetricState — pre-message `<- s`, msg1 `e,es,s,ss`, msg2 `e,ee,se`, prologue `Tailscale Control Protocol v<N>`) + frame codec ts2021 (Ts2021FrameCodec: initiation `[ver u16][type=1][len u16]` 5B header / khác `[type][len u16]` 3B, big-endian; Ts2021FrameType 1/2/3/4) + record transport (Ts2021Transport: ChaCha20-Poly1305 IETF, nonce `0^4‖counter(BE)` từ 0, AAD rỗng, max plaintext 4077B) + Ts2021NoiseStream (Stream duplex record-frame + skip EarlyNoise 9B `\xff\xff\xffTS`) + Ts2021Connector (`POST /ts2021` Upgrade+X-Tailscale-Handshake base64 → 101 → Noise IK) + TailscaleControlClient (net5+: `/key` → noise → `/machine/register` preauth Auth.AuthKey → `/machine/map` Stream long-poll, HTTP/2 h2c qua SocketsHttpHandler.ConnectCallback+Http2UnencryptedSupport, đọc khung `[len LE u32][JSON]`) + DTO tailcfg JSON PascalCase (RegisterRequest/RegisterResponse/MapRequest/MapResponse/TailscaleNode DERP-rename/Hostinfo/OverTlsPublicKeyResponse) + key codec (TailscaleKey mkey:/nodekey:/discokey: + lowercase hex 32B) + netmap→WireGuardConfig (NetmapToWireGuardConfig: self Addresses→tun IP, peer Key→WG pubkey, AllowedIPs→allowed-ips, Endpoints→endpoint).           TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ssh      VPN-over-SSH protocol layer (SSH-2 transport, V.10 — VALIDATE LIVE full-tunnel vs OpenSSH 9.6p1): clean-room từ RFC 4251/4253/4252/4254 + OpenSSH PROTOCOL (KHÔNG dùng thư viện SSH ngoài).           TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Vtun     vtun (legacy tunnel daemon, V.11 — VALIDATE LIVE full-tunnel vs vtund 3.0.4): codec wire thuần (clean-room từ vtun-3.0.4 auth.c/vtun.h/tcp_proto.c, KHÔNG copy GPL). Auth: VtunMessageCodec (khối 50-byte VTUN_MESG_SIZE NUL-pad — mỗi dòng handshake ASCII+\n pad 0) + VtunChallengeCodec (encode/decode challenge a..p cl2cs/cs2cl: alphabet abcdefghijklmnop, byte→2 char, bọc <…> 32 char + EncryptChallenge = Blowfish-ECB(key=MD5(password)) trên 16-byte challenge, encrypt_chal — LUÔN dùng kể cả encrypt no). Ref Abstractions + Crypto (Blowfish BouncyCastle BlowfishEngine ECB + MD5 BCL). 32 test offline (message 50-byte round-trip + challenge a..p + GOLDEN VECTOR OpenSSL challenge 7416f64c… + 3 GOLDEN VECTOR encryptor OpenSSL legacy-provider BF-ECB byte-exact + round-trip lengths + factory/key-derivation + flags <Tu>/<TuE1>/<TuC6K> + frame data/control/oversized). Driver runtime = Drivers.Vtun. Compression (zlib/lzo) + cipher khác BF128ECB (CBC/CFB/OFB + AES — cần sideband ivec/seq# framing) + tap = CHƯA làm

TRANSPORT TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls  DTLS 1.2 client (IDatagramTransport) qua BouncyCastle DtlsClientProtocol — SslStream không làm DTLS; bọc UDP pipe, mã hóa/giải mã từng datagram, cert-callback tùy chọn (F.3). 3 chế độ handshake (DtlsDatagramTransport ctor): (1) DTLS PSK full handshake = OpenConnectDtls12PskClient (PskTlsClient): cipher PSK-NEGOTIATE OpenConnect hiện đại, DtlsPskParameters(PSK identity "psk", PSK key 32B từ RFC 5705 EKM, session_id=X-DTLS-App-ID), suite TLS_PSK_WITH_AES_256/128_GCM, ép ClientHello.session_id qua TlsUtilities.ImportSession (session throwaway dummy-master/DTLSv12/no-EMS) — VALIDATE LIVE ✅ vs ocserv 1.2.4 (handshake completed, data qua UDP/443); (2) legacy AnyConnect resumption = DefaultDtlsClient + DtlsResumptionParameters + DtlsCipherSuiteMap (fallback, ocserv dtls-legacy); (3) full handshake thường (offline loopback).           TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.RawIp RawIpDatagramTransport (IDatagramTransport) trên raw socket (SocketType.Raw) chở IP protocol tùy ý (ESP-50/GRE-47) không bọc UDP/TCP — đường DUY NHẤT userspace cho proto tùy ý, BẮT BUỘC elevate; NativeRawSocket mở socket qua libc socket() (P/Invoke) trên Unix vì .NET managed Socket từ chối protocol number lạ (EPROTONOSUPPORT kể cả root) — đã validate live P0.8c; IRawIpTransportFactory (interface ở Abstractions) probe quyền thật + ném RawIpNotPermittedException; RawIpv4 strip IPv4 header + drop fragment; best-effort trên Windows (OS/firewall có thể nuốt proto-50) (F.9 — consumer P0.8c native ESP, V6.b PPTP-GRE, V.8b IP-in-IP/GRE/SIT)

          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Tls   2 bản TLS-over-TCP: (a) TlsByteStream (ITlsByteStream) bọc TcpByteStream + SslStream — dùng chung SSTP/SoftEther/OpenConnect-TLS-only: capture RemoteCertificate (SSTP crypto binding), cert-callback (P0.6), 2 ctor resolve-host/IPEndPoint-sẵn (F.1); (b) BouncyCastleTlsByteStream (ITlsByteStream + ITlsKeyingMaterialExporter) bọc TcpByteStream + BouncyCastle TlsClientProtocol — TLS 1.2, exporter RFC 5705 (ExportKeyingMaterial): tính TLS 1.2 PRF tay (PRF(master_secret, label, client_random+server_random)) như gnutls — bỏ qua EMS-guard của BouncyCastle (ocserv không bật extended_master_secret) — pre-register export qua RequestKeyingMaterialExport + tính trong NotifyHandshakeComplete rồi cache (master secret bị xóa ngay sau handshake). Chỉ OpenConnect-DTLS-PSK dùng (b) (qua OpenConnectBouncyCastleTransportFactory); SSTP/SoftEther giữ (a) — không regression. VALIDATE LIVE ✅ (CSTP-over-TLS + DTLS-PSK vs ocserv 1.2.4)
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
```

> Project `TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Udp` (tầng TRANSPORT cũ) đã **gom vào `Ipsec` dưới `Nat/`** — xem bảng
> [Khác biệt so với design docs](#khác-biệt-so-với-design-docs).

## 3. Hợp đồng cốt lõi (Abstractions)

Chuỗi 3 interface phân cấp là xương sống của toàn bộ thư viện:

| Interface | Vai trò |
|---|---|
| [IVpnProtocolDriver.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Interfaces/IVpnProtocolDriver.cs#L9) | Điểm vào plugin: `Name`, `Capabilities`, `ConnectAsync(endpoint, credentials, ct)` |
| [IVpnConnection.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Interfaces/IVpnConnection.cs#L7) | Một kết nối sống (1 IKE-SA / 1 TLS), sở hữu nhiều `IVpnSession`; `OpenSessionAsync()` |
| [IVpnSession.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Interfaces/IVpnSession.cs#L10) | Một endpoint IP logic: `Config` (IP/DNS/route/MTU) + `PacketChannel` |
| [IPacketChannel.cs:6](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/Interfaces/IPacketChannel.cs#L6) | Kênh L3: `WriteIpPacketAsync()` + event `InboundIpPacket` — "card mạng ảo" mà IP stack bám vào |
| [ILinkChannel.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/Interfaces/ILinkChannel.cs#L9) | Base chung: `Mtu`, `MaxHeaderLength`, `Medium` (Ip/Ethernet), `RequiresLinkAddressResolution` |
| [IEthernetChannel.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/Interfaces/IEthernetChannel.cs#L7) | Kênh **L2** (kế thừa `ILinkChannel`): `LinkAddress` (MAC 6 byte), `WriteFrameAsync()` + event `InboundFrame` — **đã có impl** [`EthernetSwitch.Port`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetSwitch.Port.cs#L14) + [`OpenVpnTapChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnTapChannel.cs#L15) trên nền L2.0–L2.3 (switch học MAC + `VirtualHost` bridge L2↔L3 + ARP IPv4 — xem §5 *Ethernet*/§9); **2 driver L2 tiêu thụ thật bridge 1-host xuống L3**: OpenVPN tap-mode (`OpenVpnTapChannel` → `VirtualHost`+`ArpResolver`, IP từ ifconfig) và **SoftEther** (`SoftEtherEthernetChannel` → `VirtualHost`+`ArpResolver`, IP từ **DHCP** SecureNAT — driver L2 thật đầu tiên có lease, V4.c); **`EthernetAdapter` (L2.7) + `MultiHostSession` (L2.8) nay ráp sẵn multi-host** (N station = N `IVpnSession`) + năng lực driver tap/SoftEther khai báo `L2Ethernet`/`L2BroadcastDomain`/`SupportsMultiHost`; **còn lại** = gắn uplink VPN vào adapter (driver data-plane đa-host) |

Hợp đồng transport phụ trợ: [IByteStreamTransport.cs:4](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IByteStreamTransport.cs#L4) — **đã có hiện thực dùng chung** [`TcpByteStream`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Tcp/TcpByteStream.cs#L22) (TCP trần, project `Transport.Tcp`) + [`TlsByteStream`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Tls/TlsByteStream.cs#L25) (TLS bọc TcpByteStream, project `Transport.Tls` — **F.1 đã tách project**: đáy TCP/TLS cho SSTP_DUPLEX_POST + PPP-over-stream, dùng chung SSTP/SoftEther/OpenConnect; OpenVPN-tcp dùng TcpByteStream trần) — và [IDatagramTransport.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IDatagramTransport.cs#L10) (UDP, chưa có impl; IKE/ESP demux thật ở [`Ipsec/Nat`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Nat), giữ làm nền DTLS F.3). *(2 hợp đồng `ISecuritySession`/`IPacketEncapsulator` đã **xóa ở P0.1** — shape phân kỳ với `EspSession`/framing thật; sẽ tái thiết kế từ ≥2 consumer thật ở roadmap F.2.)* Seam **resolve outer host**: [IHostResolver.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Net/IHostResolver.cs#L10) → [DnsHostResolver.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Net/DnsHostResolver.cs#L14) (literal-passthrough + chọn họ theo [`AddressFamilyPreference`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Net/AddressFamilyPreference.cs); pure `Select` ưu-tiên-1-họ-fallback-họ-kia, testable không cần DNS) — 2 consumer thật: SSTP `TlsByteStream` + L2TP `L2tpIpsecConnection.ResolveAsync` (P1.2).

đa số enum nay đã có **driver tiêu thụ thật** (đủ 7 driver đã wire — xem §4/§6/§7): 2 driver SSTP + L2TP/IPsec khai **L3Ip + UsesPpp +
AddressAssignment=Ipcp** (xem §6/§7), driver **IKEv2-native (V.1)** khai **L3Ip + không-PPP + Esp + AddressAssignment=ConfigPush** (CP cấp IP, ESP tunnel mode); thêm **OpenVPN (V2.h)** L3Ip(tun)/L2Ethernet(tap) + Tls + AEAD/CBC, **WireGuard (V3.f)** L3Ip + Udp + **Noise** + AddressAssignment=OutOfBand, **OpenConnect (V5.x)** L3Ip + Tls/**Dtls** + bare-IP (ConfigPush qua X-CSTP-*), và **SoftEther (V4.c)** L2Ethernet + Tls + AddressAssignment=**Dhcp**. Khi driver cần quyền (RawIp) mà process thiếu → ném [VpnElevationRequiredException.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/VpnElevationRequiredException.cs#L7).
**Phân loại lỗi kết nối**: cây ngoại lệ [VpnConnectionException.cs:8](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/VpnConnectionException.cs#L8) (base, **không** sealed) với 3 lớp con sealed —
[VpnAuthenticationException.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/VpnAuthenticationException.cs#L7) (sai credential: PPP MS-CHAPv2 fail / IKE PSK·HASH_R mismatch),
[VpnServerRejectedException.cs:8](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/VpnServerRejectedException.cs#L8) (server từ chối ở mức giao thức: SSTP Call-Connect-Nak / non-200 handshake / crypto-binding thiếu-hoặc-ngắn / IKE Quick Mode HASH(2) sai hoặc không có SA / **IKE handshake bị gateway từ chối bằng NOTIFY lỗi** NO-PROPOSAL-CHOSEN… — **P0.8a**),
[VpnNetworkTimeoutException.cs:8](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/VpnNetworkTimeoutException.cs#L8) (transport: socket/TLS/IO fail, IKE no-response **phân loại theo cổng** — im lặng sau float UDP/4500 ⇒ thông điệp nghi **forced-NAT-T** (P0.8a), Quick-Mode-rekey no-response). `OperationCanceledException` do caller hủy **không** bị tái phân loại (xem throw site ở §6/§7).
Model đi kèm: [VpnEndpoint.cs:6](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Models/VpnEndpoint.cs#L6) (Host/Port **+ `AddressFamilyPreference`** — chọn họ IP cho outer transport, P1.2),
[VpnCredentials.cs:4](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Models/VpnCredentials.cs#L4) (Username/Password + PreSharedKey),
[TunnelConfig.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Models/TunnelConfig.cs#L9) (AssignedAddress, PrefixLength=32, **AssignedAddressV6/PrefixLengthV6=64** (P1.1, null nếu không bật IPv6), DnsServers, Routes, Mtu=1400 — chính là `Config` ở bảng trên).

## 4. Điểm vào

[VpnClientBuilder.cs:18](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L18) đăng ký driver kiểu fluent;
[VpnClient.cs:8](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClient.cs#L8) tra driver theo tên (qua helper [`ResolveDriver` @ :25](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClient.cs#L25)) rồi ủy thác `ConnectAsync`.
Façade nay wire **7 driver**: `UseSstp()` / [`UseSstp(RemoteCertificateValidationCallback)` @ :36](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L36) (callback xác thực cert TLS — **P0.6**; không truyền ⇒ chấp nhận mọi cert) / `UseL2tpIpsec()` / [`UseL2tpIpsec(L2tpIpsecReconnectOptions)` @ :47](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L47) / [`UseL2tpIpsec(reconnect, L2tpIpsecTimeoutOptions)` @ :50](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L50) / `UseIkev2()` / [`UseIkev2(Ikev2ReconnectOptions)` @ :57](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L57) / [`UseIkev2(IkeCertificateTrust, …)` @ :65](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L65) (verify gateway bằng cert RFC 7296 §2.15) / [`UseOpenVpn(OpenVpnProfile)` @ :70](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L70) (+ overload client-cert/cert-callback/reconnect @ :73) / [`UseWireGuard(WireGuardConfig)` @ :78](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L78) (+ overload reconnect @ :81) / [`UseOpenConnect()` @ :89](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L89) (+ overload reconnect @ :92 và `(reconnect, cert-callback, groupSelect)` @ :99) / [`UseSoftEther(string hubName)` @ :107](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L107) (+ overload `SoftEtherSessionParams` @ :110, `(session, reconnect)` @ :113, `(hubName, enableIpv6)` @ :121) đều là wrapper gọi
[`AddDriver(IVpnProtocolDriver)` @ :23](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L23) (keyed theo `driver.Name`) — nên driver tự định nghĩa cũng nạp được.
`VpnClient` còn có [`GetCapabilities(protocol)` @ :22](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClient.cs#L22) trả `VpnDriverCapabilities`; **P0.5** gom cả hai về cùng [`ResolveDriver` @ :25](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClient.cs#L25) nên `GetCapabilities` và `ConnectAsync` ném **cùng `NotSupportedException`** (kèm danh sách protocol đã đăng ký) khi tra protocol chưa có driver.

```csharp
var vpn  = new VpnClientBuilder().UseSstp().UseL2tpIpsec().Build();
IVpnConnection conn = await vpn.ConnectAsync("l2tp-ipsec", endpoint, creds);
IVpnSession    sess = conn.Sessions[0];

// mở socket chạy TRONG tunnel:
var stack = sess.CreateTcpStack();                       // VpnSessionSocketsExtensions
var tcp   = await VpnTcpClient.ConnectAsync(stack, ip, 80);
Stream s  = tcp.GetStream();                             // cắm thẳng vào HttpClient
```

**MPPE** [Mppe/MppeKeyDerivation.cs:18](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Mppe/MppeKeyDerivation.cs#L18), [Mppe/MppeSession.cs:16](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Mppe/MppeSession.cs#L16); **Noise** [Noise/Curve25519DhGroup.cs:15](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/Curve25519DhGroup.cs#L15), [Noise/Blake2s.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/Blake2s.cs#L12), [Noise/Blake2sKeyedMac.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/Blake2sKeyedMac.cs#L11), [Noise/HmacBlake2sPrf.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/HmacBlake2sPrf.cs#L14), [Noise/NoiseKdf.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/NoiseKdf.cs#L11), [Noise/NoiseSymmetricState.cs:21](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/NoiseSymmetricState.cs#L21), [Noise/Ed25519Signer.cs:17](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/Ed25519Signer.cs#L17), [Sha256Hash.cs:13](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Sha256Hash.cs#L13) **(mới V.7.1: Ed25519 verify cert Nebula + SHA-256 transcript Noise IX)** | Primitive theo hợp đồng (đảo ngược phụ thuộc §1). DH MODP group 2 (1024-bit) + 14 (2048-bit); factory integrity `HmacSha1_96` (key20/ICV12 — IKEv1) & `HmacSha256_128` (key32/ICV16 — IKEv2). `Tls1Prf` = PRF TLS 1.0 (P_MD5⊕P_SHA1, RFC 2246) cho key-method-2 OpenVPN; `AntiReplayWindow` cửa sổ trượt 64-gói (RFC 4303) **dùng chung ESP + OpenVPN**. MD4/DES bắt buộc cho MS-CHAPv2 dù lỗi thời; `Sha0` (FIPS 180 1993 = SHA-1 bỏ ROTL1 ở message schedule, `IHashAlgo` 20B) bắt buộc cho auth password SoftEther (V.4, hash cục bộ không lên wire) — KAT FIPS-180 + đối chiếu khác SHA-1. **MPPE/RC4 (F.5b, nền PPTP V.6)**: `Rc4` (stream cipher KSA/PRGA, RFC 6229 KAT, broken RFC 7465) + `MppeKeyDerivation` (RFC 3078 §7.3 `GetNewKeyFromSHA` SHA-1 + initial-key SHA-only + re-key SHA→RC4-self + strength reduction 40/56/128-bit) + `MppeSession` (1 chiều: RC4 + coherency 12-bit + framing A/B/C/D, stateless re-key-mỗi-gói vs stateful re-key-mỗi-256-gói); MPPE start key suy từ MS-CHAPv2 qua `MsChapV2.DeriveMppe*StartKey` (cờ `isServer` chọn Magic2/Magic3). **MPPE+MS-CHAPv2 đã bị phá** — chỉ tương thích legacy. KAT RFC 3079 §3.5 (MasterKey/StartKey/SessionKey 40/56/128 + "Sample Encrypted Message"). `AesGcmCipher`/`ChaCha20Poly1305Cipher` là nơi `#if`: BCL native (`AesGcm` net7+, `ChaCha20Poly1305` net5+) vs BouncyCastle (netstandard2.0); cùng shape AEAD nonce 12B/tag 16B/key 32B (ChaCha20-Poly1305 RFC 8439, dùng cho NCP OpenVPN); `XChaCha20Poly1305Cipher` (draft-irtf-cfrg-xchacha: `HChaCha20` suy subkey rồi ủy quyền `ChaCha20Poly1305Cipher`, nonce 24B — dùng cho WireGuard cookie-reply V3.c). **Noise/ (F.4 — nền WireGuard V.3 / Nebula V.7, đã KAT; consumer đầu: [WireGuard](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard) V3.b/c)**: `Curve25519DhGroup` (X25519 RFC 7748, IANA group 31, `IDhGroup`), `Blake2s` (BLAKE2s-256 RFC 7693, `IHashAlgo`), `Blake2sKeyedMac` (keyed BLAKE2s output tùy chỉnh — WG mac1/mac2 16B), `HmacBlake2sPrf` (HMAC-BLAKE2s RFC 2104, `IPrf`), `NoiseKdf` (HKDF RFC 5869 trên HMAC-BLAKE2s), **`NoiseSymmetricState`** (V3.a — Noise spec §5.2 SymmetricState cho `Noise_IKpsk2_25519_ChaCha20Poly1305_BLAKE2s`: `InitializeWireGuard` seed `ck=HASH(CONSTRUCTION)`/`h=HASH(ck‖IDENTIFIER)`, `MixHash`/`MixKey` (Kdf2)/`MixKeyAndHash` (Kdf3, PSK)/`EncryptAndHash`+`DecryptAndHash` (ChaCha20-Poly1305 nonce `0^4‖counter` LE, AAD = `h` hiện tại)/`Split` (Kdf2 → cặp transport key 32B) — class state machine **đối xứng thuần**, không trạng thái mạng; tái dùng nguyên primitive F.4 qua DI `IPrf`/`IHashAlgo`/`IAeadCipher`). Khác `Aead/`: **không** `#if` native — BCL cả 2 TFM đều thiếu X25519/BLAKE2s nên dùng BouncyCastle giống nhau (vì vậy `BouncyCastle.Cryptography` nay là PackageReference **không điều kiện**). **ChaCha20 (V.10 — nền SSH)**: [`ChaCha20`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/ChaCha20.cs#L25) (stream cipher djb gốc — key 256-bit, nonce 8-byte, counter 64-bit, 20 vòng, qua BouncyCastle `ChaChaEngine`; keystream **stateful** [`Stream.NextKeystream`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/ChaCha20.cs#L81)/`Process`/`Skip` giữ counter qua các lần gọi như Salsa20 — **KHÔNG** phải layout IETF RFC 8439; KAT TC1 keystream block 0+1 byte-exact vs draft-strombergson) — `chacha20-poly1305@openssh.com` của SSH (Ssh V.10) dùng nó. |
| **Ipsec.Esp** | [EspSession.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspSession.cs#L9), [EspDataPlane.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspDataPlane.cs#L9), [EspTunnelChannel.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspTunnelChannel.cs#L12), [EspCipherSuite.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspCipherSuite.cs#L10) (+ [EspCbcHmacSuite.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspCbcHmacSuite.cs#L11) / [EspGcmSuite.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspGcmSuite.cs#L11)), [AntiReplayWindow.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/AntiReplayWindow.cs#L7) (ở Crypto — dùng chung ESP + OpenVPN data channel) | Data-plane IPsec: `Protect`/`TryUnprotect`, sequence dùng [`checked(+1)` @ EspSession:43](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspSession.cs#L43) → **OverflowException ở gói thứ 2³²** (backstop; rekey-by-sequence ở `EspDataPlane` bên dưới), chống replay (cửa sổ 64 gói). [`EspDataPlane`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspDataPlane.cs#L9) là base dùng chung của **cả 2 mode**: giữ SA hiện tại + SA cũ (make-before-break), `ProtectOutbound`/`TryUnprotectInbound`, watermark `RekeyNeeded` quanh 2³². [`EspTunnelChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspTunnelChannel.cs#L12) = ESP **tunnel mode** → `IPacketChannel` (gói IP nguyên gói, NextHeader 4/41, decap demux — data plane IKEv2, **F.8 xong**); `IpsecL2tpTransport` (driver L2TP) là **transport mode** trên cùng base. `EspCipherSuite` là base + 3 factory: `AesCbcHmacSha1` (đường **live** IKEv1), `AesCbcHmacSha256` (mặc định IKEv2), `AesGcm` (RFC 4106 — **nay negotiate được** cả IKEv1+IKEv2); wire `SPI‖Seq‖IV‖ct‖ICV`, encrypt-then-MAC. [`EspSuiteSelection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspSuiteSelection.cs#L14) (+ enum [`EspEncryptionAlgorithm`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/Enums/EspEncryptionAlgorithm.cs#L4)) là descriptor "suite đã chọn": ánh xạ thuật toán → độ dài keymat (`EncryptionKeyLengthBytes`+`SecondSliceLengthBytes` = integ-key cho CBC / salt 4B cho GCM) → `EspCipherSuite` qua `BuildSuite`, dùng chung V1 lẫn V2. |
| **Ipsec.Ike.V1** | [IkeV1Client.cs:18](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Client.cs#L18) + codec [IsakmpMessage.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IsakmpMessage.cs#L11), khóa [IkeV1KeyMaterial.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1KeyMaterial.cs#L12)/[IkeV1Phase2Keys.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Phase2Keys.cs#L10), [IkeV1Cipher.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Cipher.cs#L12), [IkeV1Auth.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Auth.cs#L10), [IkeV1QuickMode.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1QuickMode.cs#L10), [IkeV1NatDetection.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1NatDetection.cs#L12), [IkeV1Proposals.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Proposals.cs#L12), [IkeV1Lifetimes.cs:4](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Lifetimes.cs#L4) | Bắt tay ISAKMP/IKEv1 cho L2TP: Main Mode (MM1–MM6) + Quick Mode (QM1–QM3) → KEYMAT cho ESP. **Đây là IKE đang chạy thực tế.** Phase 1 đề xuất **AES-CBC + SHA1 + PSK + MODP 2/14**; Phase 2 đề xuất **AES-CBC-256+SHA1 trước, AES-GCM-16-256 sau** (ESP transform id 20). `ProcessQuickMode2`/`ProcessRekeyQuickMode2` **xác thực HASH(2)** của responder (RFC 2409 §5.5 = `prf(SKEYID_a, M-ID‖Ni_b‖payload-sau-HASH)`, hash trên **byte gốc nhận** qua `PayloadChainAfterFirst` — không re-encode nên gateway hợp lệ không bị false-reject; mismatch ⇒ `VpnServerRejectedException`) rồi đọc transform server chọn → lộ `NegotiatedEsp`/`RekeyNegotiatedEsp` (`EspSuiteSelection`); khoan dung suite — chỉ là GCM khi id=20, còn lại fallback CBC, nên VPN Gate vẫn CBC. `IkeV1Cipher` giữ **CBC IV-chaining** (RFC 2409 §5.5: IV Quick Mode/Informational = hash(IV-Phase1-cuối ‖ M-ID)) — lý do mỗi DPD/Delete/rekey có IV riêng. Thêm qua **Informational**: DPD keepalive ([IkeV1Dpd.cs](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Dpd.cs)), Quick Mode rekey (`BuildRekeyQuickMode1/2/3`), Delete teardown ([IkeV1Delete.cs](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Delete.cs)). **Rekey Phase 1 in-place (P1.3)**: client thuần chạy lại Main Mode+Quick Mode dưới một `IkeV1Client` mới (ISAKMP SA mới) — `IsForThisSa` so cookie initiator (8 byte cleartext) để orchestrator tách reply rekey khỏi DPD của SA cũ trên cùng socket. **Phân loại handshake bị từ chối** (P0.8a): `IkeV1Client.TryReadRejectNotify` nhận diện Informational clear-text mang NOTIFY lỗi (type 1–16383, tái dùng `IkeV1Dpd.TryReadNotifyType`) để driver fail-fast thay vì parse nhầm thành reply. |
| **Ipsec.Ike.V2** | [IkeClient.cs:19](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/IkeClient.cs#L19) + [IkeSaInitiator.cs:15](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/IkeSaInitiator.cs#L15), khóa [IkeKeyMaterial.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/IkeKeyMaterial.cs#L11)/[ChildSaKeys.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/ChildSaKeys.cs#L11), [IkeCipher.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/IkeCipher.cs#L12), [IkePskAuth.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/IkePskAuth.cs#L12), [NatDetection.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/NatDetection.cs#L12), [IkeProposals.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/IkeProposals.cs#L11), codec [IkeMessage.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/IkeMessage.cs#L10) + payload concrete [V2/Payloads/](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Payloads/) (gồm CERT/CERTREQ) + verify chữ ký [IkeSignatureAuth.cs:15](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/IkeSignatureAuth.cs#L15) + trust [Models/IkeCertificateTrust.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Models/IkeCertificateTrust.cs#L11) | IKEv2 PSK: IKE_SA_INIT + IKE_AUTH (sinh CHILD_SA/ESP keys, opt-in **CFG_REQUEST** cho virtual IP/DNS tunnel mode + **CERTREQ** khi verify responder bằng cert + **multi-TS** TSi/TSr nhiều subnet), IKE SA = AES-CBC-256 + HMAC-SHA-256-128 + PRF-SHA-256 + MODP-2048 + NAT-D. ESP CHILD_SA chào **2 proposal**: AES-CBC-256+SHA256 (#1) rồi AES-GCM-16-256 (#2) ([`EspProposals`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/IkeProposals.cs)); `ProcessAuthResponse` đọc proposal server chọn → `NegotiatedEsp` + `ChildKeys` đúng độ dài. Hậu-AUTH (F.7): **INFORMATIONAL** (DPD `BuildDeadPeerDetection` + DELETE `BuildDeleteChildSa()`/`BuildDeleteChildSa(spi)` [xóa CHILD_SA cũ theo SPI cụ thể sau rekey, §2.8]/`BuildDeleteIkeSa` + `BuildInformationalResponse`), **CREATE_CHILD_SA** rekey CHILD_SA make-before-break (`BuildRekeyChildSaRequest`/`ProcessRekeyChildSaResponse` → [`ChildSaParameters`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Models/ChildSaParameters.cs#L11)) **và rekey IKE SA** (F.7 3b — `BuildRekeyIkeSaRequest`/`ProcessRekeyIkeSaResponse`: SPI/DH mới, `IkeKeyMaterial.DeriveRekey`=`prf(SK_d_old, g^ir\|Ni\|Nr)` §2.18, swing toàn bộ "current IKE SA" SPI/cipher/SK_d + reset message-id về 0 — Phase-1-equivalent; **trước khi swing chuẩn bị sẵn** INFORMATIONAL+DELETE cho IKE SA cũ mã hóa bằng SK_* cũ → `TakePendingOldIkeSaDelete` cho driver gửi trên SA cũ, §2.18); message-id counter. Payload model: [`ConfigurationPayload`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Payloads/ConfigurationPayload.cs#L13) (§3.15) + [`DeletePayload`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Payloads/DeletePayload.cs#L10) (§3.11) + [`EapPayload`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Payloads/EapPayload.cs#L11) (§3.16, bọc gói EAP RFC 3748 §4) + [`CertificatePayload`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Payloads/CertificatePayload.cs#L10)/[`CertificateRequestPayload`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Payloads/CertificateRequestPayload.cs#L11) (§3.6/§3.7, X.509 DER); VendorId còn lại → [RawPayload.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Payloads/RawPayload.cs#L9). **Responder cert auth** (RFC 7296 §2.15 chữ ký số): `IkeClient.VerifyResponderAuth` parse CERT → `IkeCertificateTrust.IsTrusted` (pin leaf / chain CA) → `IkeSignatureAuth.VerifyResponderSignature` (RSA method 1 cả 2 TFM; ECDSA 9/10/11 net5+) verify trên SignedOctets (dùng chung `IkePskAuth.ComputeSignedOctets`); fail/cert-không-tin/downgrade-PSK ⇒ `VpnServerRejectedException`. **EAP-MSCHAPv2** (RFC 7296 §2.16): `BuildAuthRequestEap` (IKE_AUTH bỏ AUTH ⇒ báo EAP) + `ProcessAuthResponseEap` pump (verify PSK AUTH responder msg4, bơm EAP qua nhiều vòng IKE_AUTH, AUTH cuối bằng **MSK** 2 chiều, CHILD_SA ở exchange cuối) → `EapEstablished`/`EapFailed`; state-machine [`EapMsChapV2Client`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Eap/EapMsChapV2Client.cs#L14) tái dùng codec [`MsChapV2`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/MsChapV2.cs) (Crypto). **Protocol đủ cho driver V.1 IKEv2-native; driver nay consume PSK / EAP-MSCHAPv2 (auth client) + verify responder PSK / cert + multi-TS + gắn timer rekey CHILD_SA và IKE SA, mỗi loại rekey phát DELETE cho SA cũ (không để gateway tự timeout) — còn lại của V.1 là validate live (lab Q.1) + honest-first NAT-T + cert trên đường EAP.** |
| **L2tp** | [L2tpClient.cs:13](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpClient.cs#L13) + [L2tpSession.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpSession.cs#L9) trên [IL2tpTransport.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/IL2tpTransport.cs#L7), [L2tpControlChannel.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpControlChannel.cs#L12), codec [L2tpCodec.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpCodec.cs#L11) | L2TPv2 (RFC 2661): tunnel SCCRQ→SCCRP→SCCCN, session ICRQ→ICRP→ICCN (SCCCN/ICCN tự gửi trong `OnControl`); truyền tin cậy Ns/Nr + ZLB ack + retransmit head-of-line với **exponential backoff+jitter** (1s ×2 tới cap 8s, P1.4) + **cap số lần** (`MaxRetransmits`, 0 = vô hạn; driver L2TP/IPsec đặt 8) → vượt cap raise [`Failed` @ :49](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpControlChannel.cs#L49). **Multi-session (P1.7)**: một tunnel mang **N session** — `ConnectAsync` dựng `PrimarySession`, [`OpenSessionAsync` @ :80](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpClient.cs#L80) mở session phụ (best-effort; server từ chối bằng CDN ⇒ exception). Mỗi `L2tpSession` có `LocalSessionId`/`PeerSessionId` + `DataReceived`/`SendDataAsync` riêng; inbound data **demux theo session id**, ICRP/CDN tương quan theo session id ở header (fallback session đang mở khi peer trả 0). `L2tpCodec` serialize header+AVP, phân biệt control (T=1) vs data (T=0). Keepalive `SendHelloAsync` (HELLO); teardown `L2tpSession.SendCallDisconnectAsync` (CDN) + `SendStopControlConnectionAsync` (StopCCN). Event [`Disconnected` @ :59](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpClient.cs#L59) (StopCCN/control-fail **hoặc** session chính bị CDN) chính là tín hiệu "L2TP teardown" ở §6.1; [`DataReceived` @ :56](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpClient.cs#L56) là PPP inbound của session chính. |

[Transport/OpenVpnTapChannel.cs:15](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnTapChannel.cs#L15) | Protocol OpenVPN thuần (community server) **không PPP**. **V2.a+config+V2.b xong**: (1) codec gói control — byte đầu = 5-bit opcode + 3-bit key_id (`Header`/`ReadOpcode`/`ReadKeyId`), gói control = `session_id(8)` + ACK array (`ack_len(1)` + `4·M` packet-id + `remote_session_id(8)` nếu M>0) + `packet_id(4)` + payload TLS (P_ACK_V1 bỏ 2 trường cuối); `EncodeControl`/`TryDecodeControl`. (2) **reliability state machine** (clock inject, tất định): `OpenVpnReliableSendWindow` (gán packet-id từ 0 + in-flight window + `CollectDue(nowMs)` gửi/retransmit backoff + `Acknowledge` + `IsExhausted`), `OpenVpnReliableReceiveWindow` (dedup + buffer lệch-thứ-tự + `TryDeliver` in-order cho TLS + `TakeAcks` ≤8/≤4), policy `OpenVpnReliabilityOptions` (mirror `L2tpRetransmitOptions`). (3) **config**: [`OpenVpnProfile`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Config/OpenVpnProfile.cs#L11) (model lập trình driver tiêu thụ — remote(s)/proto/device/TLS material/cipher/auth/options + `OtherDirectives` raw) + [`OpenVpnConfigParser`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Config/OpenVpnConfigParser.cs#L13) `Parse(text)` đọc `.ovpn` **thuần text→model không I/O** (cert/key inline `<ca>…</ca>` → PEM, dạng path → `FilePath`; bỏ comment, arg trong `"…"`, flatten `<connection>`, inline thắng path). (4) **V2.b TLS-in-control**: `OpenVpnControlChannel` (client) ráp 2 reliability window + codec + session-id (64-bit random) + transport `IOpenVpnTransport`, `ConnectAsync` làm reset HARD_RESET_CLIENT_V2 ⇄ HARD_RESET_SERVER_V2 (packet-id 0) rồi `SslStream` AuthenticateAsClient trên `OpenVpnTlsBridgeStream` in-memory (write TLS → fragment ≤1200 + backpressure theo window; read ← payload in-order); pump acks piggyback ≤4 / P_ACK riêng ≤8 + retransmit theo timer; lộ `TlsStream` cho V2.d. (5) **V2.c wrap control packet** (opt-in `IOpenVpnControlWrap` ở ctor; null = gửi verbatim): [`OpenVpnStaticKey`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/OpenVpnStaticKey.cs#L17) parse `ta.key` 2048-bit (16 dòng×32 hex = `key2`: 2 bộ `cipher[64]\|hmac[64]`); [`OpenVpnTlsAuthWrap`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/OpenVpnTlsAuthWrap.cs#L19) (`--tls-auth`) bọc HMAC (mặc định SHA1, dùng được SHA256…) — wire `op\|sid\|HMAC\|replay_id(4)\|net_time(4)\|body`, HMAC = `H(K_out, replay_id\|net_time\|op\|sid\|body)`, key theo `OpenVpnKeyDirection` (client = Inverse/Bidirectional); [`OpenVpnTlsCryptWrap`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/OpenVpnTlsCryptWrap.cs#L21) (`--tls-crypt`) xác thực **+ mã hóa** cố định HMAC-SHA256 + AES-256-CTR (tái dùng [`AesCtr`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/AesCtr.cs)) — wire `op\|sid\|packet_id(8)\|tag(32)\|E(body)`, tag = `HMAC256(Ka, op\|sid\|packet_id\|body)`, IV = `tag[0..16]`, hướng cố định theo role (client out=set1/in=set0); cả 2 bọc **mọi** gói control kể cả HARD_RESET, unwrap thất bại ⇒ drop datagram. Codec là byte→byte quanh `EncodeControl`/`TryDecodeControl` (decode/state-machine không đổi). (6) **V2.d key-method-2 + data channel AEAD**: sau handshake, client gửi key-method-2 message trên `TlsStream` (`uint32 0 \| key_method=2 \| key_source2(pre-master 48 + 2×random 32) \| P_string options/user/pass`) rồi đọc reply server (random×2 + options), [`OpenVpnKeyMethod2.DeriveDataKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnKeyMethod2.cs#L122) suy khóa bằng [`Tls1Prf`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Tls1Prf.cs#L11) (master secret 48 → key2 256B, layout `key2` tái dùng `OpenVpnStaticKey`), **hướng key SỬA BUG**: [`SliceDataKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnKeyMethod2.cs#L108) nay đúng `isServer ? (1,0) : (0,1)` ⇒ **client out=set0/in=set1** (server ngược) — trước đảo nửa key2 (out=set1/in=set0) nên data không chạy live; **đã kiểm chứng live** với OpenVPN server thật (VPN Gate) → [`OpenVpnDataChannelKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnDataChannelKeys.cs#L9) (cipher key 32 + implicit IV 8 mỗi chiều); [`OpenVpnKeyNegotiation`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnKeyNegotiation.cs#L9) chạy trao đổi đó trên stream (hook [`OpenVpnControlChannel.NegotiateKeyMaterialAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/OpenVpnControlChannel.cs#L149)). **Data channel sau interface [`IOpenVpnDataChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/IOpenVpnDataChannel.cs#L10)** (`Protect`/`TryUnprotect`/`SentPacketCount`) với **2 hiện thực** dùng chung wrapper [`OpenVpnDataPlane`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnDataPlane.cs#L11): (a) **AEAD** [`OpenVpnDataChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnDataChannel.cs#L22) gói **AES/ChaCha-GCM** (tái dùng [`AesGcmCipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Aead/AesGcmCipher.cs)): wire `op\|key_id(1)\|[peer_id(3)]\|packet_id(4)\|tag(16)\|ct`, nonce = `packet_id ‖ implicit_iv(8)`, AAD = header rõ; (b) **non-AEAD CBC** [`OpenVpnCbcDataChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnCbcDataChannel.cs#L23) (cipher một server NCP-less như OpenVPN function của SoftEther dùng — AES-128/192/256-CBC + HMAC `--auth`): wire `op\|key_id(1)\|[peer_id(3)]\|HMAC(full)\|IV(16)\|AES-CBC(PKCS7(packet_id(4)‖payload))`, HMAC phủ `IV‖ct` (prepend, so hằng-thời-gian), packet-id 4B **trong** envelope mã hóa (IV random/gói) — [`OpenVpnCbcCipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnCbcCipher.cs#L12) catalog AES-CBC + [`OpenVpnDataAuth`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnDataAuth.cs#L12) map `--auth`→HMAC full-digest SHA1/256/384/512/MD5, key [`OpenVpnCbcDataKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnCbcDataKeys.cs#L9) cắt qua [`SliceCbcDataKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnKeyMethod2.cs#L132)/[`OpenVpnKeyMaterial.DeriveCbcDataKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnKeyMaterial.cs#L29) (cipher key + HMAC key từ key2). **P_DATA_V1 vs V2**: cả 2 channel có tham số `dataV2` (gửi V2 có peer-id 3B / V1 không peer-id 1B); **nhận tự phát hiện theo opcode** (DataV2→header 4B, DataV1→header 1B) nên dung nạp cả hai; cả 2 đều packet-id `checked(++)` (overflow ⇒ phải rekey) + cửa sổ chống replay 64-gói ([`AntiReplayWindow`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/AntiReplayWindow.cs#L7) ở Crypto). (7) **V2.e config-pull + keepalive + make-before-break**: [`OpenVpnControlMessage`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnControlMessage.cs#L10) build/read control string NUL-terminated trên `TlsStream` (text — không có 4-byte sentinel như key-method); [`OpenVpnControlChannel.RequestConfigAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/OpenVpnControlChannel.cs#L164) gửi `PUSH_REQUEST` đọc `PUSH_REPLY` → [`OpenVpnPushReply`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnPushReply.cs#L14) parse `ifconfig`/`route`/`dhcp-option DNS`/`peer-id`/`ping`/`ping-restart`/`cipher`/`topology` → `ToTunnelConfig` (subnet→prefix từ netmask, net30→/30); keepalive [`OpenVpnPing`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnPing.cs#L8) magic 16B (gói data) + [`OpenVpnKeepalive`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnKeepalive.cs#L11) timing clock-inject (`ShouldSendPing`/`IsPeerDead`); [`OpenVpnDataPlane`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnDataPlane.cs#L11) **mirror `EspDataPlane`** giữ current + previous data channel (soft-reset rekey không mất gói in-flight), `RekeyNeeded` quanh 2³² packet-id. (8) **V2.f NCP + compression stub**: [`OpenVpnDataCipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnDataCipher.cs#L12) catalog (AES-256-GCM/AES-128-GCM/**CHACHA20-POLY1305**, `TryResolve` theo tên, `TryResolveServerList`/`ExtractIvCiphers` đọc `IV_CIPHERS` server đẩy ngược, `AdvertisedList`, key size + factory AEAD); [`OpenVpnPeerInfo`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnPeerInfo.cs#L16) build `IV_*` (IV_PROTO/IV_NCP=2/**IV_CIPHERS**) cho key-method-2 — cấu hình qua [`OpenVpnPeerInfoOptions`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnPeerInfo.cs#L85) (**push-peer-info nâng cao**: IV_PLAT auto-detect linux/win/mac + **IV_MTU** (driver bơm tun MTU) + informational IV_PLAT_VER/IV_SSL_VER/IV_GUI_VER + user-vars `UV_*` qua `Extra`); suy khóa tách **cipher-independent** `DeriveKey2` → `SliceDataKeys(key2, cipher, isServer)` để chốt cipher **sau PUSH_REPLY** (`OpenVpnKeyMaterial` giữ key2; `OpenVpnKeyNegotiation`/`NegotiateKeyMaterialAsync` trả material), `OpenVpnDataChannel` tự-chọn AES-GCM theo độ dài khóa (16/128, 32/256); [`OpenVpnCompression`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnCompression.cs#L11) framing **stub** (None/CompLzo 1-byte 0xFA/StubV2 zero-overhead) — chỉ chào no-compression, gói thật-sự-nén ⇒ reject. **CHACHA20-POLY1305** (RFC 8439, [`ChaCha20Poly1305Cipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Aead/ChaCha20Poly1305Cipher.cs#L18) shim BCL native net5+ / BouncyCastle ns2.0) đã vào catalog + IV_CIPHERS, cả 3 AEAD chạy thật ở data channel (driver truyền `cipher.CreateCipher()`). (9) **V2.g transport TCP + tap-mode**: [`OpenVpnTcpFraming`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnTcpFraming.cs#L15) framing 16-bit big-endian length cho stream transport (`Encode` egress + decoder `Append`/`TryReadPacket` ráp lại gói qua mọi ranh đọc — hiện thực OpenVPN của seam F.2 `IPacketEncapsulator`), [`OpenVpnTcpTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnTcpTransport.cs#L14) bọc [`IByteStreamTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IByteStreamTransport.cs) (F.1 — TCP/TLS) thành `IOpenVpnTransport` (`SendAsync` length-prefix + write nối tiếp; `RunReceiveLoopAsync` đọc→ráp→`DatagramReceived`); cầu nối **device-link** [`OpenVpnDataLink`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnDataLink.cs#L15) (compression-frame + `OpenVpnDataPlane.Protect`/`TryUnprotect` ↔ sink transport) với 2 hiện thực: [`OpenVpnTunChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnTunChannel.cs#L12) (`dev tun` → L3 `IPacketChannel`, payload = gói IP, MaxHeaderLength 0) + [`OpenVpnTapChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnTapChannel.cs#L15) (`dev tap` → L2 `IEthernetChannel` cắm fabric Ethernet, payload = khung Ethernet, MaxHeaderLength 14 + MAC + resolution) — wire data channel **y hệt**, chỉ khác nội dung payload + medium kênh. **(10) V2.h transport UDP + driver**: [`OpenVpnUdpTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnUdpTransport.cs#L13) bọc [`IDatagramTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IDatagramTransport.cs) (UDP) thành `IOpenVpnTransport` — 1 datagram = 1 gói nên **không framing** (sibling UDP của `OpenVpnTcpTransport`); 0-byte không phải EOF. `OpenVpnDataLink.TryReceivePayload` nay **drop gói ping** (`OpenVpnPing.IsPing`) sau giải mã+de-compress để keepalive không lọt vào IP/Ethernet layer. Driver `Drivers.OpenVpn` ráp tất cả thành tunnel chạy thật (xem bảng **Drivers.OpenVpn** ở §5). **(11) V.2-occ** (offline): [`OpenVpnClientCertificate`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Helpers/OpenVpnClientCertificate.cs#L26) nạp `cert`/`key` (PEM inline hoặc path) → `X509Certificate2` có private key (net5+ `CreateFromPem`→PKCS#12; ns2.0 BouncyCastle PEM→PKCS#12); [`OpenVpnControlChannel.SendExitNotifyAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/OpenVpnControlChannel.cs) gửi explicit-exit-notify (`EXIT_NOTIFY`) best-effort + lộ `ServerKeyMethodOptions` (NCP-less mining IV_CIPHERS). **Chưa**: `tls-ekm` (F.5a — scaffold interface [`ITlsKeyingMaterialExporter`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/ITlsKeyingMaterialExporter.cs) khai báo nhưng **chưa hiện thực**: `SslStream` net8/ns2.0 không có RFC 5705 exporter — đã kiểm bằng reflection; `ExportKeyingMaterial` chỉ có net9+ / cần BouncyCastle TLS); **soft-reset make-before-break** (hiện rekey bằng re-establish). **VALIDATE LIVE RỘNG (đã chạy thật, 2026-06-24)**: (a) **VPN Gate** tun/UDP AES-128-CBC NCP-less P_DATA_V1 — tunnel + HTTP checkip + UDP DNS + ICMP. (b) **server tự host** (lab [`openvpn`](../lab/openvpn) — OpenVPN 2.6 community, biến PROTO/DEV/CIPHER): **tun UDP + NCP AES-256-GCM (P_DATA_V2)** (server `Data Channel: cipher 'AES-256-GCM', peer-id: 0` + PUSH_REPLY `protocol-flags cc-exit`) + **tun TCP** (16-bit framing, HTTP 4/4 + 64KB) + **gói lớn ~64KB** cả 2 carrier (Q.4 **không tái hiện** trên download) + **tap server-bridge** (L2/ARP, `tap bridge bound on 10.60.0.50` + ICMP RTT 1ms). **RESIDUAL (KHÔNG phải OpenVPN — shared IpStack, cross-ref Q.4)**: HTTP **upload** đôi khi stall do `TcpIpStack` send-window không reopen (1 byte/segment zero-window persist) — tcpdump xác nhận tunnel chở MỌI gói TCP đúng 2 chiều (data plane V.2 đúng); intermittent theo RTT; ghi bảng "Khác biệt". **Còn lại (chưa kiểm live)**: tap IPv6 pool / tap pure-DHCP & multi-host với server thật / OCC strict. **Data plane server-role chỉ trong test.** (xem [`11`](11-todo-roadmap.md) §V.2 + [`06`](06-openvpn.md)). |

[DataChannel/WireGuardReplayProtector.cs:19](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/DataChannel/WireGuardReplayProtector.cs#L19), [DataChannel/WireGuardTransport.cs:24](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/DataChannel/WireGuardTransport.cs#L24), [Handshake/Models/WireGuardInitiationMessage.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/Models/WireGuardInitiationMessage.cs#L9), [Handshake/Models/WireGuardResponseMessage.cs:8](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/Models/WireGuardResponseMessage.cs#L8), [Handshake/Models/WireGuardCookieReplyMessage.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/Models/WireGuardCookieReplyMessage.cs#L11), [Handshake/Models/WireGuardTransportKeys.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/Models/WireGuardTransportKeys.cs#L11) | Protocol WireGuard thuần — **V3.b handshake Noise_IKpsk2 + V3.c mac1/mac2 + cookie-reply + V3.d data channel type-4 + V3.e timers/state machine + V3.f config tĩnh/channel xong** (consumer đầu của Noise/ F.4 + V3.a). (1) [`WireGuardConstants`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/WireGuardConstants.cs#L17) — `CONSTRUCTION`/`IDENTIFIER` re-export từ [`NoiseSymmetricState`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/NoiseSymmetricState.cs#L21) (single source, không lệch) + `LABEL_MAC1`/`LABEL_COOKIE` (chờ V3.c) + kích thước (`KeyLength`32/`TagLength`16/`TimestampLength`12/`MacLength`16/`IndexLength`4) + message type 1–4 + `InitiationMessageLength`148/`ResponseMessageLength`92. (2) [`WireGuardTai64n`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/WireGuardTai64n.cs#L19) — `Now()`/`Encode(instant)` ra TAI64N 12B (8B giây TAI base `0x400000000000000A` big-endian + 4B nanosecond big-endian) + `Compare` lexicographic đơn điệu (responder chỉ kiểm timestamp tăng nghiêm ngặt). (3) [`WireGuardMessageCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/WireGuardMessageCodec.cs#L13) — `EncodeInitiation`/`TryDecodeInitiation` (type-1 148B) + `EncodeResponse`/`TryDecodeResponse` (type-2 92B) + `EncodeCookieReply`/`TryDecodeCookieReply` (type-3 64B) đúng từng byte: type byte + 3 reserved zero + index 32-bit **little-endian** + ephemeral 32 + AEAD field; length/type sai ⇒ `false` (drop). V3.c thêm `ApplyMacs`/`VerifyMac1`/`ReadMac1` thao tác mac1/mac2 **in-place** trên buffer đã encode (offset suy từ độ dài: mac1 = cuối−32, mac2 = cuối−16, dùng chung type-1/2). (4) [`WireGuardHandshake`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/WireGuardHandshake.cs#L23) — state machine **đối xứng thuần** 1 phía (initiator `CreateInitiation`→`ConsumeResponse`, responder `ConsumeInitiation`→`CreateResponse`, `DeriveTransportKeys` Split + hoán đổi theo role để `send`bên-này = `recv`bên-kia); chỉ **xếp thứ tự** mix/DH/AEAD đúng whitepaper §5.4, tái dùng nguyên [`NoiseSymmetricState`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/NoiseSymmetricState.cs#L21) (`InitializeWireGuard`/`MixHash`/`MixKey`/`MixKeyAndHash`/`EncryptAndHash`/`DecryptAndHash`/`Split`) + [`Curve25519DhGroup`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/Curve25519DhGroup.cs#L15) (X25519) + [`ChaCha20Poly1305Cipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Aead/ChaCha20Poly1305Cipher.cs#L18) qua DI; mỗi `KDF1(ck,x)` whitepaper hiện thực bằng `MixKey` (KDF2) — output đầu (chaining key) giống hệt, cipher key thừa luôn bị ghi đè trước AEAD kế; bước PSK `KDF3` là `MixKeyAndHash`. Sai tag/PSK ⇒ `ConsumeInitiation`/`ConsumeResponse` trả `false`. (5) **V3.c mac1/mac2 + cookie-reply (DoS, whitepaper §5.4.4/§5.4.7)** — [`WireGuardMac`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/WireGuardMac.cs#L22) keyed-BLAKE2s-128: `ForRecipient(pub)` tiền-hash `mac1Key=HASH(LABEL_MAC1‖pub)`/`CookieKey=HASH(LABEL_COOKIE‖pub)`, `ComputeMac1`/`VerifyMac1` + `ComputeMac2`/`VerifyMac2` (cookie-keyed), so sánh **constant-time** (tự cài cho cả ns2.0); [`WireGuardCookie`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/WireGuardCookie.cs#L21) `ComputeCookie(secret,addr)=MAC(secret,addr)` + `CreateReply` (responder seal cookie bằng [`XChaCha20Poly1305Cipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Aead/XChaCha20Poly1305Cipher.cs#L14), nonce 24B, AAD = mac1 gói kích hoạt) / `TryReadCookie` (initiator mở, sai ⇒ false). `WireGuardHandshake` gắn wire layer: `StampOutgoingMacs` (stamp mac1 key-peer + mac2 nếu có cookie, lưu mac1 vừa gửi), `VerifyIncomingMac1` (verify key-self, drop nếu sai), `CreateCookieReply`/`ConsumeCookieReply` (cache cookie → mac2 lần kế). (6) **V3.d data channel type-4 (whitepaper §5.4.6)** — [`WireGuardDataCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/DataChannel/WireGuardDataCodec.cs#L17) dựng/đọc gói transport-data 16B header `type(1)|reserved(3)|receiver(4 LE)|counter(8 LE)` + AEAD output (ciphertext‖tag16); `WriteNonce` ra nonce 12B = `0^4‖counter(8 LE)`; length/type/reserved sai ⇒ `false` (drop). [`WireGuardTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/DataChannel/WireGuardTransport.cs#L24) stateful theo cặp [`WireGuardTransportKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/Models/WireGuardTransportKeys.cs#L11) từ Split: `Seal` (ChaCha20-Poly1305 nonce counter-LE, **AAD rỗng**, counter u64 đơn điệu **từ 0**, overflow ⇒ ném — rekey trước), `TryOpen` (kiểm receiver-index của mình → anti-replay → AEAD; sai ⇒ drop), `Keepalive` = `Seal(empty)` (payload 0). [`WireGuardReplayProtector`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/DataChannel/WireGuardReplayProtector.cs#L19) chống replay 64-gói **trên counter u64 đầy đủ**: **tái dùng** [`AntiReplayWindow`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/AntiReplayWindow.cs#L7) cho 32-bit thấp (ánh xạ counter-0-based → window-1-based bằng `low+1`) trong một epoch high-32, tự theo dõi high-32 (epoch tiến ⇒ reset window; epoch cũ ⇒ replay) — vì `AntiReplayWindow` là `uint` còn WG counter là `u64`. (7) **V3.e timers + state machine (whitepaper §6.2)** — [`WireGuardTimers`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/WireGuardTimers.cs#L14) hằng timer ở **ms**: `RekeyAfterTimeMs`120s/`RejectAfterTimeMs`180s/`RekeyAttemptTimeMs`90s/`RekeyTimeoutMs`5s/`KeepaliveTimeoutMs`10s + `RekeyAfterMessages`(2⁶⁰)/`RejectAfterMessages`(2⁶⁴−2¹³−1) + `PersistentKeepaliveMs`(0=tắt mặc định), bất biến + override cho test + `Default`. [`WireGuardPeerState`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/WireGuardPeerState.cs#L22) state machine **clock-inject** (mirror [`OpenVpnKeepalive`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnKeepalive.cs#L11): mỗi quyết định nhận `nowMs`): ghi sự kiện `OnHandshakeInitiated`/`OnHandshakeCompleted`/`OnDataSent`/`OnDataReceived`/`Reset`; quyết định **thuần** `NeedsHandshake`/`NeedsRekey`(t≥120s hoặc đếm gói)/`IsSessionDead`(t≥180s hoặc đếm gói)/`ShouldResendHandshake`(REKEY_TIMEOUT 5s+jitter inject)/`ShouldAbandonHandshake`(REKEY_ATTEMPT_TIME 90s)/`ShouldSendKeepalive`(persistent đúng nhịp + passive sau nhận data 10s) + `Evaluate(nowMs)` chọn 1 [`WireGuardSessionAction`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Enums/WireGuardSessionAction.cs#L8) theo độ khẩn (abandon>resend; initiate>dead>keepalive); không giữ key/crypto, không thread-safe (driver gọi từ 1 timer/IO loop). (8) **V3.f config tĩnh + channel** — [`WireGuardConfig`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Config/WireGuardConfig.cs#L20) (private key, address/DNS, MTU 1420) **single-peer** qua trường tiện ích (`PeerPublicKey?`/`PresharedKey?`/`AllowedIps`/`PersistentKeepaliveSeconds`) **hoặc multi-peer** qua `Peers` (`IReadOnlyList<`[`WireGuardPeer`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Config/WireGuardPeer.cs#L12)`>`) + `EnumeratePeers()` chuẩn hóa + `ToTunnelConfig()` → `TunnelConfig` **tĩnh** (không IPCP/DHCP, routes = hợp allowed-ips mọi peer); [`WireGuardChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Transport/WireGuardChannel.cs#L24) `IPacketChannel` (Medium=Ip, MaxHeaderLength=0) bọc một [`WireGuardTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/DataChannel/WireGuardTransport.cs#L24): `WriteIpPacketAsync` = Seal+send, `Deliver` = TryOpen→raise (drop keepalive rỗng), `SendKeepaliveAsync`; callback `onPacketSealed`/`onPacketReceived` cho driver bơm timer. (9) **V.3 multi-peer crypto-routing** — [`IpPrefix`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Routing/IpPrefix.cs#L18) value-object CIDR thuần (`TryParse` net/prefix|host, mask host-bits, `Contains` so bit, lệch family ⇒ false), [`IpPacketDestination`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Routing/IpPacketDestination.cs#L13) đọc dest từ goi IP v4 (offset 16)/v6 (offset 24) — tối thiểu, **không kéo IpStack** vào project protocol, [`WireGuardCryptoRouter`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Routing/WireGuardCryptoRouter.cs#L18) bảng route bất biến `Build(per-peer allowed-ips)` + `TryRoute(dest)` **longest-prefix** → peer index (tie = peer thêm trước; không phủ ⇒ false), [`WireGuardMultiPeerChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Transport/WireGuardMultiPeerChannel.cs#L25) `IPacketChannel` ổn định trước N `WireGuardChannel`: `WriteIpPacketAsync` route dest → peer (single-peer ⇒ peer 0 không cần parse IP), `SetPeerChannel(i, ch)` hot-swap channel 1 peer (rekey, peer khác giữ nguyên), `Deliver(span)` thử từng peer channel → index peer mở được (gói inbound gán về peer đó) hoặc −1, `onNoRoute` báo drop (`VpnDropReason.NoRoute`). I/O socket + handshake loop đa-peer nằm ở driver `Drivers.WireGuard` (V3.f). **Thuần protocol, không server; interop với WireGuard thật chờ lab Q.1.** (xem [`11`](11-todo-roadmap.md) §V.3). |
| **SoftEther** *(V4.a–c)* | [Pack/Pack.cs:17](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/Pack.cs#L17), [Pack/PackElement.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackElement.cs#L12), [Pack/PackValue.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackValue.cs#L11), [Pack/Enums/PackValueType.cs:8](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/Enums/PackValueType.cs#L8), [Pack/PackConstants.cs:8](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackConstants.cs#L8), [Pack/PackBufferWriter.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackBufferWriter.cs#L11), [Pack/PackBufferReader.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackBufferReader.cs#L12), [Pack/SoftEtherAnsi.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/SoftEtherAnsi.cs#L9) | **V4.a PACK codec xong** (framing nền của mọi control/RPC SoftEther; re-implement từ spec [`07`](07-softether.md), **không copy GPL**). [`Pack`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/Pack.cs#L17) = list [`PackElement`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackElement.cs#L12); mỗi element {`Name`≤63, một [`PackValueType`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/Enums/PackValueType.cs#L8) (`Int`=0/`Data`=1/`Str`=2/`UniStr`=3/`Int64`=4), mảng [`PackValue`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackValue.cs#L11) ≥1 cùng kiểu}. Codec **big-endian** đúng wire: `uint32(num_elements)` → mỗi element `BufStr(name)·uint32(type)·uint32(num_value)·value[]`; **BufStr** = `uint32(len+1)`+`len` byte (quirk +1, **không** NUL); **STR** = `uint32(len)` (không +1, Latin-1 8-bit qua [`SoftEtherAnsi`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/SoftEtherAnsi.cs#L9)); **UNISTR** = `uint32(utf8len+1)`+utf8+**1 NUL** (Unicode/UTF-8); INT/INT64 big-endian 4/8 byte; DATA = `uint32(len)`+bytes. [`ToBytes`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/Pack.cs#L147)/[`Parse`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/Pack.cs#L160) thuần (**không I/O**) qua [`PackBufferWriter`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackBufferWriter.cs#L11)/[`PackBufferReader`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackBufferReader.cs#L12) (`ref struct`, chống underrun); helper `Set*`/`Get*` theo tên (single + `Set*Array` đa-value) + tra cứu **case-insensitive**; input lỗi (underrun/đếm vượt [`PackConstants`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackConstants.cs#L8)/trùng tên/kiểu lạ) ⇒ `FormatException`. **Namespace gốc** (không segment `.Pack`) để type `Pack` không bị namespace cùng tên che. **V4.b control handshake xong**: [`SoftEtherWatermark`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherWatermark.cs#L20) (POST watermark, blob placeholder) + [`SoftEtherAuth`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherAuth.cs#L18) (`secure_password` = SHA0(SHA0(pw‖UPPER(user))‖random), tái dùng `Sha0` F.5a) + [`SoftEtherHandshake`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L22) (`ParseHello`/`BuildLoginPack`/`ParseWelcome` thuần + `RunAsync` trên [`IByteStreamTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IByteStreamTransport.cs)) + [`SoftEtherHttpPackCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHttpPackCodec.cs#L14) (PACK trong thân HTTP). **V4.c data plane Ethernet-over-TLS xong**: [`SoftEtherDataFrameCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherDataFrameCodec.cs#L13) (block `uint32(n)·{uint32(size)·bytes}` thuần) + [`SoftEtherDataBlockReader`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherDataBlockReader.cs#L16) (ráp block qua partial read) + [`SoftEtherEthernetChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherEthernetChannel.cs#L19) (`IEthernetChannel`, drop keep-alive). **V.4 payload codec (use_compress/use_encrypt) xong**: [`SoftEtherPayloadCompressor`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherPayloadCompressor.cs#L23) (DEFLATE per-frame, magic `0xDEADBEEFCAFEFACE` + chỉ nén khi nhỏ hơn; `DeflateStream` cả 2 TFM) + [`SoftEtherEncryptedTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherEncryptedTransport.cs#L22) (decorator `IByteStreamTransport` áp RC4 keystream **per-direction** dưới block framing, tái dùng [`Rc4`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Rc4.cs); khóa suy từ session key + nhãn hướng); thứ tự **compress-rồi-encrypt** (mặc định tắt — payload thô trên TLS). Driver L2 thật ở [`Drivers.SoftEther`](#drivers) (§5 *Drivers.SoftEther*). |

(1) **CSTP framing 8-byte** [`CstpFraming`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpFraming.cs#L19): header `STF(0x53,0x54,0x46)·0x01·length(2 BE)·type(1)·0x00`; `Encode(type,payload)`/`Decode(frame)` + reassembler instance `Append`+`TryReadPacket` ráp gói qua mọi ranh đọc TLS; magic sai ⇒ `FormatException`. status ≠200 ⇒ `UnauthorizedAccessException`. **(V5.b data plane)** [`CstpChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpChannel.cs#L24) = `IPacketChannel` CSTP-over-TLS bọc `IByteStreamTransport` + `CstpFraming`: `WriteIpPacketAsync` đóng khung DATA → ghi (serialise qua semaphore), `RunReceiveLoopAsync` đọc stream→`Append`/`TryReadPacket` demux (DATA/COMPRESSED→`InboundIpPacket`, DPD-REQ→event reply, DISCONNECT/TERMINATE→`PeerClosed`), event `PacketSent`/`PacketReceived`/`DpdRequestReceived` cho driver bơm timer;
