[`CstpDpdState`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpDpdState.cs#L17) DPD/keepalive **clock-inject** (như `OpenVpnKeepalive`/`WireGuardPeerState`): `ShouldSendDpd`/`IsPeerDead` (theo `X-CSTP-DPD`, dead-window 2×) + `ShouldSendKeepalive` (theo `X-CSTP-Keepalive`). **(V5.d rekey)** [`OpenConnectRekeyMethod`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/Enums/OpenConnectRekeyMethod.cs#L9) (None/Ssl/NewTunnel) + `OpenConnectTunnelInfo.ParsedRekeyMethod` (parse `X-CSTP-Rekey-Method`, None khi `none`/unknown/period≤0) + [`CstpRekeyState`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpRekeyState.cs#L18) **clock-inject** (`ShouldRekey`/`OnRekeyDone` theo `X-CSTP-Rekey-Time`, cùng shape `CstpDpdState`); driver wire thành re-establish make-before-break (§6 *Drivers.OpenConnect*). **Pure protocol, mã hóa do TLS lo.** DTLS data path = V5.c (dùng **Transport.Dtls** F.3 — xem bảng dưới). |
| **Transport.Dtls** *(F.3)* | [DtlsDatagramTransport.cs:28](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsDatagramTransport.cs#L28), [OpenConnectDtls12PskClient.cs:21](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/OpenConnectDtls12PskClient.cs#L21), [DtlsPskParameters.cs:13](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsPskParameters.cs#L13), [DefaultDtlsClient.cs:26](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DefaultDtlsClient.cs#L26), [DtlsResumptionParameters.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsResumptionParameters.cs#L14), [DtlsCipherSuiteMap.cs:16](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsCipherSuiteMap.cs#L16), [BouncyCastleDatagramBridge.cs:19](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/BouncyCastleDatagramBridge.cs#L19), [DtlsServerCertificateValidationCallback.cs:15](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsServerCertificateValidationCallback.cs#L15) | **DTLS 1.2 datagram transport (F.3 xong)** — concrete [`IDatagramTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IDatagramTransport.cs#L9) qua **BouncyCastle** (`Org.BouncyCastle.Tls.DtlsClientProtocol`); `SslStream` BCL **không** làm DTLS nên BouncyCastle dùng **cả 2 TFM** (`netstandard2.0`+`net8.0`). [`DtlsDatagramTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsDatagramTransport.cs#L28) bọc một inner `IDatagramTransport` (UDP plaintext): `ConnectAsync` chạy handshake DTLS 1.2 client (full: pin `ProtocolVersion.DTLSv12`, chào AEAD ECDHE/DHE-RSA+ECDSA+RSA-KT AES-GCM trong [`DefaultDtlsClient`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DefaultDtlsClient.cs#L26)), sau đó `SendAsync`/`ReceiveAsync` = 1 DTLS record mã hóa/giải mã (giữ ranh giới datagram giống UDP — drop-in thay UDP thô); phơi `SendLimit`/`ReceiveLimit`; `DisposeAsync` gửi close_notify. **Resume legacy AnyConnect (V5.c live):** khi truyền [`DtlsResumptionParameters`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsResumptionParameters.cs#L14) (master secret 48B + session id + cipher — đem in-band qua TLS CONNECT), `DefaultDtlsClient` dựng `TlsSession` (`TlsUtilities.ImportSession`) + `GetSessionToResume` + **`AllowLegacyResumption=true`** (session không EMS; thiếu ⇒ BouncyCastle **xóa** session_id ⇒ ocserv `invalid session ID size`) → chào **handshake rút gọn** ClientHello mang session_id ocserv chờ, DTLS 1.2→1.0, cipher CBC; [`DtlsCipherSuiteMap`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsCipherSuiteMap.cs#L16) map tên `X-DTLS-CipherSuite` (CBC legacy resolve = tín hiệu resume; AEAD/GCM ⇒ full handshake). Cert server validate/pin qua tùy chọn [`DtlsServerCertificateValidationCallback`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsServerCertificateValidationCallback.cs#L15) (null⇒accept all; reject⇒`TlsFatalAlert`); client **anonymous** (không cert client). Record layer BouncyCastle **đồng bộ** → cầu sync↔async [`BouncyCastleDatagramBridge`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/BouncyCastleDatagramBridge.cs#L19) (vòng nền pull inbound vào `BlockingCollection`; `Receive(...,waitMillis)` timeout⇒`-1` cho retransmit timer DTLS; `Send` đồng bộ), handshake + mỗi send/receive offload `Task.Run`; chịu **1 sender + 1 receiver** đồng thời (như socket thô). **Refs CHỈ Abstractions** + PackageReference `BouncyCastle.Cryptography` 2.4.0 (không điều kiện). **Consumer:** OpenConnect V5.c (đã wire). Test offline dựng **server DTLS giả lập** (`DtlsServerProtocol` + cert RSA self-signed, full handshake) qua loopback datagram in-memory: handshake + round-trip 2 chiều + cert-callback + reject-cert-abort + **record loss** (drop flight⇒retransmit) + **reorder**. **DTLS 1.2 PSK hiện đại (`PSK-NEGOTIATE`) — đường ưu tiên, VALIDATE LIVE ✅ ocserv 1.2.4:** khi truyền [`DtlsPskParameters`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsPskParameters.cs#L13) (PSK identity `"psk"`, PSK key 32B từ RFC 5705 EKM của CSTP TLS, session_id = `X-DTLS-App-ID`), [`OpenConnectDtls12PskClient`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/OpenConnectDtls12PskClient.cs#L21) (`PskTlsClient`) chạy **full DTLS 1.2 PSK handshake** (suite `TLS_PSK_WITH_AES_256/128_GCM`) — KHÔNG legacy resumption ⇒ né hẳn bug interop; ép `ClientHello.session_id` = App-ID qua `TlsUtilities.ImportSession` (session throwaway dummy-master/DTLSv12/no-EMS + `AllowLegacyResumption`). PSK thắng resumption khi cả hai có. Test offline self-pair vs BouncyCastle `PskTlsServer` (`SimulatedDtlsPskServer`: handshake + echo + reject wrong-key). **Resume legacy lộ qua validate live ocserv** (session_id ĐÚNG; handshake rút gọn residual — nay đã thay bằng PSK, bảng "Khác biệt"). |

| **Ppp** | [PppEngine.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/PppEngine.cs#L14) trên [IPppFrameChannel.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Interfaces/IPppFrameChannel.cs#L7); negotiate [PppNegotiator.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/PppNegotiator.cs#L11) (base) → [LcpNegotiator.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/LcpNegotiator.cs#L10)/[IpcpNegotiator.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/IpcpNegotiator.cs#L12)/[Ipv6cpNegotiator.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Ipv6cpNegotiator.cs#L14); auth [IPppAuthenticator.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Interfaces/IPppAuthenticator.cs#L9) → [MsChapV2Authenticator.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Auth/MsChapV2Authenticator.cs#L12) (codec [MsChapV2.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/MsChapV2.cs#L11) ở Crypto, dùng chung với IKEv2 EAP); framing [HdlcFramer.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Framing/HdlcFramer.cs#L7)/[HdlcDecoder.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Framing/HdlcDecoder.cs#L7) | Engine chạy **LCP → MS-CHAPv2 → IPCP** (demux theo protocol field dưới 1 lock), event `LinkUp`/`AuthSucceeded`/`AuthFailed`. LCP chỉ chấp nhận MS-CHAPv2 (0xC223+0x81), reject auth khác; IPCP xin IP 0.0.0.0+DNS, nhận qua Configure-Nak; `MsChapV2Authenticator` là nơi `DeriveHlak()` (cho crypto binding SSTP). **IPV6CP (RFC 5072) opt-in** (`enableIpv6`): `Ipv6cpNegotiator` thương lượng Interface-Identifier → link-local `fe80::/64`, chạy song song IPCP + event `Ipv6Up`/`AssignedAddressV6`, **không** đổi link-up IPv4 (mặc định tắt); **nay đã wire vào 2 driver SSTP/L2TP** (opt-in `enableIpv6`) → `TunnelConfig.AssignedAddressV6` (P1.1). Data plane **multiplex hai họ trên một `IPacketChannel`**: `SendIpAsync` chọn PPP Protocol theo version nibble (0x0021 IPv4 / 0x0057 IPv6), inbound demux `Ip`+`Ipv6` cùng đổ về [PppPacketChannel.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/PppPacketChannel.cs#L10) để `TcpIpStack` dual-stack tách lại. Có sẵn **chế độ server** (assignPeer*) — chỉ dùng cho loopback test. HDLC chỉ dùng cho đường SSTP. **Global IPv6 over PPP (P1.1, namespace `Ipv6/`)**: sau IPV6CP (link-local), [`PppIpv6Autoconfigurator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Ipv6/PppIpv6Autoconfigurator.cs#L20) (impl [`IPppIpv6Autoconfigurator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Ipv6/IPppIpv6Autoconfigurator.cs#L15)) gửi Router Solicitation, nhận RA (SLAAC) hoặc DHCPv6 trên kênh PPP để suy địa chỉ **global** = prefix ‖ IID (IID = 64 bit thấp của link-local IPV6CP); best-effort (không RA ⇒ null, giữ link-local). Tái dùng engine NDISC/SLAAC/DHCPv6 của Ethernet (`NdiscResolver`/`Ipv6AddressConfigurator`) qua adapter [`PppEthernetChannelAdapter`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Ipv6/PppEthernetChannelAdapter.cs#L26) (trình diễn `IPacketChannel` L3 thành `IEthernetChannel`: gửi bỏ 14 byte Ethernet header → `WriteIpPacketAsync`, nhận IPv6 thuần → raise `InboundFrame`; MAC tổng hợp chỉ cosmetic) + option [`Ipv6AddressConfiguratorOptions.InterfaceIdentifierOverride`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/Ipv6AddressConfiguratorOptions.cs#L28) (SLAAC dùng IID của link thay vì EUI-64 từ MAC). **Ppp nay ref Ethernet** (acyclic — Ethernet chỉ ref Abstractions). |
| **IpStack** | [TcpIpStack.cs:19](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs#L19), [TcpConnection.cs:28](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L28), [TcpRetransmitOptions.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpRetransmitOptions.cs#L14), [UdpConnection.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Udp/UdpConnection.cs#L12); codec [Ipv4.cs:6](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Ipv4.cs#L6)/[Ipv4Reassembler.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Ipv4Reassembler.cs#L12)/[Ipv6.cs](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Ipv6.cs)/[Ipv6Reassembler.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Ipv6Reassembler.cs#L12)/[IpLayer.cs](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/IpLayer.cs)/[TcpSegment.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpSegment.cs#L7)/[UdpDatagram.cs:6](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/UdpDatagram.cs#L6)/[Icmpv4.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Icmpv4.cs#L7)/[Icmpv6.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Icmpv6.cs#L7), [TcpState.cs:4](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/Enums/TcpState.cs#L4) | TCP/IP userspace **dual-stack**: demux inbound theo **version-nibble** (4→IPv4 / 6→IPv6) rồi protocol→port (cấp ephemeral port từ **49152**, chung TCP+UDP, chung 2 họ), **sau khi ráp lại gói phân mảnh** (IPv4 [`Ipv4Reassembler.Offer` @ :38](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Ipv4Reassembler.cs#L38) RFC 791 §3.2; IPv6 Fragment-header [`Ipv6Reassembler.Offer` @ :38](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Ipv6Reassembler.cs#L38) RFC 8200 §4.5; cả 2 buffer theo (src,dst,id) + timeout + bound chống DoS). TCP active-open **FSM đầy đủ** (Closed/SynSent/Established/FinWait1/FinWait2/Closing/TimeWait/CloseWait/LastAck): MSS **suy từ link MTU** (`IPacketChannel.Mtu`−40, mặc định **1360**, clamp theo MSS peer quảng bá), **window scaling RFC 7323** (cửa sổ nhận hiệu lực ≈256 KB + scale cửa sổ peer khi negotiated), receive window field **65535**, ACK tích lũy, RST→IOException. **Phía gửi tin cậy** ([TrySendData @ :413](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L413)): retx queue + retransmit theo **RTO RFC 6298** ([OnRtoTimer @ :594](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L594), RTT SRTT/RTTVAR + ×2 backoff + give-up cap → fault) + **sliding-window flow control** (tôn trọng cửa sổ peer, [ProcessAck @ :438](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L438)) + **zero-window persist** ([OnPersistTimer @ :651](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L651)). **Phía nhận** reassembly out-of-order ([ReceiveData @ :304](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L304)); **half-close FSM đầy đủ** + TIME-WAIT linger ([AdvanceClose @ :370](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L370)); tunable [`TcpRetransmitOptions`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpRetransmitOptions.cs); terminal (graceful CLOSED / RST / hết retry) → event `Closed` ⇒ stack gỡ khỏi `_connections` + dispose. **Congestion control NewReno** (cwnd/slow-start/fast-retransmit, RFC 5681/6582) trên nền flow control. **SACK (RFC 2018/6675)** đàm phán SACK-Permitted (cả 2 bên) → phía nhận sinh SACK blocks từ out-of-order, phía gửi retransmit **chọn lọc đúng hố** (`RetransmitHoles`) + pipe-fill `(_sndNxt−_sndUna)−sacked` (`InFlight`); không SACK → fallback NewReno. Tự tính checksum ([InternetChecksum.cs:6](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/InternetChecksum.cs#L6)). **Chiều gửi**: chokepoint [`SendIp` @ :156](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs#L156) tự **phân mảnh** datagram > `IPacketChannel.Mtu` ([`Ipv4.Fragment` @ :85](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Ipv4.cs#L85), RFC 791 §2.3, cắt trên ranh 8 byte) thay vì gửi nguyên với DF rồi bị drop — đối xứng reassembly inbound; MSS TCP suy từ link MTU (clamp theo MSS peer). **PMTUD động (RFC 1191/8201)**: segment TCP đi ra với cờ DF → router path nhỏ hơn trả **ICMP Fragmentation-Needed (type 3/code 4)** / **ICMPv6 Packet-Too-Big (type 2)**; [`TcpIpStack.DeliverPathMtu` @ :354](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs#L354) trích source-port+sequence của segment được quote → định tuyến về connection → [`TcpConnection.OnIcmpPacketTooBig` @ :333](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L333) **hạ MSS** (chỉ giảm, sàn 576/1280) + [`ResegmentRetxQueue` @ :694](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L694) chẻ retx queue in-flight thành mảnh vừa path + retransmit (phá black-hole). Chỉ TCP (UDP/ICMP không retx). **ICMP (RFC 792)** nay được xử lý: [`OnIcmp`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs) tự trả lời Echo Request, [`PingAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs) gửi Echo Request + chờ Echo Reply (match identifier/sequence) → [`PingReply`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/PingReply.cs); Destination Unreachable trích đúng Echo Request đã gửi ⇒ [`IcmpUnreachableException`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/IcmpUnreachableException.cs). Gói tới **local port không có socket** nay tự sinh phản hồi (cả 2 họ): TCP → **RST** ([`SendTcpReset` @ :368](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs#L368), RFC 793 p.36), UDP → **ICMP/ICMPv6 port-unreachable** ([`SendPortUnreachableV4` @ :404](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs#L404) / [`SendPortUnreachableV6` @ :416](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs#L416), RFC 1122 §3.2.2.1 / RFC 4443 §3.1). **Dual-stack**: TCP/UDP chạy y hệt trên IPv4 lẫn IPv6 — chỉ lớp IP bọc ([`IpLayer.Build`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/IpLayer.cs)) + pseudo-header checksum ([`InternetChecksum.PseudoHeaderSum`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/InternetChecksum.cs)) khác theo họ; ICMPv6 echo/dest-unreachable + Fragment-header reassembly + fragmentation. App-facing: [`SendAsync` @ :236](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L236) (cạnh `Send` fire-and-forget) thêm **backpressure** (giới hạn buffer chưa-gửi theo `SendBufferHighWaterMark`) + **propagate fault** (`IOException` khi RST/give-up) cho `VpnNetworkStream` (P0.3). **Chưa** ND/SLAAC (point-to-point L3 không cần — thuộc tầng L2). |
| **Ethernet** *(L2.0–L2.9)* | [MacAddress.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/MacAddress.cs#L9), [EthernetFrame.cs:8](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetFrame.cs#L8), [EthernetSwitch.cs:16](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetSwitch.cs#L16) (+ [SwitchPort.cs](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetSwitch.SwitchPort.cs) base / [Port.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetSwitch.Port.cs#L14) host / [UplinkPort.cs](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetSwitch.UplinkPort.cs) uplink), [VirtualHost.cs:23](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/VirtualHost.cs#L23), [ArpResolver.cs:26](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/ArpResolver.cs#L26), [NdiscResolver.cs:31](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/NdiscResolver.cs#L31), [DhcpV4Configurator.cs:30](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/DhcpV4Configurator.cs#L30), [Ipv6AddressConfigurator.cs:34](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/Ipv6AddressConfigurator.cs#L34), [EthernetAdapter.cs:24](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetAdapter.cs#L24), [MultiHostSession.cs:25](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/MultiHostSession.cs#L25); slot [INeighborResolver.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/Interfaces/INeighborResolver.cs#L12)/[IAddressConfigurator.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/Interfaces/IAddressConfigurator.cs#L11) | **Nền tầng L2**: (L2.0) codec khung Ethernet II 14 byte (`EthernetFrame.Build` + readers; EtherType IPv4 `0x0800`/IPv6 `0x86DD`/ARP `0x0806`) + `MacAddress` 48-bit (ulong-backed: parse/format, cờ broadcast/multicast/ipv6-mcast `33:33`, key FDB) — đối xứng codec `Ipv4`/`Ipv6`. (L2.1) **`EthernetSwitch`** học MAC in-memory: hai loại port dưới base `SwitchPort` — `ConnectHost(mac)→IEthernetChannel` (host `Port` switch sở hữu) và **`ConnectUplink(IEthernetChannel)→UplinkPortHandle`** (uplink port bọc kênh VPN ngoài: switch forward ra → `uplink.WriteFrameAsync`, `uplink.InboundFrame` → ingress vào switch — **đường gắn data-plane đa-host**, switch không sở hữu kênh). FDB `Dictionary<MacAddress,SwitchPort>` học src-MAC→port + forward (unicast-đã-học đi 1 port; broadcast/multicast/unknown-unicast **flood** port khác; không phản xạ ingress; MAC-move + disconnect purge FDB) — quyết định dưới lock, deliver ngoài lock (IEEE 802.1D §7, **không** STP/aging/VLAN/snooping). 2 **slot** `INeighborResolver` (ARP/NDISC) + `IAddressConfigurator` (trả `TunnelConfig`) khai báo ở Abstractions bằng **raw bytes/`IPAddress`** (tránh phụ thuộc vòng). (L2.2) **`VirtualHost`** = cầu nối L2↔L3 (`: IPacketChannel`): giữ MAC + port switch + resolver, **expose `IPacketChannel`** cho `TcpIpStack` — egress resolve dest-MAC qua `INeighborResolver` rồi wrap Ethernet → switch; ingress strip header → `InboundIpPacket` (khung non-IP/ARP → event `InboundNonIpFrame` seam cho L2.3); `Mtu=link−14` (kẹp MSS), `Medium=Ip`, resolve header L3 bằng offset cố định (không ref project IpStack — giữ no-horizontal-dep §2). (L2.3) **`ArpResolver`** hiện thực `INeighborResolver` IPv4 (RFC 826, codec `ArpPacket` 28 byte): egress resolve next-hop IP→MAC (cache + request/reply + timeout/retry + coalesce), học mọi gói ARP, **trả lời** request hỏi IP của ta; nhận khung ARP inbound qua seam `VirtualHost.InboundNonIpFrame`. (L2.4) **`NdiscResolver`** `INeighborResolver` IPv6 (RFC 4861, codec `Icmpv6Ndisc`, mirror ARP): NS-to-solicited-node/NA + học LLA + trả NA + **DAD** + **parse RA → `RouterAdvertisementInfo`** (gateway+prefix); ride trong IPv6 nên nối cả `InboundIpPacket` lẫn `InboundNonIpFrame`. (L2.5) **`DhcpV4Configurator`** `IAddressConfigurator` IPv4 (RFC 2131, codec `DhcpV4Packet`/`DhcpV4Options`): DISCOVER→OFFER→REQUEST→ACK qua broadcast UDP 68→67 → `TunnelConfig` (IP/prefix/route/DNS). (L2.6) **`Ipv6AddressConfigurator`** `IAddressConfigurator` IPv6 (RFC 4862 SLAAC + RFC 8415 DHCPv6, codec `Dhcpv6Packet`/`Dhcpv6Options` + helper `SlaacAddress`): chọn theo RA (do L2.4 parse) — **SLAAC** (prefix autonomous /64 → địa chỉ global EUI-64/opaque RFC 7217) + **DHCPv6 stateful** (cờ M/O/force → SOLICIT→ADVERTISE→REQUEST→REPLY qua UDP 546→547 tới `ff02::1:2`) → `TunnelConfig` v6 (`AssignedAddressV6`/prefix/route `::/0`/DNS); gửi RS tới `ff02::2` đợi RA. Tự dựng IPv4/IPv6+UDP + ICMPv6 (checksum pseudo-header RFC 768/791/8200) — **không** ref `IpStack`. (L2.7) **`EthernetAdapter`** ráp `EthernetSwitch` + N×`VirtualHost` + backpressure thành LAN userspace multi-host; `ConnectUplink(IEthernetChannel)` gắn uplink VPN vào switch như một port (data-plane đa-host). (L2.8) **`MultiHostSession`** phơi N station = N `EthernetHostSession` (`: IVpnSession`) trên adapter (mỗi station MAC/IP/`IPacketChannel`/`TunnelConfig` riêng, DHCP/SLAAC lease qua `AddStationAsync`) + năng lực driver tap/SoftEther khai báo `L2Ethernet`/`L2BroadcastDomain`/`SupportsMultiHost`. `ArpResolver.SetLocalAddress` cập nhật địa chỉ sau DHCP (station gắn trước khi lease). (L2.9) **composite dual-stack** `DualStackNeighborResolver` (route ARP/NDISC theo `AddressFamily`) + `DualStackAddressConfigurator` (merge DHCPv4 + SLAAC/DHCPv6 vào một `TunnelConfig`) để **một** host nói cả 2 họ — chốt tầng L2 với test multi-host dual-stack offline. **Cố ý lược bỏ**: VLAN 802.1Q/FCS/padding (codec); FDB aging/STP/snooping (switch); routing/gateway on-link; proxy/gratuitous ARP; NUD (NDISC); lease renew T1/T2 + DECLINE/RELEASE + Rapid-Commit/IA_PD + privacy-ext RFC 8981 (DHCPv6/SLAAC). **Data-plane đa-host đã có** (`ConnectUplink` + `MultiHostSession`); tiêu thụ bởi SoftEther + OpenVPN-tap (opt-in `multiHost`). |
| **Ipsec.Nat** | [NatTraversalChannel.cs:13](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Nat/NatTraversalChannel.cs#L13), [NatTraversal.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Nat/NatTraversal.cs#L9) (enum [NatTPacketKind](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Nat/Enums/NatTPacketKind.cs#L4), hằng `IkePort=500`/`NatTPort=4500`/`MarkerLength=4`) | NAT-T (RFC 3948): 1 UDP socket. **Bind local port ephemeral (≠500/4500)** để gateway coi client là NATed → **forced-NAT-T** (xem §8). Trên port 500 phân loại bằng độ dài ≥28 (ISAKMP header), không marker. *(Gom từ project cũ `TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Udp`; namespace `TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec.Nat`.)* |
| **Sockets** | [VpnTcpClient.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Sockets/VpnTcpClient.cs#L9), [VpnUdpClient.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Sockets/VpnUdpClient.cs#L11), [VpnNetworkStream.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Sockets/VpnNetworkStream.cs#L7) | API socket trên tunnel: TCP trả `Stream` (cắm `HttpClient`) — `VpnNetworkStream` no-seek, `WriteAsync`/`FlushAsync` qua [`TcpConnection.SendAsync` @ :236](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L236) (**backpressure** theo cửa sổ peer + ném `IOException` khi connection fault — P0.3, thay đường `Send` fire-and-forget cũ), `Dispose` phát **half-close** (FIN). Phần **IKEv2-riêng giữ trong driver, cố ý ngoài supervisor** (rekey làm tươi SA in-place, **không** re-establish): DPD keepalive (INFORMATIONAL rỗng + ack peer), rekey CHILD_SA make-before-break (timer ~90%×1h + watermark sequence 2³² → `SwapSession` + grace drop + DELETE §2.8) **và rekey IKE SA** (`RekeyIkeSaAsync` timer ~90%×8h: SPI/DH mới + swing SK_* + DELETE §2.18, data plane không đổi; chung guard `_rekeyInProgress`) — chạy trên timer riêng, `StopAttemptLoop` dispose timer + tắt `_espActive`; chỉ drop thật (DPD timeout / server DELETE) gọi `OnLinkLost` của base. `OnReconnected` raise `Reconnected(Ikev2ReconnectInfo)`; `DisconnectAsync` override gửi DELETE IKE SA trước teardown base. **Logging Q.2**: ctor nhận `ILoggerFactory?` (null⇒no-op) → handshake (IKE_SA_INIT/IKE_AUTH)/DPD/rekey/state/link-lost/reconnect. **Refs**: Abstractions + **Drivers.Core** + Ipsec (tái dùng `NatTraversalChannel` chung L2TP + `IkeClient` F.7 + `EspTunnelChannel` F.8 + codec `MsChapV2` Crypto). **1 CHILD_SA/1 IP ảo** (`OpenSessionAsync`⇒`NotSupported`); auth client PSK\|EAP, **auth responder PSK\|cert** (cấu hình [`IkeCertificateTrust`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Models/IkeCertificateTrust.cs#L11) qua ctor `Ikev2Driver` / `UseIkev2(trust)` → gửi CERTREQ, verify CERT + chữ ký AUTH bằng [`IkeSignatureAuth`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/IkeSignatureAuth.cs#L15), fail⇒`VpnServerRejectedException`; capability +`Certificate`); **multi-traffic-selector** opt-in (nhiều subnet TSi/TSr) + forced NAT-T. **Validate live cần lab Q.1** — test offline phủ capabilities/guard + responder-cert/multi-TS self-interop ([`IkeCertAuthHandshakeTests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec.Ike.Tests/IkeCertAuthHandshakeTests.cs)) + toán protocol ở Ipsec.Ike/Esp.Tests. |

Vòng đời: keepalive **ping/ping-restart** (`OpenVpnKeepalive` + `OpenVpnPing.Magic`; drop ping inbound ở device-link) trong timer riêng (`StopAttemptLoop` dispose timer + tắt `_dataActive`), rekey = **re-establish** khi `OpenVpnDataPlane.RekeyNeeded` (~2³² packet-id, tránh tái dùng nonce GCM) gọi `OnLinkLost` của base, teardown (`DisconnectAsync` override gửi **explicit-exit-notify** `EXIT_NOTIFY` best-effort + time-box 2s trước `DisconnectCoreAsync`), supervisor/auto-reconnect (gom về base, không còn `_lifetimeCts`/`ReconnectLoopAsync`/`WithJitter`/`SetState` chép riêng). `OnReconnected` raise `Reconnected(OpenVpnReconnectInfo)`. **SỬA crash reconnect-window**: data-plane sink đọc `_transport` **hiện tại** + bỏ qua khi đang reconnect (`!_dataActive`) + nuốt `ObjectDisposedException`/`SocketException` ([sink @ OpenVpnConnection.cs:273](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenVpn/OpenVpnConnection.cs#L273)) — trước đây một RTO retransmit của TCP-stack bắn vào socket vừa dispose ⇒ unhandled trong timer ⇒ sập process; [`OpenVpnSocketTransportFactory.UdpDatagramSocket`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnSocketTransportFactory.cs#L48) giữ ref `Socket` (tránh `UdpClient.Client` null khi dispose đua) + tắt `SIO_UDP_CONNRESET` trên Windows (ICMP port-unreachable không còn làm receive/send sau đó ném `ConnectionReset`). **Logging Q.2**: ctor nhận `ILoggerFactory?` (null⇒no-op) → handshake (reset/TLS/key-method-2/PUSH)/keepalive/rekey/state/link-lost/reconnect (test offline `OpenVpnLoggingTests.cs`). **Refs**: Abstractions + **Drivers.Core** + OpenVpn + Ethernet (fabric L2 cho tap) + **Transport.Tcp** (TCP trần proto-tcp, F.1). tun + tap-1-host: **1 IP ảo** (`OpenSessionAsync`⇒`NotSupported`); **tap multi-host** (`multiHost: true`): N station = N `IVpnSession`, thêm qua `OpenSessionAsync`. tap IPv4/ARP (pure-DHCP đã có); **client-cert PEM auto-load + explicit-exit-notify + NCP-less fallback cipher (AEAD + AES-CBC non-AEAD) + P_DATA_V1/V2 đã có (V.2-occ)**; half-duplex theo [`SoftEtherConnectionDirectionPlanner`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherConnectionDirectionPlanner.cs#L19)) → cùng path mang **data session** [`SoftEtherEthernetChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherEthernetChannel.cs#L19) (V4.c, egress `mux.SendBlockAsync` + ingress `mux.InboundFrame → channel.Deliver`) → **2 chế độ** (helper `EstablishSingleHostAsync`/`EstablishMultiHostAsync`): (mặc định) bridge-1-host **DHCP lease** [`DhcpV4Configurator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/DhcpV4Configurator.cs#L29) (L2.5, SecureNAT cấp IP) → [`ArpResolver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/ArpResolver.cs#L26) (L2.3) + [`VirtualHost`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/VirtualHost.cs#L23) (L2.2); (opt-in `multiHost: true`) data channel gắn vào [`EthernetAdapter.ConnectUplink`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetAdapter.cs#L62) như uplink port + [`MultiHostSession`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/MultiHostSession.cs#L25), station thêm qua `OpenSessionAsync` (mỗi station DHCP lease riêng) → `IPacketChannel` qua [`SwappablePacketChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/SwappablePacketChannel.cs#L14). **IPv6 trong tunnel (opt-in `enableIpv6`, V.4-ipv6)**: link-local `fe80::/64`+EUI-64(MAC) ([`SlaacAddress`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/Helpers/SlaacAddress.cs#L13)) → ngoài ARP/DHCPv4 còn dựng [`NdiscResolver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/NdiscResolver.cs#L31) (L2.4) + [`Ipv6AddressConfigurator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/Ipv6AddressConfigurator.cs#L34) (L2.6) trên cùng channel, gom qua [`DualStackNeighborResolver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/DualStackNeighborResolver.cs#L24)/[`DualStackAddressConfigurator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/DualStackAddressConfigurator.cs#L22) (L2.9), `ConfigureIpv6BestEffortAsync` chạy RS→RA→SLAAC (+ DHCPv6 DNS/stateful) đẩy `AssignedAddressV6`/`PrefixLengthV6`/DNS/route `::/0` lên `TunnelConfig` — **best-effort** (server IPv4-only ⇒ bỏ leg v6, IPv4 vẫn chạy); **mặc định tắt** giữ wire IPv4-only. **use_compress/use_encrypt (V.4)**: khi `login.Session.UseCompress` ⇒ `SoftEtherEthernetChannel` nén/giải-nén frame DEFLATE; khi `login.Session.UseEncrypt` ⇒ bọc mỗi connection trong [`SoftEtherEncryptedTransport.CreateClient`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherEncryptedTransport.cs#L40) (RC4 per-direction, khóa từ `welcome.SessionKey`) sau handshake (handshake HTTP/PACK chạy plaintext); cả hai **mặc định tắt** (`SoftEtherSessionParams.UseEncrypt`/`UseCompress` mặc định `false` — payload thô trên TLS). Vòng đời: keep-alive timer (chuỗi `"Internet Connection Keep Alive Packet"`), stream đóng/fault → supervisor/auto-reconnect (mirror OpenVPN/WireGuard). **Refs**: Abstractions + Crypto + SoftEther + Ethernet. **1 IP ảo bridge-1-host** mặc định (`OpenSessionAsync`⇒`NotSupported`); **multi-host** (`multiHost: true`): N station = N `IVpnSession` qua `OpenSessionAsync`; **IPv6 tunnel opt-in `enableIpv6` đã xong** (V.4-ipv6); **còn lại: watermark blob THẬT (GPL) + validate live (Q.1)** — server SoftEther thật từ chối placeholder (403). **Refs**: Abstractions + Crypto + SoftEther + Ethernet + **Transport.Tls** (TLS dùng chung, F.1). Test offline qua **server SecureNAT giả lập** (control + DHCP server + ARP responder + IP echo; multi-connection N-socket round-trip không mất gói + half-duplex; **+3 test** use_encrypt/use_compress/cả-hai; **+3 test IPv6** 1-host SLAAC+DHCPv6-DNS+round-trip v4/v6 qua NDISC thật / IPv4-only-server vẫn Connected không-v6 / multi-host station v4+v6). |

Data plane: COM push qua [`NETWORK_CREDENTIALS`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Vl2/NetworkCredentialsCodec.cs) (sau join + ERROR code-6); EXT_FRAME tới đúng tap MAC node (node nhận). **Data-plane VL2 ICMP live = còn lại**: controller ERROR `NEED_MEMBERSHIP_CERTIFICATE` — COM trích từ dict `C` controller 1.4.6 chưa được chấp nhận (serialize COM 1.4.6 khác docs `dev`); **2 member zerotier-one thật ping nhau OK** (lab+MAC fix đúng — residual ở COM exchange phía client). |

**tap (ether)** → [`VtunEthernetChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Vtun/DataChannel/VtunEthernetChannel.cs) (`IEthernetChannel` L2, payload = Ethernet frame trần) + `ArpResolver` + `VirtualHost` (tái dùng Ethernet fabric) bind bridge L2↔L3 (stack vẫn thấy IP trần); inbound route qua `_deliverData` delegate theo mode; frame length-prefix (encrypt trước/decrypt sau frame) → `Facade.SetInner` → `MarkConnected`; receive loop (data→channel, `ECHO_REQ`→`ECHO_REP`, `CONN_CLOSE`/EOF→link-loss) + keepalive timer (`ECHO_REQ` idle). [`VtunDriver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Vtun/VtunDriver.cs#L21) (`Name="vtun"`, caps **L3Ip**/Tcp/Security=None/Auth=PreSharedKey/OutOfBand) + [`VpnClientBuilder.UseVtun`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs). **Refs**: Abstractions + Drivers.Core + Vtun + Transport.Tcp. **1 IVpnSession** (`OpenSessionAsync`⇒`NotSupported`). **VALIDATE LIVE FULL-TUNNEL ICMP 2 chiều ✓** (lab [`vtun`](../lab/vtun), **vtund 3.0.4** thật, host `test` type tun/tcp/encrypt no/compress no, `10.11.0.1`↔`10.11.0.2`): server log `Use SSL-aware challenge/response`+`Session test opened`+`tun0` bound; client **4/4 ICMP echo reply** RTT~0.4ms; reject path live (sai password → `Denied connection`/`VpnAuthenticationException`). tcpdump: khối auth 50-byte + frame data 62-byte + control echo 2-byte. **0 bug** — golden vector OpenSSL Blowfish khoá offline ⇒ đúng ngay lần đầu. **DATA-PLANE ENCRYPT VALIDATE LIVE ✓** (host `enc` `encrypt blowfish128ecb`, vtund chạy `OPENSSL_CONF=openssl-legacy.cnf`): flags Encrypt+Tcp+Tun (E1) → "data-plane encryption enabled: Blowfish128Ecb" → server `Blowfish-128-ECB encryption initialized` → **ICMP 4/4 2 chiều**; tcpdump tcp/5002 data frame **length 66 = 2-byte header + 64-byte CIPHERTEXT** (ICMP 60B pad→64), 0 chuỗi plaintext "ICMP", 0 `0040 4500` (IP header trong frame) ⇒ mã hóa hoàn toàn. 1 blocker MÔI TRƯỜNG: OpenSSL 3.0 ẩn Blowfish trong legacy provider (fix = `OPENSSL_CONF`). **TAP MODE (type ether) VALIDATE LIVE ✓**: host `tapsrv` → flags Tcp+KeepAlive+Ether → `VtunEthernetChannel`+ArpResolver+VirtualHost → **ICMP 4/4 2 chiều**; server `tapsrv ether tap0`; MTU 1436 (1450−14); tcpdump data frame `length 76` (2-byte header + 74-byte Ethernet frame) + 2 ARP frame (ethertype 0806) → bridge L2↔L3 đúng. Demo `vtun://pass@host/test?addr=&peer=`. Còn lại: cipher khác BF128ECB (CBC/CFB/OFB+AES) + compression + UDP. |
