- ✅ **WireGuard** (`SecurityKind=Noise`, `AddressAssignment=OutOfBand`, UDP) nay có driver [`Drivers.WireGuard`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.WireGuard) (V3.f) — config tĩnh (single hoặc **multi-peer**) → tunnel L3 chạy thật (handshake initiator mỗi peer + data type-4 + keepalive + rekey make-before-break per-peer + supervisor/reconnect), **crypto-routing** longest-prefix chọn peer theo địa chỉ đích (`WireGuardCryptoRouter`/`WireGuardMultiPeerChannel`, V.3), **per-peer endpoint** (mỗi peer transport UDP tới endpoint của chính nó; peer cùng endpoint chia sẻ 1 socket — de-dup theo `IPEndPoint`), `VpnClientBuilder.UseWireGuard`. Còn lại: validate live (Q.1) + roaming endpoint.
- ✅ **SoftEther PACK codec (V4.a)** — project mới [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther): framing nhị phân typed key-value nền của **mọi** control/RPC SoftEther, re-implement từ spec [`07`](07-softether.md) (**không copy GPL** `Pack.c`/`Pack.h`). [`Pack`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/Pack.cs#L17) = list [`PackElement`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackElement.cs#L12){`Name`≤63, [`PackValueType`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/Enums/PackValueType.cs#L8) (`Int`=0/`Data`=1/`Str`=2/`UniStr`=3/`Int64`=4), mảng [`PackValue`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackValue.cs#L11) ≥1}; codec **big-endian** [`ToBytes`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/Pack.cs#L147)/[`Parse`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/Pack.cs#L160) thuần (**không I/O**) qua [`PackBufferWriter`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackBufferWriter.cs#L11)/[`PackBufferReader`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackBufferReader.cs#L12): `uint32(num_elements)` → mỗi element `BufStr(name)·type·num_value·value[]`; **BufStr** prefix `len+1` không-NUL (quirk), **STR** prefix đúng-len Latin-1, **UNISTR** prefix `utf8len+1` + utf8 + **1 NUL**, INT/INT64 BE 4/8B, DATA `len`+bytes. Helper `Set*`/`Get*` theo tên (single + `Set*Array` đa-value) + tra cứu case-insensitive; input lỗi ⇒ `FormatException`. Test offline [`SoftEther.Tests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther.Tests) (**25 test PACK**: round-trip mọi kiểu + đa-value array + tên dài 63 + bool + empty + case-insensitive + **byte-layout đối chiếu PACK dựng tay** (single-int/STR-no-+1/UNISTR-+1-trailing-NUL/INT64-BE) + **PACK hello/login mẫu** (hello/version/build/random + login với `secure_password`=SHA-0 qua `Sha0`) + reject underrun/đếm-vượt/trùng-tên).
- ✅ **SoftEther control handshake (V4.b)** — cùng project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther), **tách phần codec/state thuần khỏi I/O socket** (test offline qua server giả lập in-memory), nay **ref** [`Abstractions`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions) (seam [`IByteStreamTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IByteStreamTransport.cs) F.1) + [`Crypto`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto) (SHA-0). Luồng [`SoftEtherHandshake.RunAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L177): (1) **watermark POST** [`SoftEtherWatermark.BuildRequest`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherWatermark.cs#L73) `POST /vpnsvc/connect.cgi HTTP/1.1` + headers + thân `signature‖padding` (signature là **placeholder byte-exact reproducible** [`DefaultSignature`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherWatermark.cs#L27) — **KHÔNG** copy blob GPL `Watermark.c`; server thật truyền blob qua `WithSignature`); (2) đọc hello PACK [`ParseHello`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L41) (`hello`/`version`/`build`/`random` 20B challenge); (3) dựng/gửi login PACK [`BuildLoginPack`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L68) `method=login`/`hubname`/`username`/`authtype` + **`secure_password`** [`SoftEtherAuth.ComputeSecurePassword`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherAuth.cs#L76) = `SHA0(SHA0(password‖UPPER(username))‖random)` (tái dùng [`Sha0`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Sha0.cs) qua `IHashAlgo` — **password gốc không qua wire**) + session params (`max_connection`/`use_encrypt`/`use_compress`/`half_connection`/`unique_id`) ([`SoftEtherSessionParams`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Models/SoftEtherSessionParams.cs#L11)); (4) đọc welcome [`ParseWelcome`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L110) → `error`≠0 ⇒ [`SoftEtherProtocolException`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherProtocolException.cs#L9)(ErrorCode), else `session_name`/`session_key_32`. PACK đi trong thân HTTP qua [`SoftEtherHttpPackCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHttpPackCodec.cs#L15) (`uint32 len` + PACK; build POST/200 + parse). Test offline (**+17 test** `SoftEtherHandshakeTests.cs`).
- ✅ **SoftEther data plane Ethernet-over-TLS + driver L2 (V4.c)** — data plane ở project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther) (`DataChannel/`): codec block thuần [`SoftEtherDataFrameCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherDataFrameCodec.cs#L13) (`uint32(num_frames)` + mỗi frame `uint32(size)·bytes`, `EncodeBlock`/`EncodeSingle`/`DecodeBlock`/`IsKeepAlive`) + reader streaming [`SoftEtherDataBlockReader`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherDataBlockReader.cs#L16) (ráp 1 block qua partial read; EOF ranh block ⇒ rỗng) + [`SoftEtherEthernetChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherEthernetChannel.cs#L19) (`IEthernetChannel`: `WriteFrameAsync` encode block ra sink / `Deliver` raise `InboundFrame`, drop keep-alive). **Driver L2 thật đầu tiên** [`Drivers.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.SoftEther) (V4.c) ráp end-to-end: TLS byte-stream ([`TlsByteStream`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Tls/TlsByteStream.cs#L25) chung **F.1** sau seam [`ISoftEtherTransportFactory`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.SoftEther/Transport/ISoftEtherTransportFactory.cs#L13)) → `SoftEtherHandshake.RunAsync` (V4.b) → data session → **DHCP lease** [`DhcpV4Configurator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/DhcpV4Configurator.cs#L29) (SecureNAT) → bridge L2↔L3 [`ArpResolver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/ArpResolver.cs#L26) + [`VirtualHost`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/VirtualHost.cs#L23) → `IPacketChannel`; keep-alive + supervisor reconnect qua base [`ReconnectingVpnConnection<SoftEtherConnectionState>`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Core/ReconnectingVpnConnection.cs#L24) dùng chung (F.6 — `EstablishAsync`/`CleanupAttemptResourcesAsync`/`StopAttemptLoop` dispose keep-alive timer + `OnReconnected` raise `Reconnected(SoftEtherReconnectInfo)`; `SoftEtherReconnectOptions : VpnReconnectOptions`). `VpnClientBuilder.UseSoftEther(hubName)`. **Multi-host opt-in** (`multiHost: true`): data channel gắn uplink-as-port vào `EthernetAdapter` + `MultiHostSession`, primary station + `OpenSessionAsync` thêm station (mỗi station DHCP lease riêng). **IPv6 trong tunnel opt-in `enableIpv6` (V.4-ipv6)**: ngoài ARP/DHCPv4, bridge dựng `NdiscResolver` (L2.4) + `Ipv6AddressConfigurator` (L2.6) qua `DualStackNeighborResolver`/`DualStackAddressConfigurator` (L2.9) trên cùng channel SecureNAT, link-local `fe80::/64`+EUI-64 (`SlaacAddress`), `ConfigureIpv6BestEffortAsync` chạy SLAAC/DHCPv6 đẩy `AssignedAddressV6`/`PrefixLengthV6` lên `TunnelConfig` — best-effort (server IPv4-only vẫn kết nối), mặc định tắt; cả 1-host lẫn multi-host (dual-stack station). `AssignedAddressV6`/`IsIpv6Enabled` + overload `UseSoftEther(hub, enableIpv6)`. Test offline (**+23 test**: `SoftEtherConnectionTests` end-to-end qua server SecureNAT giả lập — control + DHCP server + ARP responder + IP echo + 2 test multi-host + 3 test use_encrypt/use_compress + **3 test IPv6** (1-host SLAAC+DHCPv6-DNS+round-trip v4/v6 qua NDISC thật / IPv4-only-server vẫn Connected không-v6 / multi-host station v4+v6) — và `SoftEtherDataFrameCodecTests`). **Còn lại**: validate live (Q.1).
- ✅ **OpenVPN VALIDATE LIVE RỘNG với server tự host (V.2, 2026-06-24)** — lab [`openvpn`](../lab/openvpn) (OpenVPN 2.6 community server Docker, PKI openssl, `.ovpn` inline, 2 container bridge; biến `PROTO`/`DEV`/`CIPHER` đổi giữa lần): **(1) tun UDP + NCP AES-256-GCM (P_DATA_V2)** — client HARD_RESET→TLS→key-method-2 (peer-info IV_CIPHERS)→PUSH_REPLY `cipher AES-256-GCM`; server log `Peer Connection Initiated` + `Data Channel: cipher 'AES-256-GCM', peer-id: 0` + `protocol-flags cc-exit` (explicit-exit-notify); HTTP nhỏ + UDP DNS (`[✓]`) + ICMP RTT 1ms + EXIT_NOTIFY teardown. **(2) tun TCP** (16-bit framing [`OpenVpnTcpFraming`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnTcpFraming.cs#L15)) — HTTP 4/4 + gói lớn 64KB 2/2; server `TCPv4_SERVER … bound`. **(3) gói lớn ~64KB** cả UDP + TCP carrier (`Received 65536 bytes`) — **Q.4 không tái hiện** trên download. **(4) tap server-bridge** ([`OpenVpnTapChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnTapChannel.cs#L15)→`ArpResolver`→`VirtualHost`) — `tap bridge bound on 10.60.0.50` + ICMP gateway RTT 1ms qua ARP/Ethernet 2 chiều (lab tự bring-up tap0 + gán GW vì `server-bridge` không tự cấp IP tap0). **SHARED IpStack [`TcpConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs) — Q.4 ĐÃ SỬA + VALIDATE LIVE ✓**: triệu chứng HTTP **upload** stall "1 byte/segment" (sender-side SWS) đã sửa (xem bảng "Khác biệt"); re-validate live qua lab này — POST 10 MB qua tunnel (UDP carrier) ⇒ HTTP 200 + `received 10485760 bytes`, tcpdump tun0 ≈99% segment đầy/gần-đầy MSS, **0 segment 1-byte**. **Còn lại (chưa kiểm live)**: tap IPv6 pool / tap pure-DHCP & multi-host với server thật / OCC strict. Không sửa code (driver đã đúng) — chỉ thêm lab + docs. (xem [`11`](11-todo-roadmap.md) §V.2 + bảng "Khác biệt").
- ✅ **OpenVPN tap-mode IPv6 trong tunnel (V.2-ipv6)** — **mirror y hệt SoftEther V.4-ipv6**, nhánh L2 của P1.1(2) (PPP/L3 đã xong cho SSTP/L2TP). Opt-in [`enableIpv6`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenVpn/OpenVpnConnection.cs#L137) trên [`OpenVpnConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenVpn/OpenVpnConnection.cs#L41)/[`OpenVpnDriver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenVpn/OpenVpnDriver.cs#L45) (mặc định tắt, **không đổi hành vi cũ**; chỉ tap-mode — tun-mode bỏ qua). Test offline (**+3 test** [`OpenVpnConnectionTapIpv6Tests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenVpn.Tests/OpenVpnConnectionTapIpv6Tests.cs): server tap giả lập phát RA autonomous /64 + DHCPv6-DNS + NA — 1-host SLAAC ra địa chỉ global prefix‖EUI-64 /64 + DNS v6 + route `::/0` / IPv4-only-bridge không-RA vẫn Connected không-v6 / multi-host primary static-v4 + SLAAC v6). **Còn lại**: validate live OpenVPN `server-bridge` tap + IPv6 pool (Q.1).
- ✅ **SoftEther multi-connection (V.4)** — 1–32 TCP/TLS song song = 1 session logic. Protocol-level (project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther)): [`ParseWelcome`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L110) nay đọc `max_connection` (server clamp theo policy hub) + `half_connection` → [`SoftEtherWelcomeInfo`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Models/SoftEtherWelcomeInfo.cs#L9); codec [`BuildAdditionalConnectPack`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L140)/[`ParseAdditionalConnectReply`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L155) + driver I/O [`RunAdditionalConnectAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L209) (watermark→hello→`method=additional_connect`+`session_name`(session key)→ack, server `GetSessionFromKey` gắn socket vào session đã login); [`SoftEtherMultiConnectionMux`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherMultiConnectionMux.cs#L26) gộp N transport thành 1 data path — egress block **round-robin** các connection gửi-được ([`SendBlockAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherMultiConnectionMux.cs#L97)), ingress **1 decode loop/connection** ([`SoftEtherDataBlockReader`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherDataBlockReader.cs#L16) reuse) gộp `InboundFrame` (frame self-contained ⇒ reassemble = hợp mọi connection, thứ tự trong-1-connection giữ nguyên), fault/peer-close ⇒ `linkLost` **một lần** (one-shot guard); [`SoftEtherConnectionDirectionPlanner`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherConnectionDirectionPlanner.cs#L19) chia hướng theo [`SoftEtherConnectionDirection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/Enums/SoftEtherConnectionDirection.cs#L9) (full-duplex ⇒ mọi `Both`; **half_connection** ⇒ nửa `Send`-only + nửa `Receive`-only, ≥1 mỗi hướng, 1 connection thì luôn `Both`). Driver [`Drivers.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.SoftEther): sau login lấy `welcome.MaxConnection`, mở `min(login.MaxConnection, granted, 32)−1` connection phụ ([`OpenAdditionalConnectionsAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.SoftEther/SoftEtherConnection.cs)), gắn `SoftEtherEthernetChannel` lên mux (egress `mux.SendBlockAsync` + `mux.InboundFrame += channel.Deliver`), keep-alive đi qua mux; connection phụ fail = best-effort (log + chạy tiếp với số connection đã gắn); `ConnectionCount` phơi số connection. Test offline: protocol **+14 test** (`SoftEtherMultiConnectionTests` — codec additional_connect, welcome max/half, planner, mux round-robin/merge-ingress/half-duplex/link-lost-once) + driver **+4 test** (`SoftEtherMultiConnectionTests` qua `SoftEtherMultiConnectionServer` giả lập N-connection: 4-connection round-trip 40 gói không mất, clamp về số server cấp, single-connection vẫn chạy, half-duplex chia hướng vẫn 2 chiều). **Còn lại**: IPv6 tunnel, validate live (Q.1).
- ✅ **SoftEther payload codec use_compress/use_encrypt (V.4)** — protocol-level (project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther), `DataChannel/`). **use_compress**: [`SoftEtherPayloadCompressor`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherPayloadCompressor.cs#L23) nén **per-frame** bằng DEFLATE (`System.IO.Compression.DeflateStream`, RFC 1951, cả 2 TFM) **trước** khi block-encode; frame nén mang prefix magic `0xDEADBEEFCAFEFACE` (doc [`07`](07-softether.md) §"Multi-host & multi-connection") + chỉ gửi nén khi nhỏ hơn (frame không nén được giữ thô → receiver phân biệt qua magic); giải nén ở [`DecompressFrame`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherPayloadCompressor.cs#L55) (inflate vượt `MaxFrameSize`/stream hỏng ⇒ `FormatException`). Hook vào [`SoftEtherEthernetChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherEthernetChannel.cs#L19) qua cờ ctor `useCompress` (`WriteFrameAsync` nén / `Deliver` giải-nén) — codec block + reader **giữ nguyên**. **use_encrypt**: [`SoftEtherEncryptedTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherEncryptedTransport.cs#L22) decorator `IByteStreamTransport` áp RC4 keystream **liên tục per-direction** (dưới block framing — đúng behavior SoftEther, RC4 nằm dưới framing), **tái dùng** [`Rc4`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Rc4.cs) (F.5b); 2 keystream độc lập (RC4 order-sensitive) suy từ session key + nhãn hướng 1 byte qua [`DeriveDirectionKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherEncryptedTransport.cs#L61) (`CreateClient`/`CreateServer` mirror nhau). Thứ tự egress **compress-rồi-encrypt** (ciphertext không nén được). Driver [`Drivers.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.SoftEther) wire theo `login.Session.UseCompress`/`UseEncrypt` (RC4 bọc connection sau handshake plaintext, dùng `welcome.SessionKey`). **Mặc định tắt** ([`SoftEtherSessionParams.UseEncrypt`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Models/SoftEtherSessionParams.cs#L24)/`UseCompress` mặc định `false`) — payload thô trên TLS, không vỡ test cũ; RC4 broken (RFC 7465) chỉ để interop legacy trên TLS. Test offline: protocol **+9 test** (`SoftEtherPayloadCodecTests` — compressor nén/raw-passthrough/corrupt + RC4 mirror 2 chiều/ciphertext≠plaintext + block round-trip 4 tổ hợp) + driver **+3 test** (`SoftEtherConnectionTests.Connect_WithEncryptAndCompress_RoundTripsIp` end-to-end qua server giả lập mirror RC4+DEFLATE). **Còn lại**: validate live (Q.1) — watermark/PACK/SecureNAT thật.

- ✅ **OpenConnect/AnyConnect codec (V5.a)** — project mới [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect) (PROTOCOL-layer, ngang WireGuard/SoftEther; chỉ ref `Abstractions`): **CSTP framing 8-byte** [`CstpFraming`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpFraming.cs#L19) (header `STF·0x01·length(2 BE)·type·0x00`, `Encode`/`Decode` + reassembler `Append`/`TryReadPacket` qua mọi ranh đọc TLS, magic hỏng ⇒ `FormatException`; [`CstpPacketType`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/Enums/CstpPacketType.cs#L9) DATA/DPD-REQ/DPD-RESP/DISCONNECT/KEEPALIVE/COMPRESSED/TERMINATE — hiện thực OpenConnect của **seam F.2 `IPacketEncapsulator`**); **HTTP auth ocserv** [`OpenConnectAuthCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/OpenConnectAuthCodec.cs#L14) (XML `<config-auth>` init/auth-reply + parse `<form><input/>` → [`OpenConnectAuthForm`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/Models/OpenConnectAuthForm.cs#L11) + `IsSuccess` + `ExtractCookie` `webvpn=`); **HTTP CONNECT** [`OpenConnectConnectCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/OpenConnectConnectCodec.cs#L17) (`CONNECT /CSCOSSLC/tunnel` + parse `X-CSTP-*` → [`OpenConnectTunnelInfo`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/Models/OpenConnectTunnelInfo.cs#L14) → `TunnelConfig`, non-200 ⇒ `UnauthorizedAccessException`). **Pure codec, không I/O** (re-implement từ draft-mavrogiannopoulos-openconnect + ocserv, **không copy GPL**).
- ✅ **OpenConnect data plane + driver (V5.b, TLS-only)** — protocol-level (project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect)): [`CstpChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpChannel.cs#L24) = `IPacketChannel` CSTP-over-TLS bọc `IByteStreamTransport`+`CstpFraming` (DATA framing/demux + DPD-REQ→event reply + DISCONNECT/TERMINATE→`PeerClosed` + event `PacketSent`/`PacketReceived` bơm timer); [`OpenConnectHttpTransactor`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/OpenConnectHttpTransactor.cs#L18) chạy auth POST + CONNECT **byte-exact** (header tới CRLFCRLF rồi đúng `Content-Length`, **không nuốt** gói CSTP đầu sau CONNECT 200); [`CstpDpdState`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpDpdState.cs#L17) DPD/keepalive **clock-inject** (`ShouldSendDpd`/`IsPeerDead` theo `X-CSTP-DPD` dead-window 2× + `ShouldSendKeepalive` theo `X-CSTP-Keepalive`, như `OpenVpnKeepalive`/`WireGuardPeerState`). - ✅ **DTLS 1.2 datagram transport (F.3)** — project mới [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls) (tầng TRANSPORT, ngang [`Transport.Tls`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Tls)/`TlsByteStream` F.1; chỉ ref `Abstractions` + PackageReference `BouncyCastle.Cryptography` 2.4.0 **không điều kiện cả 2 TFM**): concrete [`IDatagramTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IDatagramTransport.cs#L9) qua **BouncyCastle** (`Org.BouncyCastle.Tls.DtlsClientProtocol`) — `SslStream` BCL **không** làm DTLS trên `net8.0` lẫn `netstandard2.0`. [`DtlsDatagramTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsDatagramTransport.cs#L28) bọc một inner `IDatagramTransport` (UDP plaintext): `ConnectAsync` chạy handshake DTLS 1.2 client (full: pin `ProtocolVersion.DTLSv12`, chào AEAD ECDHE/DHE-RSA+ECDSA+RSA-KT AES-GCM ở [`DefaultDtlsClient`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DefaultDtlsClient.cs#L26)) rồi `SendAsync`/`ReceiveAsync` = 1 DTLS record mã hóa/giải mã (giữ ranh giới datagram — drop-in thay UDP thô), phơi `SendLimit`/`ReceiveLimit`, `DisposeAsync` gửi close_notify. **Resume legacy AnyConnect (V5.c — code, lộ qua validate live):** [`DtlsResumptionParameters`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsResumptionParameters.cs#L14) (master secret 48B + session id + cipher đem in-band qua TLS CONNECT) ⇒ `DefaultDtlsClient` dựng `TlsSession` (`TlsUtilities.ImportSession`) + `GetSessionToResume` + **`AllowLegacyResumption=true`** (session không EMS) → chào handshake rút gọn ClientHello mang session_id ocserv chờ (DTLS 1.2→1.0, cipher CBC `AES256-SHA`); [`DtlsCipherSuiteMap`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsCipherSuiteMap.cs#L16) map tên `X-DTLS-CipherSuite` (CBC=resume; AEAD=full). Cert server validate/pin qua tùy chọn [`DtlsServerCertificateValidationCallback`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsServerCertificateValidationCallback.cs#L15) (null⇒accept all; reject⇒`TlsFatalAlert`); client **anonymous**. Record layer BouncyCastle **đồng bộ** → cầu sync↔async [`BouncyCastleDatagramBridge`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/BouncyCastleDatagramBridge.cs#L19) (vòng nền pull inbound vào `BlockingCollection`; `Receive(...,waitMillis)` timeout⇒`-1` cho retransmit timer DTLS; `Send` đồng bộ), handshake + mỗi send/receive offload `Task.Run`, chịu **1 sender + 1 receiver** đồng thời. **Consumer:** OpenConnect V5.c (đã wire — bullet dưới). Test offline (**+7 test** [`Transport.Dtls.Tests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls.Tests)) dựng **server DTLS giả lập** (`DtlsServerProtocol` + cert RSA self-signed, full handshake) qua loopback datagram in-memory: handshake xong, round-trip 2 chiều nhiều datagram, cert-callback quan sát đúng cert server, reject-cert ⇒ abort handshake, **record loss** (drop flight đầu ⇒ DTLS retransmit ⇒ vẫn xong) + **reorder** (đảo 2 datagram đầu server ⇒ vẫn xong). **Chỉ DTLS 1.2** full handshake (DTLS 1.3 chưa chào). **Resume legacy lộ qua validate live ocserv** (session_id ĐÃ ĐÚNG; handshake rút gọn còn residual — bảng "Khác biệt").
- ✅ **OpenConnect DTLS data path song song + fallback TLS (V5.c)** — protocol-level (project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect)): [`CstpDatagramFraming`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpDatagramFraming.cs#L13) (framing CSTP cho DTLS = header **1-byte type**, **không** STF magic/length — 1 datagram = 1 gói, `Encode`/`Decode`, đối xứng `CstpFraming` 8-byte của đường TLS) + [`CstpDatagramChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpDatagramChannel.cs#L19) (`IPacketChannel` CSTP-over-DTLS bọc `IDatagramTransport`+`CstpDatagramFraming`: `WriteIpPacketAsync` đóng khung DATA, `RunReceiveLoopAsync` đọc datagram→demux DATA/DPD/DISCONNECT, raise **cùng event** `DpdRequestReceived`/`PeerClosed`/`PacketReceived`/`PacketSent` như `CstpChannel` để dùng chung `CstpDpdState`). - ✅ **OpenConnect rekey X-CSTP-Rekey-Method (V5.d)** — protocol-level (project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect)): enum [`OpenConnectRekeyMethod`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/Enums/OpenConnectRekeyMethod.cs#L9) (None/Ssl/NewTunnel) + `OpenConnectTunnelInfo.ParsedRekeyMethod` (parse `X-CSTP-Rekey-Method`, None khi `none`/unknown/`X-CSTP-Rekey-Time`≤0) + [`CstpRekeyState`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpRekeyState.cs#L18) timer **clock-inject** (`ShouldRekey`/`OnRekeyDone` theo `X-CSTP-Rekey-Time`, cùng shape `CstpDpdState`). Driver [`Drivers.OpenConnect`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect): `OpenConnectConnection` (`partial`) arm `CstpRekeyState` ở `EstablishAsync`; timer loop `TimerTickAsync` `ShouldRekey` ⇒ [`RekeyAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect/OpenConnectConnection.cs#L554) **re-establish make-before-break**: `BuildCstpChannelAsync` (helper không-chạm-field) dựng tunnel mới (auth + CONNECT + `CstpChannel` + tùy chọn DTLS) vào biến cục bộ **trong khi** tunnel cũ vẫn chở traffic, rồi swap `Facade.SetInner` + field + token receive-loop mới (`_recvCts` rotate, cancel được loop cũ độc lập), cuối mới tear-down tunnel cũ (detach event ⇒ EOF cũ không gọi `OnLinkLost` → DISCONNECT → cancel/await loop cũ → dispose). `RekeyCount`/`Rekeyed`; guard `_rekeyInProgress` chống chạy chồng (và không bao giờ overlap reconnect). **Cả `new-tunnel` lẫn `ssl` đều re-establish**: `SslStream` net8/ns2.0 **không** lộ TLS-renegotiation phía client (chỉ net9+ `ExportKeyingMaterial`/renegotiate) ⇒ `ssl` là fallback re-establish (ghi chú ở `OpenConnectRekeyMethod`). Rekey lỗi (`MaybeRekeyAsync` catch) ⇒ **giữ tunnel hiện tại** + re-arm; DPD/keepalive + supervisor lo session chết thật. IP stack không re-bind ⇒ tunnel **không rớt** khi rekey. **VALIDATE LIVE ✓** (2026-06-24, lab [`openconnect`](../lab/openconnect) ocserv `rekey-time` ngắn + `rekey-method new-tunnel`): client log `CSTP rekey (NewTunnel) due` → `rekey complete (#1)` địa chỉ mới `10.70.0.195`; server thấy **2 session login chồng** (tunnel mới TRƯỚC khi cũ disconnect) ⇒ make-before-break đúng. Test offline (**+3 test** [`Drivers.OpenConnect.Tests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect.Tests/OpenConnectRekeyTests.cs) + harness `MultiAttemptOpenConnectFactory` dựng server mới mỗi connect, clock-inject): rekey kích hoạt đúng `X-CSTP-Rekey-Time` (`new-tunnel`) ⇒ re-establish (attempts≥2) + swap sang tunnel mới (đổi địa chỉ `10.10.0.9`) + round-trip qua tunnel mới + state vẫn `Connected`; `ssl` cũng re-establish; **không advertise Rekey-Time ⇒ không rekey** (RekeyCount=0); **+4 test** [`OpenConnect.Tests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect.Tests/CstpRekeyStateTests.cs) (`CstpRekeyStateTests` — `ParsedRekeyMethod` map method/period (theory), `ShouldRekey` đúng-sau-period + `OnRekeyDone` re-arm + None-method disabled; +1 assert `ParsedRekeyMethod=Ssl` ở `OpenConnectConnectCodecTests`).
- ✅ **MPPE + RC4 crypto legacy (F.5b — nền PPTP V.6)** — trong project [`Crypto`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto): [`Rc4`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Rc4.cs#L13) (stream cipher KSA/PRGA, `Process`/`GenerateKeystream`/`Apply`) + [`MppeKeyDerivation`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Mppe/MppeKeyDerivation.cs#L18) (RFC 3078 §7.3 `GetNewKeyFromSha` = `SHA1(StartKey‖40×0x00‖SessionKey‖40×0xF2)`, **initial key SHA-only** RFC 3079 §3.1 + **re-key SHA→`RC4(InterimKey, InterimKey)`** RFC 3078, strength reduction 40→`0xD1 0x26 0x9E`/56→`0xD1`/128 nguyên) + [`MppeSession`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Mppe/MppeSession.cs#L16) (1 chiều: RC4 state + coherency count 12-bit + framing header A(flush)/B/C/D(encrypt) RFC 3078 §3.1, `Encrypt`/`Decrypt`; **stateless** = re-key + FLUSHED mỗi gói, **stateful** = re-key mỗi 256 gói khi low-octet coherency=0xFF). MPPE start key suy từ MS-CHAPv2 qua [`MsChapV2.DeriveMppeMasterKey`/`DeriveMppeSendStartKey`/`DeriveMppeReceiveStartKey`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/MsChapV2.cs#L156) — **tái dùng `GetMasterKey`/`GetAsymmetricStartKey` sẵn có**, thêm cờ `isServer` chọn Magic2/Magic3 (client-send=server-receive=Magic2; client-receive=server-send=Magic3). **CẢNH BÁO BẢO MẬT: MPPE + MS-CHAPv2 đã bị phá hoàn toàn** (RC4 RFC 7465, MS-CHAPv2 brute-force DES) — chỉ tương thích PPTP legacy. **Chưa wire driver** (CCP negotiator + GRE data plane ở V.6.a). KAT offline: RC4 RFC 6229 (40/128-bit keystream) + classic Rivest; MPPE RFC 3079 §3.5 (MasterKey `FDECE371…`/StartKey `8B7CDC14…`/SessionKey 40/56/128) + "Sample Encrypted Message" `rc4(SessionKey,"test message")` (byte cuối 56-bit §3.5.2 là erratum RFC, giá trị thật `…57B8`); session round-trip stateless/stateful qua 600 gói.
- ✅ **PPTP control plane + CCP/MPPE negotiate (V6.a, offline)** — project mới [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp) (PROTOCOL-layer, ngang OpenConnect/WireGuard; ref `Abstractions`+`Crypto`+`Ppp`): **control codec TCP/1723** [`PptpControlCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/PptpControlCodec.cs#L22) (header chung 12-byte `Length·MsgType·MagicCookie 0x1A2B3C4D·CtrlMsgType·Reserved0` + body big-endian/ASCII NUL-pad cho mọi message RFC 2637 §2.x: SCCRQ/SCCRP/OCRQ/OCRP/Echo/Set-Link-Info/Call-Clear/CDN/Stop-CC; `Encode`/`Decode` + reassembler `Append`/`TryReadMessage` qua mọi ranh đọc TCP, magic/length sai ⇒ `FormatException`); **state machine** [`PptpControlConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/PptpControlConnection.cs#L22) (PNS/client trên `IByteStreamTransport`: SCCRQ→SCCRP → OCRQ→OCRP ghi `PeerCallId`=GRE Call-ID → Echo keep-alive (auto-reply) + Set-Link-Info → Call-Clear→CDN + Stop-CC; refuse ⇒ `InvalidOperationException`); **CCP/MPPE** [`CcpNegotiator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/CcpNegotiator.cs#L22) **kế thừa [`PppNegotiator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/PppNegotiator.cs#L11) dùng chung** (RFC 1962): offer option MPPE đơn (RFC 2118/3078 type 18), `OnNak` adopt + `EvaluatePeerRequest` cap về cường độ tối đa + pin 1 bit, `OnReject`⇒`NotSupportedException`; [`MppeConfigOption`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/MppeConfigOption.cs#L19) codec 4-byte supported-bits ↔ [`MppeKeyStrength`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Mppe/Enums/MppeKeyStrength.cs)/stateless; [`MppeSessionFactory`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/MppeSessionFactory.cs#L20) ráp cặp [`MppeSession`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Mppe/MppeSession.cs#L16) (F.5b) từ MS-CHAPv2 (`DeriveMppeMasterKey`/asymmetric Send-Receive start key RFC 3079) + kết quả CCP. **Thêm `PppProtocol.Ccp`=0x80FD/`Compressed`=0x00FD** ở Ppp. **MS-CHAPv2+MPPE/RC4 đã bị phá — chỉ tương thích legacy.** Test offline (**+31 test** `Pptp.Tests`): codec round-trip mọi control message + đúng kích thước wire (156/168/32/16/20/24/148B) + reject magic/length sai + reassembler split-5-byte qua 3 gói; state machine end-to-end qua PAC giả lập (establish→call→echo→clear→stop) + refuse-control/refuse-call; CCP negotiate 128-bit/Nak-down-to-40 + multi-bit→Nak-strongest + unknown-option→reject + reject-MPPE→`NotSupportedException`; `MppeConfigOption` codec BE + strength→bit; `MppeSessionFactory` interop encrypt/decrypt 2 chiều 40/56/128-bit + stateless 5 gói.
- ✅ **PPTP GRE + MPPE data plane (V6.b, offline)** — bổ sung [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp): **GRE codec** [`PptpGreCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Gre/PptpGreCodec.cs#L21)/[`PptpGrePacket`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Gre/PptpGrePacket.cs#L11) (Enhanced GRE RFC 2637 §4.1: version 1, Key high word=payload length/low word=Call ID, Sequence/Acknowledgment tùy chọn — codec thuần Encode/TryDecode) + **kênh data plane** [`PptpGreChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Gre/PptpGreChannel.cs#L21) (`IPppFrameChannel` trên `IDatagramTransport` proto-47: lọc theo `localCallId`, sequence tăng + ack piggyback §4.4, receive-loop identity-guard + dispose-to-unblock kiểu native-ESP, strip/re-prepend HDLC `FF 03`) + **decorator MPPE** [`MppePppFrameChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/MppePppFrameChannel.cs#L23) (chạy CCP nội bộ giữa `PppEngine` ↔ GRE; LCP plaintext, còn lại mã hóa `MppeSession` thành proto 0x00FD khi CCP Opened). **OFFLINE only — driver runtime + validate live chờ F.9 raw-IP** (elevate). Test offline (`Pptp.Tests`): GRE codec round-trip plain/+seq/+ack + reject wrong-version/magic; channel cặp 2 đầu qua loopback `IDatagramTransport` trao đổi PPP frame + drop wrong-Call-ID + sequence/ack piggyback; MPPE decorator CCP-opened encrypt↔decrypt.

[`PptpDriver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Pptp/PptpDriver.cs) (`IVpnProtocolDriver` Name=`pptp`, Caps Tcp+RawIp/Mppe/UserPassword/RequiresElevation) + [`VpnClientBuilder.UsePptp`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs). **Thêm [`MppeSessionFactory.CreateServerSessions`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/MppeSessionFactory.cs)** (đối xứng `CreateClientSessions`, RFC 3079 `isServer:true`) cho vai server/test. **OFFLINE code+test; validate live (poptop/accel-ppp Docker, elevate) chờ Q.1. MS-CHAPv2+MPPE/RC4 đã bị phá — chỉ tương thích legacy.** Test offline (**+5 test** `Drivers.Pptp.Tests`, không socket thật): control handshake qua PAC giả lập sinh đúng Local/Peer Call-ID; client GRE-wrap LCP Configure-Request đầu tiên với `PeerCallId` tới được server-end (decode `PptpGreCodec`); frame server→client tới được kênh GRE client; khóa MPPE client↔server round-trip 2 chiều (`CreateClientSessions`/`CreateServerSessions`); refuse control-connection ⇒ connect fail; caps driver. **Defer Q.1**: MS-CHAPv2 server-auth đầy đủ + CCP/MPPE Opened end-to-end + IPCP→`Connected` (lib chưa có server-side PPP MS-CHAPv2).

header byte0 `C R0 K S s Recur(3)`, byte1 `Reserved0(5) Version(3)`=0, ProtocolType(2); thứ tự field tùy chọn **Checksum(2)+Reserved1(2) → Key(4) → Sequence(4)**; validate Version==0/bounds/checksum-zero, **leniency** bỏ qua Reserved0/routing/recursion) + [`GreTunnelChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap/Gre/GreTunnelChannel.cs#L22) (ctor `(IDatagramTransport, GreTunnelOptions?, ILogger?)`; `Start()` + identity-guard + dispose-to-unblock như [`PptpGreChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Gre/PptpGreChannel.cs#L21) / native-ESP loop). **KHÁC PPTP Enhanced GRE** (v1, key=payload-len+call-id) — codec riêng **không** tái dùng [`PptpGreCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Gre/PptpGreCodec.cs#L21). **IPIP** (proto-4, RFC 2003 — IPv4-in-IPv4) + **SIT/6in4** (proto-41, RFC 4213 — IPv6-in-IPv4): **một** [`RawIpPassthroughChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap/RawIpPassthroughChannel.cs#L21) header-less dùng chung (outbound gửi gói IP verbatim làm datagram; inbound raise payload verbatim; family-agnostic — proto-number do caller chọn lúc tạo transport). Thêm hằng [`RawIpProtocols.IpIp=4`/`.Sit=41`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.RawIp/RawIpProtocols.cs#L4) cho caller (kênh **không** ref Transport.RawIp). **Refs**: chỉ Abstractions (`ILogger`/`NullLogger` qua transitive). **OFFLINE codec+kênh+test; driver (b) + EtherIP(proto-97)/L2TPv3(proto-115) + validate live (c, cần IP public) chờ Q.1.** ⚠️ TRẦN không mã hóa — chỉ mạng tin cậy hoặc kèm IPsec ESP. Test offline (**+14 test** [`IpEncap.Tests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap.Tests), không socket thật): [`GreCodecTests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap.Tests/GreCodecTests.cs) (round-trip plain/+Key/+Seq/+Checksum/combined + thứ tự byte chính xác + v4/v6 proto-type + malformed version≠0/truncated/bad-checksum + leniency Reserved0), [`GreTunnelChannelTests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap.Tests/GreTunnelChannelTests.cs) (cặp kênh qua loopback `IDatagramTransport`: inner v4/v6 round-trip **byte-for-byte** + garbage dropped), [`RawIpPassthroughChannelTests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap.Tests/RawIpPassthroughChannelTests.cs) (v4/v6 verbatim). Build xanh cả `netstandard2.0` + `net8.0`.

- ✅ **tinc 1.1 SPTPS protocol (V.7.2 phase a — code + test offline + VALIDATE LIVE handshake & record layer vs tincd 1.1pre18 THẬT)** — project mới [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc) (PROTOCOL-layer, ngang Nebula/WireGuard; ref **chỉ `Crypto`**). [`SptpsHandshake`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc/Sptps/SptpsHandshake.cs#L20) drive KEX→SIG→derive ([`SptpsEcdh`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc/Sptps/SptpsEcdh.cs#L33) ECDH có khóa Ed25519 + [`Ed25519Signer`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/Ed25519Signer.cs#L15) — KHÔNG viết lại crypto); transcript `fill_msg(flag‖kex0‖kex1‖label)`, KDF seed `"key expansion"‖init_nonce‖resp_nonce‖label`. [`SptpsEcdh`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc/Sptps/SptpsEcdh.cs#L33) = **ECDH có khóa Ed25519** (KEX public = Ed25519 Edwards, shared = X25519 ladder trên `montgomeryX=(1+y)/(1−y)`, scalar `clamp(SHA512(seed))`; orlp `ecdh.c`/`key_exchange.c` — KHÔNG X25519 thuần). [`SptpsPrf`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc/Sptps/SptpsPrf.cs#L29) = **TLS-1.0 P_hash XOR-fold** HMAC-SHA-512 (`prf_xor`: inner `A[n]=HMAC(secret,A[n-1]‖seed)` + outer `block=HMAC(secret,A[n]‖seed)`, output `^=` block — KHÔNG TLS-1.2 copy). [`TincChaChaPoly1305`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc/Sptps/TincChaChaPoly1305.cs#L21) = record cipher biến thể tinc (nonce seqno 8B BE djb, poly key=keystream block0, tag-on-ciphertext — **KHÁC RFC 8439**, trên BouncyCastle `ChaChaEngine`+`Poly1305`). Record layer [`SptpsRecordLayer`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc/Sptps/SptpsRecordLayer.cs#L14) (TCP stream, **seqno đếm CẢ handshake record** → record mã hóa đầu = seqno 2) + [`SptpsDatagramRecordLayer`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc/Sptps/SptpsDatagramRecordLayer.cs#L16) (UDP data + [`AntiReplayWindow`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/AntiReplayWindow.cs#L8)) + KEX codec + [`TincMetaRequest`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc/Meta/TincMetaRequest.cs#L13) + [`TincBase64`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc/Hosts/TincBase64.cs#L15) (base64 LE phi chuẩn tinc) + [`TincHostConfig`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc/Hosts/TincHostConfig.cs#L11). 35 test offline (handshake self-interop + crossed keys, cipher round-trip/tamper/replay, framing, **KAT ChaCha20 djb + Poly1305 chuẩn**, **+5 KAT interop golden từ live**). **VALIDATE LIVE (2026-06-24, Docker VM)**: harness initiator → `tincd` (SPTPS-only) ⇒ **`server SIG VERIFIED`** + client **giải mã đúng record meta đầu** server gửi (ACK `4 655 N 0x700000c`); lab [`lab/tinc`](../lab/tinc) build tinc 1.1pre18 từ source. **4 bug interop self-pair-offline-KHÔNG-bắt sửa qua live**: (1) [`TincBase64`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc/Hosts/TincBase64.cs#L15) base64 LE phi chuẩn (KHÁC RFC 4648 → tincd decode pubkey khác → `Failed to verify SIG`), (2) [`SptpsEcdh`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc/Sptps/SptpsEcdh.cs#L33) Ed25519-keyed ECDH (X25519 thuần → shared khác → record fail; SIG vẫn pass vì không đụng shared), (3) [`SptpsPrf`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc/Sptps/SptpsPrf.cs#L29) TLS-1.0 XOR (không TLS-1.2), (4) [`SptpsRecordLayer`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tinc/Sptps/SptpsRecordLayer.cs#L14) seqno đếm cả handshake record. **Phase b driver runtime chưa làm.**
- ⏳ **Salsa20 ở Crypto + ZeroTier V1 protocol layer (V.7.3 phase a — code + test offline; address + VL1 VALIDATE LIVE byte-exact vs zerotier-one 1.16.2)** — **Mới ở Crypto**: [`Salsa20`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Salsa20.cs) (stream cipher rounds tham số — Salsa20/20 chuẩn + Salsa20/12 ZeroTier, trên BouncyCastle `Salsa20Engine(rounds)`; **KAT ECRYPT eSTREAM byte-exact**) + **`Salsa20.CreateStream`/`Stream`** (keystream stateful, counter giữ qua nhiều `Process` — cần cho memory-hard hash CBC-like). Project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier) (PROTOCOL-layer; ref **chỉ `Crypto`**). **Identity C25519**: [`ZeroTierIdentityCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Identity/ZeroTierIdentityCodec.cs) (idtool-string + binary), [`ZeroTierAddressDerivation`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Identity/ZeroTierAddressDerivation.cs) (memory-hard hash: `SHA-512(pubkey)` → Salsa20/20 **key=digest[0:32]/iv=digest[32:40]** trên **1 stream LIÊN TỤC** → genmem 2MB **CBC-like** (block0=encrypt zeros, block i=encrypt copy block i-64) → shuffle **131072 vòng** đọc 2 uint64 **big-endian**, swap 8B digest[n1%8]↔genmem[n2%262144], **re-encrypt digest mỗi vòng** → hashcash `digest[0]<17`, addr=digest[59:64]). **VL1 transport**: [`Vl1PacketCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Vl1/Vl1PacketCodec.cs) (seal/open: **`MangleKey`** (shared key XOR header: IV+dest+src 18B, flags hops-mask `0xf8`, packet size LE 2B) → Salsa20/12 + Poly1305; **cipher 0 `C25519_POLY1305_NONE`** payload không mã hóa (HELLO) / **cipher 1 `Salsa2012Poly1305`** mã hóa; byte 18 = `FFCCCHHH`; poly key = keystream block0, tag 8B truncated), [`Vl1KeyDerivation`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Vl1/Vl1KeyDerivation.cs) (C25519 agreement → SHA-512 = `ECC::agree`, **tái dùng [`Curve25519DhGroup`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/Curve25519DhGroup.cs#L15)**), [`HelloMessageCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Vl1/HelloMessageCodec.cs) (verb HELLO, `Identity::serialize` đủ privlen + nil InetAddress physical-dest). **VL2**: [`Vl2FrameCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Vl2/Vl2FrameCodec.cs). 39 test offline (gồm **KAT address 8 identity `zerotier-idtool` thật** + **VL1 HELLO interop golden** dearmor + re-seal byte-exact). **VALIDATE LIVE 2026-06-24** (lab/zerotier, zerotier-one 1.16.2): address derivation KAT 8 identity idtool KHỚP; VL1 codec dearmor + re-seal HELLO thật (capture 2 node) BYTE-EXACT — armor/dearmor đối xứng đúng 2 chiều. **Phase b driver runtime = bullet dưới.** Crypto 118 + ZeroTier 39 không regression; build xanh ns2.0+net8.
- ✅ **ZeroTier driver runtime + VALIDATE LIVE VL1 OK peering + VL2 network join (V.7.3 phase b)** — project mới [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.ZeroTier`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.ZeroTier) (DRIVER-layer; ref `Abstractions`+`Crypto`+`Drivers.Core`+`Ethernet`+`ZeroTier`). **Codec phase b thêm vào [ZeroTier](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier)**: [`OkMessageCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Vl1/OkMessageCodec.cs) (OK common header + OK(HELLO) tail) + [`InetAddressCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Vl1/InetAddressCodec.cs) + [`ZeroTierDictionary`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Vl2/ZeroTierDictionary.cs) + [`NetworkConfigCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Vl2/NetworkConfigCodec.cs) (request + decode config dict `v4s`/`I`/`C`/`com`/`RT`/`mtu`) + [`Vl2ExtFrameCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Vl2/Vl2ExtFrameCodec.cs) (EXT_FRAME); **SỬA [`Vl2FrameCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Vl2/Vl2FrameCodec.cs)** (FRAME body bỏ flags byte) + Vl1Verb thêm ECHO/NETWORK_CONFIG_REQUEST(0x0b)/NETWORK_CONFIG(0x0c). [`ZeroTierConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.ZeroTier/ZeroTierConnection.cs#L38) kế thừa [`ReconnectingVpnConnection<ZeroTierConnectionState>`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Core/ReconnectingVpnConnection.cs#L24) (F.6): VL1 **HELLO(cipher0) ⇄ OK(HELLO)(cipher1, timestamp echo)** + trả OK(HELLO) cho HELLO của peer → **NETWORK_CONFIG_REQUEST** (retry) → controller config (assigned IP + COM) → data plane **EXT_FRAME** qua [`ZeroTierEthernetChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.ZeroTier/DataChannel/ZeroTierEthernetChannel.cs#L28) + [`ZeroTierNeighborResolver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.ZeroTier/DataChannel/ZeroTierNeighborResolver.cs#L16) (derive MAC, no ARP) + [`VirtualHost`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/VirtualHost.cs#L23); ECHO keepalive. [`ZeroTierDriver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.ZeroTier/ZeroTierDriver.cs#L18) caps **L2Ethernet**/None/Udp/**Certificate**/OutOfBand + [`UseZeroTier`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs); demo `--vpn <file>.zerotier` (ini identity ta + peer + endpoint + network + overlay → [`ConnectZeroTierAsync`](../demo/Vpn2ProxyDemo/VpnTunnel.cs)). **VALIDATE LIVE VL1 OK peering + network join 2026-06-24** (lab [`zerotier`](../lab/zerotier) [docker-compose.live146.yml](../lab/zerotier/docker-compose.live146.yml), zerotier-one **1.4.6** thật làm controller — chọn 1.4.6 vì 1.6+ negotiate **AES-GMAC-SIV (cipher 3)** mà client chưa hiện thực; 1.4.6 giữ Salsa20/12): **HELLO⇄OK timestamp echo** (`VL1 session up`) + **NETWORK_CONFIG_REQUEST → controller gán 10.144.0.2/24 + certificate of membership** → `Connected`. **3 bug interop self-pair-offline-không-bắt sửa qua live** (clean-room, KHÔNG copy BSL): (a) **Salsa20/12 payload-cipher block-alignment** — ZeroTier lấy Poly1305 key từ block0 (32B đầu) rồi mã hóa payload từ **block KẾ** (Salsa20 block-granular, bỏ 32B đuôi block0); BouncyCastle byte-granular ⇒ decrypt cipher-1 ra rác dù MAC pass (MAC chỉ auth ciphertext+poly key); fix = [`DiscardToNextBlock`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Vl1/Vl1PacketCodec.cs) advance tới ranh 64B (KAT HELLO là cipher 0 nên không bắt). (b) **handshake VL1 2 chiều** — controller gửi HELLO riêng + KHÔNG xử lý NETWORK_CONFIG_REQUEST tới khi thấy OK(HELLO) của ta; fix = trả OK(HELLO) (echo timestamp) cho HELLO inbound + retry request 2s. (c) **dict parse** — controller pre-1.6 gán IP qua key text **`v4s`** (không phải binary `I`) + value binary chứa **raw NUL** (field `v`) ⇒ deserializer KHÔNG được coi NUL là terminator cứng; OK(NETWORK_CONFIG_REQUEST) in-re header có gap 2B tùy version ⇒ scan config body theo network id. **Advertise proto v10** để 1.6+ giữ Salsa20/12. **Data-plane MAC + COM push** (bug #4 + cont): `DeriveMac` reimplement **đúng `MAC::fromAddress`** (first octet từ nwid LAA-unicast + 40-bit address + **XOR-fold các byte nwid vào MAC byte 1..5**) — **KAT byte-exact vs 2 member zerotier-one 1.4.6 thật** (`7bfd7adbee`→`fe:5c:53:94:00:94`, `e3595d21fa`→`fe:c4:f7:b3:fa:80`); trước đó derive sai (firstOctet‖address, không XOR-fold) ⇒ EXT_FRAME tới MAC node drop. Thêm [`NetworkCredentialsCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.ZeroTier/Vl2/NetworkCredentialsCodec.cs) + driver push **certificate of membership** qua NETWORK_CREDENTIALS (0x0a) sau join + khi nhận ERROR code-6. **Data-plane VL2 ICMP live = CÒN LẠI**: với MAC đúng, controller **nhận EXT_FRAME** (trả ERROR `NEED_MEMBERSHIP_CERTIFICATE` thay vì drop), nhưng COM ta push **chưa được chấp nhận** — COM trích từ dict `C` của controller 1.4.6 có serialize khác docs nhánh `dev` (qualifier alignment lệch), echo verbatim không verify. **2 member zerotier-one thật ping nhau OK** (10.144.0.3↔10.144.0.1, 0% loss) ⇒ lab + MAC fix đúng, residual thuần ở **COM exchange phía client** (cần serialize/verify COM 1.4.6 chính xác hoặc MULTICAST cho ARP-learn). ZeroTier 48 + Drivers.ZeroTier 6 + Ethernet 133 + Crypto 118 không regression; build xanh ns2.0+net8.
- ✅ **n2n v3 protocol layer (V.7.4 phase a — code + test offline + REGISTER_SUPER VALIDATE LIVE vs n2n v3.1.1 THẬT)** — project mới [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.N2n`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.N2n) (PROTOCOL-layer, ngang Nebula/Tinc/ZeroTier; ref **chỉ `Crypto`**). [`N2nPacketCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.N2n/N2nPacketCodec.cs#L19) encode/decode đối xứng mọi message type với **cleartext common header** ([`N2nCommonHeader`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.N2n/Wire/Models/N2nCommonHeader.cs#L16) 24B: `version=3 ‖ ttl ‖ flags 2B BE = pkt-type 5-bit thấp ∣ flag-bits ‖ community 20B null-pad`, **big-endian**): REGISTER_SUPER (`cookie 4 ‖ edgeMac 6 ‖ [sock nếu SOCKET] ‖ devAddr 5 ‖ devDesc 16 ‖ auth ‖ keyTime 4`), REGISTER_SUPER_ACK (`… ‖ lifetime 2 ‖ sock ‖ auth ‖ numSn 1 ‖ sock×numSn ‖ keyTime`), PEER_INFO, REGISTER/REGISTER_ACK (edge↔edge), PACKET (`src/dstMac ‖ [sock] ‖ compression 1 ‖ transform 1 ‖ payload`). **simple-id (1) + 16B challenge** mặc định), [`N2nIpSubnet`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.N2n/Wire/Models/N2nIpSubnet.cs#L13) (addr 4 BE + bitlen 1). **Transform PACKET** ([`IN2nTransform`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.N2n/Transform/Interfaces/IN2nTransform.cs#L9)): [`N2nNullTransform`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.N2n/Transform/N2nNullTransform.cs#L11) (clear) + [`N2nAesTransform`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.N2n/Transform/N2nAesTransform.cs#L18) (**AES-CBC null-IV + 16B random preamble** = IV ngầm; **tái dùng [`AesCbcCipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/AesCbcCipher.cs#L10)** — KHÔNG viết lại AES). 21 test offline (round-trip mọi pkt-type + **wire-layout invariants** version/flags-BE/community-pad + AES self-pair 2 chiều + **3 KAT golden live byte-exact**: REGISTER_SUPER edge thật 79B + REGISTER_SUPER_ACK supernode thật 58B). **VALIDATE LIVE 2026-06-24** (lab [`lab/n2n`](../lab/n2n), n2n **v3.1.1** build từ source vì apt chỉ có 1.3.1 legacy): supernode thật **CHẤP NHẬN REGISTER_SUPER** của client .NET (community `labnet`, transform NULL, **header-enc OFF** — không `-H`) → log `Rx REGISTER_SUPER` + `created edge` + `Tx REGISTER_SUPER_ACK`; client **decode REGISTER_SUPER_ACK** thật: **cookie echoed đúng**, supernode gán `dev_addr` 10.209.172.184/24, lifetime, supernode MAC, **public socket của edge** — codec byte-compatible n2n v3 first-run **0 bug** (golden REGISTER_SUPER edge thật khớp 100% layout encode). **Header encryption (`-H`, Speck + Pearson-256 key-derivation) + transform key-derivation (Pearson-256 của password) KHÔNG hiện thực** (Speck/Pearson chưa có trong Crypto, byte-exact rủi ro cao — validate chạy header-enc OFF + transform NULL). **Phase b driver runtime** = [`Drivers.N2n`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.N2n) (XONG — bullet dưới). Crypto 118 + N2n 21 không regression; build xanh ns2.0+net8.

[`N2nDriver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.N2n/N2nDriver.cs#L18) caps **L2Ethernet**/None/Udp/PreSharedKey/OutOfBand + [`UseN2n`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs); demo `--vpn <file>.n2n` (ini community/endpoint/overlay/transform → [`ConnectN2nAsync`](../demo/Vpn2ProxyDemo/VpnTunnel.cs)). **VALIDATE LIVE L2 FULL-TUNNEL ICMP 2 chiều 2026-06-24** (lab [`n2n`](../lab/n2n) [docker-compose.live.yml](../lab/n2n/docker-compose.live.yml), n2n **v3.1.1** thật: supernode + edge gateway tun `10.7.0.1/24` + client .NET `10.7.0.2/24`, community `labnet`, transform NULL): supernode `Rx REGISTER_SUPER`→`created edge`→`Tx REGISTER_SUPER_ACK` (+ keepalive ACK, **0 NAK** sau fix); demo `Gateway nội bộ 10.7.0.1 (ICMP reachable, RTT ~7ms)`; **tcpdump edge0** (tun edge thật): `10.7.0.2 > 10.7.0.1 ICMP echo request` + `10.7.0.1 > 10.7.0.2 ICMP echo reply` — ARP resolve gateway qua fabric + ICMP 2 chiều qua L2 overlay (supernode relay). **2 bug interop self-pair-offline-không-bắt sửa qua live** (đối chiếu `sn_utils.c` auth, KHÔNG copy GPL): (a) keepalive sinh **token auth random mới** mỗi lần → supernode pin token từ register đầu (`auth_edge` memcmp toàn `n2n_auth_t`) → NAK; fix = sinh token **1 lần / connection**. (b) advertise **dev_addr Unset** → supernode gán địa chỉ động + coi keepalive là edge mới → mismatch; fix = advertise **static `-a` overlay** (`BuildDevAddr`, như edge n2n thật) → ACK giữ dev_addr, keepalive là edge known. 9 test offline (register + L2 round-trip 2 chiều NULL/AES qua ARP+VirtualHost + register-timeout + channel/config). N2n 21/Ethernet 133/Crypto không regression. **Còn lại**: header encryption (`-H`, Speck/Pearson) + P2P UDP hole-punching (QUERY_PEER/PEER_INFO) + transform ChaCha20/Speck. Build xanh cả `netstandard2.0` + `net8.0`.
- ✅ **Tailscale control plane ts2021 + driver (V.7.5 — FULL-TUNNEL VALIDATE LIVE ICMP 2 chiều vs Headscale; data plane = WireGuard tái dùng + responder role)** — 2 project mới: [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tailscale`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tailscale) (PROTOCOL-layer; ref `Abstractions`+`Crypto`+`WireGuard`) = **control plane ts2021** + [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Tailscale`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Tailscale) (DRIVER-layer; ref `Abstractions`+`Drivers.Core`+`Drivers.WireGuard`+`Tailscale`) = ráp control + **tái dùng nguyên data plane WireGuard**. **Control**: kênh Noise IK [`Ts2021NoiseHandshake`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tailscale/Control/Noise/Ts2021NoiseHandshake.cs#L34) (`Noise_IK_25519_ChaChaPoly_BLAKE2s` — tái dùng [`NoiseSymmetricState`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/NoiseSymmetricState.cs#L20) **KHÔNG refactor**; pre-message `<- s` (responder static = `mkey:` từ `/key`), msg1 `e,es,s,ss`, msg2 `e,ee,se`, prologue `Tailscale Control Protocol v<N>`) + frame codec [`Ts2021FrameCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tailscale/Control/Noise/Ts2021FrameCodec.cs#L18) (initiation 5B `[ver u16][type=1][len u16]` / khác 3B, big-endian) + record cipher [`Ts2021Transport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tailscale/Control/Noise/Ts2021Transport.cs#L20) (ChaCha20-Poly1305 IETF, **nonce `0^4‖counter(BE)`** từ 0, **AAD rỗng**, max plaintext 4077B) + duplex [`Ts2021NoiseStream`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tailscale/Control/Noise/Ts2021NoiseStream.cs#L24) (record-frame + skip EarlyNoise 9B `\xff\xff\xffTS`) + [`Ts2021Connector`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tailscale/Control/Ts2021Connector.cs#L23) (`POST /ts2021` Upgrade+`X-Tailscale-Handshake` base64 → 101 → Noise IK) + [`TailscaleControlClient`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tailscale/Control/TailscaleControlClient.cs) (**net5+**: `/key` → noise → `/machine/register` preauth `Auth.AuthKey` → `/machine/map` Stream long-poll; **HTTP/2 h2c trong kênh Noise** qua `SocketsHttpHandler.ConnectCallback` + `Http2UnencryptedSupport`; đọc khung body `[len LE u32][JSON]`) + DTO tailcfg JSON **PascalCase** ([`RegisterRequest`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tailscale/Control/Messages/RegisterRequest.cs#L13)/[`MapResponse`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tailscale/Control/Messages/MapResponse.cs)/[`TailscaleNode`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tailscale/Control/Messages/TailscaleNode.cs#L21) `DERP`-rename) + key codec [`TailscaleKey`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tailscale/Keys/TailscaleKey.cs#L18) (`mkey:`/`nodekey:`/`discokey:` + lowercase hex 32B) + [`NetmapToWireGuardConfig`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Tailscale/Netmap/NetmapToWireGuardConfig.cs#L33) (self `Addresses`→tun IP, peer `Key` nodekey→WG pubkey, `AllowedIPs`→allowed-ips, `Endpoints`→endpoint). `CapabilityVersion=113` (= `ControlProtocolVersion`, = v1.80). **System.Text.Json** (in-box net8 / package ns2.0, KHÔNG Newtonsoft). **Driver**: [`TailscaleConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Tailscale/TailscaleConnection.cs#L33) kế thừa [`ReconnectingVpnConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Core/ReconnectingVpnConnection.cs#L24): `LoginAsync` → netmap → `WireGuardConfig` đa-peer → [`WireGuardConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.WireGuard/WireGuardConnection.cs#L45) con (fixed `localPort`, **`acceptInbound: true`** — mesh peer-to-peer) → `Facade.SetInner` → `MarkConnected` (WireGuard con giữ rekey/keepalive/reconnect riêng); [`TailscaleDriver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Tailscale/TailscaleDriver.cs#L20) caps L3Ip/Udp/Noise/PreSharedKey/**RoutedPrefixes**/OutOfBand + [`UseTailscale`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs); demo scheme `.tailscale` ([`ConnectTailscaleAsync`](../demo/Vpn2ProxyDemo/VpnTunnel.cs)). **VALIDATE LIVE FULL-TUNNEL ✓ 2026-06-25** (lab [`tailscale`](../lab/tailscale), Headscale **v0.29.1** thật) giữa **2 node .NET**: control `/key?v=113` 200 → `/ts2021` **101** (Noise IK) → `/machine/register` 200 **MachineAuthorized** → `/machine/map` **netmap** (cả 2 `node connected online=true`, overlay `100.64.0.1`/`.2`); **data plane qua WireGuard responder role** (tie-break theo static pubkey: 1 node initiate, node kia đáp type-2 — xem Drivers.WireGuard) — tcpdump node2 (`eth0` udp/41641): type-1 **148B** (node1) → type-2 **92B** (node2 RESPONDER) → type-4 transport data **92B 2 chiều**; **ICMP node1→`100.64.0.2` 89/89 reply RTT 0-8ms**, chiều ngược do `TcpIpStack` node2 tự đáp echo → 2 chiều qua tunnel WireGuard 2 node .NET tự dựng. **Bug/điều chỉnh qua live**: (a, control 2026-06-24) `ControlProtocolVersion` PHẢI = `CapabilityVersion` (113) — Headscale đọc version ở initiation frame header làm capver, ver=1 bị "unsupported client version" 500; (b) map đọc khung `[len LE u32][JSON]` trực tiếp trên response stream (Stream=true + `ResponseHeadersRead`), không `ReadAsByteArrayAsync`; (c) endpoint advertisement (disco stand-in): `MapRequest.Endpoints` + fixed WG `localPort`. **Vận hành (rút từ live full-tunnel)**: vì `LoginAsync` đọc netmap MỘT lần, peer kia phải đã register + advertise endpoint TRƯỚC khi node này login (lab dùng keys X25519 cố định + pre-register mỗi node 1 lần rồi chạy 2 node đồng thời). **24 test offline (Tailscale) + 5 test offline (Drivers.Tailscale, gồm `TailscaleTwoNodeTunnelTests` end-to-end 2-node) + 18 Drivers.WireGuard (gồm 3 responder-role); WireGuard 77/Crypto 122 không regression.** **Còn lại (future)**: **disco** (NAT path discovery, interop node `tailscale` THẬT bọc magicsock) + **DERP relay** + **netmap streaming động** (re-poll học peer mới, thay pre-register tĩnh). Build xanh cả `netstandard2.0` + `net8.0` (control client gated net5+).
- ✅ **vtun protocol + driver runtime + VALIDATE LIVE FULL-TUNNEL ICMP 2 chiều (V.11)** — 2 project mới: [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Vtun`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Vtun) (PROTOCOL-layer; ref `Abstractions`+`Crypto`) codec thuần clean-room vtun 3.0.4 (`auth.c`/`vtun.h`/`tcp_proto.c`, KHÔNG copy GPL): [`VtunMessageCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Vtun/Auth/VtunMessageCodec.cs) khối auth **50-byte** NUL-pad + [`VtunChallengeCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Vtun/Auth/VtunChallengeCodec.cs) challenge **a..p** (`cl2cs`/`cs2cl`) + `EncryptChallenge` = **Blowfish-ECB(MD5(password))** (`encrypt_chal`) + [`VtunHostFlagsCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Vtun/Wire/VtunHostFlagsCodec.cs) (`cf2bf`/`bf2cf`) + [`VtunFrameCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Vtun/Wire/VtunFrameCodec.cs) (word 2-byte BE flags|length); thêm [`Blowfish`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Blowfish.cs) vào Crypto (BouncyCastle `BlowfishEngine` ECB — byte-for-byte == OpenSSL). [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Vtun`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Vtun) (DRIVER-layer; ref `Abstractions`+`Drivers.Core`+`Vtun`+`Transport.Tcp`): [`VtunConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Vtun/VtunConnection.cs#L30) kế thừa [`ReconnectingVpnConnection<VtunConnectionState>`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Core/ReconnectingVpnConnection.cs#L24) (F.6): MỘT kết nối TCP qua seam [`IVtunTransportFactory`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Vtun/Transport/IVtunTransportFactory.cs#L9) (tái dùng [`TcpByteStream`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Tcp/TcpByteStream.cs#L22) F.1) → [`VtunControlChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Vtun/VtunControlChannel.cs#L19) challenge-response → kiểm cờ (tun/tcp/encrypt no/compress no) → [`VtunPacketChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Vtun/DataChannel/VtunPacketChannel.cs#L16) (`IPacketChannel` L3) frame length-prefix sau facade; receive loop (data/ECHO_REQ→ECHO_REP/CONN_CLOSE) + keepalive ECHO_REQ. [`VtunConfig`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Vtun/Config/VtunConfig.cs#L22) → `TunnelConfig` (OutOfBand). [`VtunDriver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Vtun/VtunDriver.cs#L21) caps **L3Ip**/Tcp/None/PreSharedKey/OutOfBand + [`UseVtun`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs); demo scheme `vtun://pass@host/test?addr=&peer=` ([`ConnectVtunAsync`](../demo/Vpn2ProxyDemo/VpnTunnel.cs)). **VALIDATE LIVE FULL-TUNNEL ICMP 2 chiều 2026-06-24** (lab [`vtun`](../lab/vtun), **vtund 3.0.4** apt thật: host `test`, pass, type tun, proto tcp, encrypt no, compress no, `10.11.0.1`↔`10.11.0.2`): server log `Use SSL-aware challenge/response`+`Session test[…] opened`+`test tun tun0[…]` (tun bound)+`Session test closed` (CONN_CLOSE teardown); client **4/4 ICMP echo reply** RTT~0.4ms; **reject path live** (sai password → server `Denied connection` → `VpnAuthenticationException` "got ERR"). tcpdump eth0: histogram độ dài segment = 50 (×6 khối auth NUL-pad) / 62 (frame data = 2-byte len + 60-byte ICMP/IP) / 2 (×4 control echo) — byte-for-byte spec. **0 BUG** — golden vector OpenSSL Blowfish (`MD5("pass")`→`BF-ECB(0x00..0x0f)`=`7416f64c…`) khoá offline trước nên challenge-response đúng ngay lần đầu live (chống bẫy self-pair-bỏ-sót). 32 test offline (Vtun, +9 encryptor) + 8 test offline (Drivers.Vtun, +encrypt-roundtrip+unsupported-cipher-reject+tap-bridge) + Crypto Blowfish golden không regression. **DATA-PLANE ENCRYPT (`encrypt yes` = Blowfish-128-ECB) — VALIDATE LIVE ICMP 2 chiều vs vtund 3.0.4 (2026-06-25)**: [`VtunBlowfishEcbTransform`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Vtun/Wire/VtunBlowfishEcbTransform.cs) (`BF-ECB(MD5(pwd), PKCS7-pad-to-8)` — tái dùng [`Blowfish`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Blowfish.cs)) cài qua [`VtunControlChannel.DataTransform`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Vtun/VtunControlChannel.cs); 3 golden vector OpenSSL legacy-provider byte-exact; host `enc` server log `Blowfish-128-ECB encryption initialized` + ICMP 4/4 + tcpdump ciphertext-on-wire (frame 64-byte mã hóa, 0 plaintext IP). 1 blocker môi trường: OpenSSL 3.0 ẩn Blowfish trong legacy provider (fix `OPENSSL_CONF=openssl-legacy.cnf`, không phải lỗi codec). **TAP MODE (`type ether` = L2) — VALIDATE LIVE ICMP 2 chiều vs vtund 3.0.4 (2026-06-25)**: [`VtunEthernetChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Vtun/DataChannel/VtunEthernetChannel.cs) (`IEthernetChannel`, payload = Ethernet frame trần) + `ArpResolver` + `VirtualHost` (tái dùng Ethernet fabric — nhái N2n/SoftEther) bind bridge L2↔L3; host `tapsrv` server log `tapsrv ether tap0` + ICMP 4/4 + MTU 1436 (1450−14) + tcpdump frame `length 76` (74-byte Ethernet) + 2 ARP frame. **Còn lại**: cipher khác BF128ECB (CBC/CFB/OFB + AES128/256 — cần sideband `ivec`/`seq#` framing của `lfd_encrypt`) + compression (zlib/lzo) + UDP transport (`proto udp`). Build xanh cả `netstandard2.0` + `net8.0`.
- ✅ **VPN-over-SSH protocol + driver runtime + VALIDATE LIVE FULL-TUNNEL ICMP 2 chiều (V.10)** — 2 project mới + 1 primitive Crypto. **Crypto**: thêm [`ChaCha20`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/ChaCha20.cs#L25) (stream cipher **djb gốc** — key 256-bit/nonce 8-byte/counter 64-bit/20 vòng qua BouncyCastle `ChaChaEngine`, keystream **stateful** `Stream.NextKeystream`/`Process`/`Skip` như Salsa20 — **KHÔNG** layout IETF RFC 8439; KAT TC1 vs draft-strombergson; Crypto nay 122 test). [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ssh`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ssh) (PROTOCOL-layer; ref `Abstractions`+`Crypto`) — SSH-2 transport **clean-room từ RFC 4251/4253/4252/4254 + OpenSSH PROTOCOL** (KHÔNG dùng thư viện SSH ngoài): [`SshPacketCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ssh/Wire/SshPacketCodec.cs#L21) binary packet RFC 4253 §6 (cleartext pre-NEWKEYS rồi qua seam [`ISshPacketCipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ssh/Cipher/ISshPacketCipher.cs#L12), seqno 32-bit/chiều) + 2 cipher OpenSSH [`ChaCha20Poly1305OpenSshCipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ssh/Cipher/ChaCha20Poly1305OpenSshCipher.cs#L22) (`chacha20-poly1305@openssh.com` — K_2 payload+poly / K_1 length-only, nonce seqno u64 BE, Poly1305 constant-time trước decrypt) + [`AesGcmOpenSshCipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ssh/Cipher/AesGcmOpenSshCipher.cs#L15) (`aes256/128-gcm@openssh.com` RFC 5647 — length=AAD, IV 4-fixed‖8-invocation-counter) + KEX [`Curve25519KeyExchange`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ssh/Transport/Curve25519KeyExchange.cs#L18) (X25519 RFC 8731/5656 + H=SHA256(V_C‖V_S‖I_C‖I_S‖K_S‖Q_C‖Q_S‖K) + KDF letter A..F RFC 4253 §7.2) + [`SshEd25519HostKey`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ssh/Transport/SshEd25519HostKey.cs#L14) (verify sig over H + SHA256 fingerprint TOFU) + [`SshKexInit.Negotiate`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ssh/Transport/SshKexInit.cs#L121) + [`SshUserAuth`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ssh/Auth/SshUserAuth.cs#L17) (publickey-ed25519/password RFC 4252) + [`SshTunFraming`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ssh/Channel/SshTunFraming.cs#L15) (`tun@openssh.com` L3 = `uint32 AF‖ip_packet`, **AF-only** `Overhead`=4) + [`SshClient`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ssh/SshClient.cs#L27) orchestrate; tái dùng Crypto `ChaCha20`/`AesGcmCipher`/[`Curve25519DhGroup`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/Curve25519DhGroup.cs#L15)/[`Ed25519Signer`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/Ed25519Signer.cs#L17). [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Ssh`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Ssh) (DRIVER-layer; ref `Abstractions`+`Drivers.Core`+`Ssh`+`Transport.Tcp`): [`SshConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Ssh/SshConnection.cs#L28) kế thừa [`ReconnectingVpnConnection<SshConnectionState>`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Core/ReconnectingVpnConnection.cs#L24) (F.6): MỘT kết nối TCP/22 qua seam [`ISshTransportFactory`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Ssh/Transport/ISshTransportFactory.cs#L11) (tái dùng [`TcpByteStream`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Tcp/TcpByteStream.cs#L22) F.1) → [`SshClient.ConnectAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ssh/SshClient.cs#L63) → [`SshPacketChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Ssh/DataChannel/SshPacketChannel.cs#L15) (`IPacketChannel` L3 bare IP) sau facade; `RunReceiveLoopAsync` link-loss. [`SshConfig`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Ssh/Config/SshConfig.cs#L21) → `TunnelConfig` (OutOfBand). [`SshDriver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Ssh/SshDriver.cs#L18) caps **L3Ip**/Tcp/None/Certificate\|UserPassword/OutOfBand + [`UseSsh`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L239); demo scheme `ssh://user[:pass]@host[:port]?addr=&peer=[&key=]` ([`ConnectSshAsync`](../demo/Vpn2ProxyDemo/VpnTunnel.cs#L836)). **VALIDATE LIVE FULL-TUNNEL ICMP 2 chiều 2026-06-25** (lab [`ssh`](../lab/ssh), **OpenSSH 9.6p1** trong Docker: `PermitTunnel point-to-point` + tunuser/root + ed25519 authorized_key, watcher dựng tun0 `10.10.0.1` peer `10.10.0.2`): full SSH handshake + KEX + NEWKEYS + cipher `chacha20-poly1305@openssh.com` (host key verified, cipher byte-exact vs sshd) + **publickey ed25519 ACCEPTED** (sshd "Accepted publickey … ED25519") + **`tun@openssh.com` channel open** (**phải đăng nhập root** — OpenSSH gắn tun vào uid phiên, non-root → `sys_tun_open: Operation not permitted`) + **ICMP 2 chiều** (demo "Gateway nội bộ: 10.10.0.1 ICMP reachable RTT ~3ms"; tcpdump tun0 thấy CẢ `10.10.0.1 > 10.10.0.2 echo request` LẪN `10.10.0.2 > 10.10.0.1 echo reply`). **1 BUG interop sửa qua live** (self-pair offline BỎ SÓT vì `SimulatedSshServer` cùng framing 2 đầu): tun framing `tun@openssh.com` L3 trong channel-data string = `[uint32 AF][ip_packet]` — **KHÔNG** có packet_length dẫn đầu (PROTOCOL §2.3 "uint32 packet length" chính là length-prefix của SSH `string`, đã bị `ReadString` tiêu thụ); codec cũ chèn thừa 4-byte length → sshd đọc AF = giá trị length → misframe. Hex live: client SEND `0000003c|00000002|4500…` (thừa len) vs sshd RECV `00000018(=AF_INET6 24)|6000…` (AF-only). Fix về AF-only (`Overhead`=4) ⇒ ICMP 2 chiều live. 31 test offline (Ssh) + 6 test offline (Drivers.Ssh) + ChaCha20 KAT (+4 Crypto). **Còn lại**: KEX/cipher/auth bổ sung (rsa/ecdsa hostkey, dh-group KEX, aes-ctr EtM, keyboard-interactive) + rekey mid-session (`SSH_MSG_KEXINIT`) + tap mode L2 (`SSH_TUNMODE_ETHERNET`→`IEthernetChannel`) + parse OpenSSH PEM key trong demo (hiện chỉ seed ed25519 32-byte trần). Build xanh cả `netstandard2.0` + `net8.0`.
- ✅ **PPP Restart-timer retransmit + SSTP Crypto-Binding (live-lab 2026-06-23)** — [`PppNegotiator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/PppNegotiator.cs#L20) nay có **Restart timer RFC 1661 §4.6**: retransmit Configure-Request **nguyên văn** mỗi 3s (tối đa 10) tới khi được Ack — trước chỉ gửi 1 lần nên một ConfReq lạc/bị peer loại làm **treo link** tới hết connect-timeout (LCP qua được nhờ peer chủ động gửi ConfReq riêng; IPCP/IPV6CP thì kẹt). `PppNegotiator` + [`PppEngine`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/PppEngine.cs#L14) nay `IDisposable` (dừng+giải phóng timer khi teardown); [`SstpConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Sstp/SstpConnection.cs)/[`L2tpIpsecConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.L2tpIpsec/L2tpIpsecConnection.cs)/[`PptpConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Pptp/PptpConnection.cs) gọi `PppEngine.Dispose()` khi teardown/reconnect (extra-session L2TP dispose khi bring-up lỗi). Đồng thời **SSTP CMK** ([`SstpCryptoBinding`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Sstp/SstpCryptoBinding.cs#L51)) sửa byte độ dài seed `0x01→0x20` (32 = độ dài digest SHA-256, [MS-SSTP] §3.2.5.2.2) — **validate live** với accel-ppp (hết "invalid Compound MAC"; mọi check Call-Connected pass, npmode=PASS). Test offline **+2** [`PppNegotiatorRetransmitTests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp.Tests/PppNegotiatorRetransmitTests.cs) (retransmit verbatim + dừng sau Ack). ⚠️ **Lab finding**: accel-ppp **bridged trong Docker không bao giờ mở IPCP** (mọi network-phase NCP inert + ProtoRej `<8021>` dai dẳng dù Call-Connected accept + retransmit đủ) — blocker phía **server/môi trường container** (kernel ppp npmode), KHÔNG phải driver; P1.1 live IPv6 chờ server SSTP khác (SoftEther/RRAS) hoặc accel-ppp host-net.
- ✅ **Logging/diagnostics xuyên suốt (Q.2)** — seam dùng chung ở [`Abstractions/Diagnostics`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Diagnostics): [`VpnEventIds`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Diagnostics/VpnEventIds.cs#L11) (tập `EventId` ổn định 1xx handshake/2xx steady/3xx reconnect/4xx drop), [`VpnDropReason`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Diagnostics/Enums/VpnDropReason.cs#L8) (DecryptFailed/AuthFailed/Replay/Malformed/Unexpected), [`VpnLogExtensions`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Diagnostics/Extensions/VpnLogExtensions.cs#L15) (extension `ILogger` allocation-free `LoggerMessage.Define`). Phụ thuộc mới: `Microsoft.Extensions.Logging.Abstractions` 8.0.2 (ref ở `Abstractions.csproj`, lib netstandard2.0 ⇒ cả 2 TFM). **Tất cả driver runtime** luồn `ILoggerFactory?` qua `Driver`→`Connection` (mặc định `NullLogger` ⇒ no-op), log tại state-change / handshake-step / handshake-completed/-failed / rekey / keepalive·DPD / link-lost / reconnect-attempt·success / packet-drop (auth/replay/decrypt-fail): **đợt đầu** WireGuard / OpenConnect / SoftEther; **đợt còn lại (Q.2-logger-rest)** L2TP/IPsec (Phase 1/Quick Mode/L2TP/PPP handshake + HELLO/DPD keepalive + rekey Phase 1/2) / SSTP (TLS+Call-Connect handshake + Echo keepalive) / IKEv2 (IKE_SA_INIT/IKE_AUTH PSK·EAP + DPD + rekey CHILD/IKE SA) / OpenVPN (reset/TLS/key-method-2/PUSH handshake + ping keepalive + rekey re-establish). PPTP **chưa** (chưa có driver runtime — V6.b chờ F.9). **ADDITIVE — không đổi hành vi** (toàn bộ test cũ + round-trip vẫn xanh). Test offline (**+8 test**): `WireGuardLoggingTests.cs` (handshake/state events + foreign-datagram⇒drop + wrong-key⇒handshake-failed + NullLogger no-op), `OpenConnectLoggingTests.cs` (auth+CONNECT events + wrong-password⇒handshake-failed), `SoftEtherLoggingTests.cs` (control+DHCP events), `OpenVpnLoggingTests.cs` (handshake reset/TLS/key-method-2/PUSH + HandshakeCompleted + StateChanged khi connect end-to-end) — logger giả lập [`CapturingLoggerFactory`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.WireGuard.Tests/CapturingLoggerFactory.cs) bắt `EventId` mong đợi, không đổi luồng. - ✅ **Audit cancellation/timeout & thread-safety (Q.3)** — soát toàn bộ receive-loop / channel / `CancellationToken` xuyên solution (driver `*Connection`, [`SwappablePacketChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/SwappablePacketChannel.cs#L14), transport receive-loop, IpStack loop). **1 lỗi material đã sửa**: [`UdpConnection.ReceiveAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Udp/UdpConnection.cs#L45) đăng ký callback hủy theo **field `_waiter`** thay vì **local waiter** — một datagram tới trên thread khác null-out field (và complete chính TCS đó) **trước** khi `cancellationToken.Register(...)` chạy, callback nhận `null` ⇒ NRE trên thread hủy (đồng bộ, ngay trong `ReceiveAsync` nếu token đã hủy sẵn; hoặc văng ra từ `CancellationTokenSource.Cancel()`). Sửa: capture TCS vào local rồi `Register` theo local (đúng pattern [`TcpIpStack.PingAsync` @ :107](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs#L107)) — **không đổi hành vi happy-path**. Phần còn lại (receive-loop driver honor token + route fault qua `OnLinkLost`, [`BackpressuredPacketChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/BackpressuredPacketChannel.cs#L24) single-reader + cancel sạch, [`SwappablePacketChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/SwappablePacketChannel.cs#L14) swap dưới lock + write lock-free volatile, `_random` serialise, ConfigureAwait(false) phủ khắp lib cho consumer ns2.0) **không có lỗi material** — chốt invariant bằng test concurrency. Test offline (**+4 test** IpStack.Tests): [`UdpConnectionCancellationTests.cs`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack.Tests/UdpConnectionCancellationTests.cs) (honor-cancel khi không có datagram, token-hủy-sẵn ⇒ `OperationCanceledException` không NRE, **stress 200 vòng delivery↔cancel đua nhau** không NRE/treo) + [`SwappablePacketChannelTests.Facade_ConcurrentSwapsAndWrites_*`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack.Tests/SwappablePacketChannelTests.cs) (swap+write+inbound đồng thời không vỡ + quiesce trên inner cuối ⇒ forward đúng exactly-one-subscriber).
